
[p. 1]
[śrīḥ
pampakavi viracitaṁ
vikramārjuna vijayaṁ]

[prathamāśvāsaṁ]

śrīyanarātisādhana payōnidhiyoḷ paḍeduṁ dharitriyaṁ
jīyene bēḍikoḷḷade virōdhi narēndraranottikoṇḍumā
tmīyasupuṣpavr̥ṣṭiyanoḍambaḍe tāḷdiyumintudāttanā
rāyaṇanāda dēvanemagīgarikēsari saukhya kōṭiyaṁ // ViVi.1 [utpalamālike]

muḷisu lalāṭanētraśikhi mecce vinūtarasaprasādamu
jjaḷa jasamaṅga saṅgata lasadbhasitaṁ prabhuśakti śakti ni
rmaḷamaṇibhūṣaṇaṁ phaṇivibhūṣaṇamāge negaḻteyaṁ puduṁ
goḷisidanīśvaraṁ negaḻdudāra mahēśvaranīgebhōgamaṁ // ViVi.2 [campakamāle]

caṇḍavirōdhisādhana tamastamamōḍe viśiṣṭa padmanī
ṣaṇḍamaraldu rāgadinoṟaldire yācaka bhaṅgakōṭi kai
koṇḍu nirantaraṁ taguḷdu kīrtise mikkeseva pracaṇḍamā
rtāṇḍanalarcugenna hr̥dayāmbujamaṁ nija vāṅmarīciyiṁ // ViVi.3 [utpalamālike]

sahajada celvinoḷ ratiya sōlada kēḷiyoḷ podaḻdu sa
nnahitavenippapūrva śubha lakṣaṇa dēhadoḷoḷpanāḷdu saṁ
dahikaṭaka prasādade manōjanumaṁ gelevandanāgaḷuṁ
sahajamanōjanōjanemagīge vicitra ratōtsavaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.4 [campakamāle]


[p. 2]
kṣayamaṇamillakēḷdu kaḍegaṇḍavanāvanumillenal tada
kṣayanidhi tāne tannanosedōlagipaṅgaridillenippa vā
ṅmayamanitarkamambi[ke]sarasvati manmukhapadmaraṅgadē
ḻgeyaneḍegoṇḍu koṇḍukonedīgarigaṅge viśuddhabuddhiyaṁ // ViVi.5 [campakamāle]

tisuḷadoḷuccaḷippa posa nettare kendaḷirāgekaṇgagu
rvisuvinamokku nēlva karuḷōḷiye bāḷa mr̥ṇāḷamāge mi
kkasurara meyyoḷāda virahāgniyanāṟisutintetanna kū
rasiyoḷaḍurtu kondasiyaḷi[rka]siyoḷ paḍemeccegaṇḍanā // ViVi.6 [campakamāle]

enna dānamidāgaḷuṁ madhupāśrayaṁ dharegavyava
cchinna dānamidāgaḷuṁ vibudhāśrayaṁ gelevandane
nnannijōnnatiyindamī patiyendu mecci vināyakaṁ
tānnimircuge kabbamaṁ nayadiṁ guṇārṇava bhūpanā // ViVi.7 [mallikāmāle]

bage posatappudāgi mr̥du bandhadoḷonduvudondi dēsiyoḷ
puguvudu pokka mārgadoḷe taḷvudu taḷtoḍe kāvyabandhamo
ppugumeḷamāvu kendaḷira pūvina biṇpoṟeyiṁ baḻaldu tuṁ
bigaḷine tumbi kōgileye baggise suggiyoḷoppuvantevōl // ViVi.8 [campakamāle]

ā sakaḷārtha saṁyutamaḷaṅkr̥tiyuktamudātta[vr̥tti]vi
nyāsamanēka lakṣaṇa guṇa prabhavaṁ mr̥du pādamāda vā
kśrī subhagaṁ kaḷākaḷitamemba negaḻteyanāḷda kabbamaṁ
kūsumanīvudīvudarikēsarigalladavastugīvudē // ViVi.9 [utpalamālike]

kavigaḷa nāmadhāraka narādhiparōḷiyoḷītanoḷḷidaṁ
kavi nr̥panītanoḷḷidanenal doreyaltu negaḻtevetta sa
tkavigaḷa ṣōḍaśāvaniparōḷiyoḷaṁkavitāguṇārṇavaṁ
kaviteyoḷaggaḷam guṇadoḷaggaḷamelliyumā guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.10 [campakamāle]

kate piridādoḍaṁ kateyameygiḍalīyade muṁ samasta bhā
ratamanapūrvamāge sale pēḻda[kavīśvarari]lla varṇakaṁ

[p. 3]
kateyoḷoḍambaḍaṁ paḍeye pēḻvoḍe pampane pēḻgumendu paṁ
ḍitare taguḷdu biccaḻise pēḻaloḍarcidenī prabandhamaṁ // ViVi.11 [campakamāle]

lalitapadaṁ prasanna kavitāguṇamillade pūṇdu pēḻda be
ḷgaḷa kr̥tibandhamuṁ barepakāṟara kaigaḷa kēḍu nuṇṇana
ppaḷakada kēḍu pēḻisidoḍarthadakēḍene pēḻdu bīgi po
ṭṭaḷisi negaḻtegāṭisuva duṣkaviyuṁ kaviyemba lekkamē // ViVi.12 [campakamāle]

vyāsamunīndra rundra vacanāmr̥tavārdhiyanīsuveṁ kavi
vyāsanenemba garvamenagilla guṇārṇavanoḷpu manmanō
vāsamaneydepēḻdapenadalladegarvamedōṣamaḻtigaṁ
dōṣame kāṇenennaṟiva māḻkeye pēḻvenidāva dōṣamō // ViVi.13 [utpalamālike]

vipuḷa yaśō vitāna guṇamilladanaṁ prabhu māḍi pūrva bhū
mipara padaṅgaḷaṁ pugisipōlipoḍītanudātta pūrva bhū
miparumanoḷpinoḷ taguḷevandoḍeyī katheyoḷ taguḷci pō
lipoḍenagaḻtiyādudu guṇārṇava bhūbhujanaṁ kirīṭiyoḷ // ViVi.14 [campakamāle]

śrīmaccaḷukya vaṁśa
vyōmāmr̥takiraṇanenipa kāntiyanoḷakoṁ
ḍī mahiyoḷātmavaṁśa śi
khāmaṇi jasameseyeyuddhamallaṁnegaḻdaṁ // ViVi.15 [kandaṁ]

ātaṁ nija bhujavijaya
khyātiyanāḷdāḷdanadhikabalanavanipati
vrāta maṇimakuṭa kiraṇa
dyōtitapādaṁ sapādalakṣa kṣitiyaṁ // ViVi.16 [kandaṁ]


[p. 4]
ēnaṁ pēḻvudo siriyu
ddāniyaneṇṇeyoḷe tīvi dīrghikegaḷanaṁ
tā nr̥pati niccalaynū
ṟāneyanavagāhamirisuvambōdanadoḷ // ViVi.17 [kandaṁ]

śrīpatigeyuddhamallama
hīpatige negaḻte puṭṭe puṭṭidanakhiḷa
kṣmāpāla mauḷi maṇi kira
ṇāpāḷitanakhamayūkharañjita caraṇaṁ // ViVi.18 [kandaṁ]

arikēsariyembaṁ suṁ
darāṅganatyanta vastuvaṁ madakariyaṁ
hariyaṁpaḍivaḍegurcida
karavāḷane tōṟi nr̥pati gellaṅgoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.19 [kandaṁ]

nirupama dēvana rājyado
ḷarikēsariveṅgiviṣayamaṁ tri[kaḷiṅgaṁ]
berasottikoṇḍu garvade
bareyisidaṁ pesaranakhiḷa digbhattigaḷoḷ // ViVi.20 [kandaṁ]

kṣatraṁ tējōguṇamā
kṣatriyaroḷ nelasi nindudā negaḻdādi
kṣatriyaroḷamillenisidu
dī trijagadoḷesagidesakamarikēsariyā // ViVi.21 [kandaṁ]

arikēsarigātmajarari
narapa śirōdaḷana pariṇatōgrāsi bhayaṁ
karakararāyirvaroḷār
doreyene narasiṁha bhadradēvar negaḻdar // ViVi.22 [kandaṁ]


[p. 5]
avaroḷ narasiṅgaṅgati
dhavaḷayaśaṁyuddhamallanagrasutaṁ ta
dbhuvanapradīpanāgi
rdavārya vīryaṅgebaddegaṁ piriya magaṁ // ViVi.23 [kandaṁ]

puṭṭidoḍātanoḷaṟivoḍa
vuṭṭidudaṟiviṅge pempu pempinoḷāyaṁ
kaṭṭāyadoḷaḷavaḷavino
ḷoṭṭaje puṭṭidudu pōlvarār baddeganaṁ // ViVi.24 [kandaṁ]

balvarikeyoḷari nr̥para pa
ḍalvaḍe taḷtiṟidu raṇadoḷā vikramamaṁ
solvinamāvarjisidaṁ
nālvatteraḍaṟikegāḷegaṅgaḷoḷītaṁ // ViVi.25 [kandaṁ]

vanadhi parīta bhūtaḷadoḷītane sōlada gaṇḍanemba peṁ
pinapesaraṁnimircidudumallade vikramadinde nindagu
rvenaliṟidāntaraṁmosaḷeyaṁ piḍivantire nīroḷotti bhī
mananatigarvadiṁ piḍiyemeygali baddeganannanāvanō // ViVi.26 [campakamāle]

mugilaṁ muṭṭida pempu pempanoḷakoṇḍudyōgamudyōgadoḷ
negaḻdājñāphalamājñeyoḷ toḍardagurvondondagurvindagu
rvugoḷuttirparimaṇḍaḷaṁ jasakaḍarpappannegaṁ sandanī
jagadoḷ baddeganannanāvaniḻikuṁbhrūkōṭiyiṁkōṭiyaṁ // ViVi.27 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

mēruvapon kalpāṅghripa
dārave rasadoṟavuparusavēdiyakaṇi bhaṁ
ḍāradoḷuṇṭene kuḍuvani
vārita dānakke pōlvarār baddeganaṁ // ViVi.28 [kandaṁ]


[p. 6]
surabhi dēvateyembakāpinemāṇdudēṟuvudondadeṁ
dirade māṇdududēva vāraṇavēḻeuṇṭavu pōdoḍā
kharakaraṅgaridendemāṇdi[re]māṇduvā hari nīne pē
ḻariyavendivu bhadradēvara cāgadoḷpoṟagāduvē // ViVi.29 [taraḷaṁ]

ā baddegaṅge vairi ta
mōbaḷa daśaśatakaraṁ virājita vijaya
śrī bāhuyuddhamallani
ḷābahuvidharakṣaṇa pravīṇakr̥pāṇaṁ // ViVi.30 [kandaṁ]

ātmabhavanā narādhipa
nātmajanānahuṣa pr̥thu bhagīratha naḷa mā
hātmaraniḻisi negaḻda ma
hātmaṁ narasiṁhanaṟivinoḷ paramātmaṁ> // ViVi.31 [kandaṁ]

māṅkarisadaṟivu guru vaca
nāṅkuśamaṁ pāḻiyeḍege poṇardaribalamaṁ
kiṅkoḷemāḻpeḍegaṇameni
raṅkuśamenisidudu munisu bhadrāṅkuśanā // ViVi.32 [kandaṁ]


[p. 7]
taṟisandu lāḻaroḷta
[ḷti]ṟidēṟaṁ pēḻe kēḷdumaṇḍalaminnuṁ
tiṟunīrikkuvudenisida
taṟisalavina calada balada kali narasiṁhaṁ // ViVi.33 [kandaṁ]

siṅgaṁ masagidavōl nara
siṅgaṁ taḷtiṟiyenegaḻdanettar nabhadoḷ
keṅguḍi kavidantādudi
dēṁ garvada pemposakalalōkāśrayanā // ViVi.34 [kandaṁ]

ēḻuṁ māḷamumaṁ pā
ṟēḻetaguḷdiṟidu naraganuripidoḍe kariṁ
kēḻisidātana tējada
bīḻalananukaripuvāduvogedurivurigaḷ // ViVi.35 [kandaṁ]

vijayārambha purassara
vijaya gajaṅgaḷane piḍidu ghūrjara rāja
dhvajiniyaniṟidōḍisi bhuja
vijayade vijayanumaniḻisidaṁ narasiṁhaṁ // ViVi.36 [kandaṁ]

siḍilavoleṟaguva naragana
paḍegagidummaḷadinuṇḍeḍeyoḷuṇṇadeyuṁ
keḍedeḍeyoḷkeḍeyade niṁ
deḍeyoḷ nilladeyumōḍidaṁ mahipālaṁ // ViVi.37 [kandaṁ]

gaṅgāvārdhiyoḷātma tu
raṅgamumaṁ misisi negaḻdakāḷapriyanoḷ
saṅgata guṇanasilateyana
suṅgoḷe bhujavijaya garvadiṁ sthāpisidaṁ // ViVi.38 [kandaṁ]


[p. 8]
ā narasiṁha mahīśa ma
nōnayana priye viḷōḷa nīḷāḷake caṁ
drānane jākavve dalā
jānakigaggaḷamekuladoḷaṁ śīladoḷaṁ // ViVi.39 [kandaṁ]

posatalarda biḷiya tāvare
yesaḻgaḷa naḍuvirpa siriyumākeya keladoḷ
nasu masuḷdutōrpaḷenepō
lisuvoḍejākavveguḻida peṇḍir doreyē // ViVi.40 [kandaṁ]

ā jākavvegamā vasu
dhājaya sadvallabhaṅgamati viśada yaśō
rājitaneniparikēsari
rājaṁ tējōgnimagnaripu nr̥paśalabhaṁ // ViVi.41 [kandaṁ]

maganādanāgi cāgada
negaḻteyoḷ bīradēḻgeyoḷ negaḻe magaṁ
maganene puṭṭaloḍaṁkō
ḻmogagoṇḍudu bhuvana bhavanamarikēsariyoḷ // ViVi.42 [kandaṁ]

madada nīroḷe lōkavārtege beccunīrdaḷidāgaḷā
madagajāṅkuśadinde percisi nābhiyaṁ madadanti daṁ
tadoḷe kaṭṭida toṭṭilaṁ nayadindamēṟisebāḷakā
ladoḷe toṭṭiligaṁ gajapriyanappudaṁ sale tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.43 [taraḷaṁ]

rundrāmbhōdhi parīta ma
hīndraradārinnarī narēndraṁ sākṣā
dindraṁ tānene sale nega
ḻdindrēndrana tōḷe toṭṭilāgire baḷedaṁ // ViVi.44 [kandaṁ]


[p. 9]
amita matiguṇadinati vi
krama guṇadiṁśāstrapāramuṁ ripubaḷapā
ramumoḍane sanduvenisida
namēya balaśālimanujamārtāṇḍa nr̥paṁ // ViVi.45 [kandaṁ]

uḍevaṇipaṟiyada munname
toḍagi calaṁ negaḻe ripu balaṅgaḷane paḍa
lvaḍisi parabalada nettara
kaḍaloḷagaṇa jiguḷe baḷeva teṟadoḷe baḷedaṁ // ViVi.46 [kandaṁ]

mēleḻdabalaṁkōṭige
mēlappoḍamanya vanite negaḻdūrvaśigaṁ
mēlappoḍamakkenduṁ
sōlavu kaṇ para balābdhigaṁ para vadhugaṁ // ViVi.47 [kandaṁ]

dhuradoḷ mūṟuṁ lōkaṁ
neredireyuṁ kuḍuvapo[ḻta]ṟoḷmēruve muṁ
direyuṁ bīrada biyadaṁ
tarakke kiṟidendu cintipaṁ priyagaḷḷaṁ // ViVi.48 [kandaṁ]

samanenisuva[r]praśasti
kramadoḷ svasti samadhigata pañcamahāśa
bdamahāsāmantarenal
samanenipare guṇadoḷariganoḷ sāmantar // ViVi.49 [kandaṁ]

cāgada kambamaṁ niṟisi bīrada śāsanamaṁ negaḻci kō
ḷpōgada maṇḍalaṅgaḷane koṇḍu jagattritayaṅgaḷoḷ jasa
kkāgaramāda baddeganinā narasiṁhaninatta nālveral
mēgupodaḻda cāgadoḷamondida bīradoḷaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.50 [utpalamālike]


[p. 10]
ene sanduṁ vīra vairi kṣitipa gaja ghaṭāṭōpa kumbhasthaḷī bhē
dananugrō[dghā]si bhāsvadbhujaparighananārūḍhasarvajñanaṁ vai
rinarēndrōddāmadarpōddaḷanananekathānāyakaṁ māḍi sanda
rjunanoḷ pōlvī kathā bhittiyananunayadiṁ pēḻalendettikoṇḍeṁ // ViVi.51 [mahāsragdhare]

andentene – samunmiṣadvividharatnamālā prabhābhīlāruṇa jalaplavāviḷa viḷōḷavīcīrayapradārita kuḷācalōdadhi parītamāgirda jambūdvīpadoḷaguṇṭu nāḍu kurujāṅgaṇa nāmadiṁ antā kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayadoḷ—

jala jalanoḻkutirpa parikāl parikāloḷaḷurkegoṇḍa nai
dila posavū podaḻda posa naidila kampane bīṟe kāyta keṁ
goleyoḷe jōlva śāḷinavaśāḷige pāyva śukāḷi tōṟe ke
yvolagaḷinoppitōṟisiri nōḍugumā viṣayāntarāḷadoḷ // ViVi.52 [campakamāle]

beḷedeṟagirda keyvolane keyvolanaṁ baḷasirda pūta pū
goḷagaḷe pūtapūgoḷagaḷaṁ baḷasirda vicitra nandanā
vaḷigaḷe nandanāvaḷigaḷaṁ baḷasirda madāḷisaṅkulaṁ
gaḷe viṣayāṅganā luḷita kuntaḷadantevoloppi tōṟuguṁ // ViVi.53 [campakamāle]


[p. 11]
laḷita vicitra patra phala puṣpayutāṭavi sorkidāneyaṁ
beḷevududēvamātr̥kamenippa polaṁ nava gandha śāḷiyaṁ
beḷevudu ramya nandanavanāḷi viyōgi janakke bēṭamaṁ
baḷevudu nāḍa kāḍa beḷasimbeḷasā viṣayāntarāḷadoḷ // ViVi.54 [campakamāle]

āvalaruṁ paṇṇuṁ bī
tōvavu gaḍa bīyavalli malligegaḷumi
mmāvugaḷumendoḍiṁpeṟa
tāvudu saṁsāra sāra sarvasva phalaṁ // ViVi.55 [kandaṁ]

miḍidoḍe tanigarvurasaṁ
biḍuvuvu biridondu muguḷa kampinoḷe mogaṁ
giḍuvuvu tumbigaḷaḻkame
vaḍuvuvu kuḍidondu paṇṇa rasadoḷe giḷigaḷ // ViVi.56 [kandaṁ]

suttiṟida rasada toṟegaḷe
muttina māṇikada palavumāgarame madō
nmatta madakari vanaṅgaḷe
suttalumā nelada siriyanēnaṁ pogaḻveṁ // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

antu sogayisuva kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayakke rājadrājadhāniyāgirdu
hara jaṭājūṭakke candralēkheyirpantedikkarikaṭa taṭakkemadalēkheyirpante
kaiṭabhārātiya viśālōrasthaḷakke kaustubhamirpante sogayisutirdudu hastinapura
vembudu poḻalalli—

adaṟa poṟavoḻala viśāḷa kanaka kr̥taka girigaḷiṁ phaḷaprakīrṇatarugaḷiṁ
naneya koneya taḷira muguḷa vanalatānikuñjadiṁprasūna rajada puñjadiṁ
gaganataḷame paṟidu biḻdudenipa bahu taṭākadiṁ kukilva naliva kōkadiṁ

[p. 12]
suriva surayiyarala muguḷge mogasidaḷikuḷaṅgaḷiṁtoda[lva]śiśu śukaṅgaḷiṁ
tegeye bīra ravadamēlepariva madagajagaḷiṁ caḷatturaṅga maṅgaḷiṁ
lavaṇa jaḷadhi baḷasidante baḷasidagaḻa nīḷadindudagrakanaka śāḷadiṁ
doḷage kula nagaṅgaḷenipa dēvakulada bhōgadiṁ sarāgamāda rāgadiṁ
divamanēḷipantu miḷirva vividha kētanaṅgaḷiṁ sadānikētanaṅgaḷiṁ
dhanada bhavanamenipa siriya baccarāpaṇaṅgaḷiṁpodaḻda[kāva]ṇaṅgaḷiṁ
viṭajanakke toḍarva cāriyenipa sūḷegēriyiṁ vidagdha hr̥daya hāriyiṁ
kanaka gōpuraṅgaḷoḷagaṇeraḍu deseyaguṇaṇeyiṁ viḷāsiniyara gaḍaṇeyiṁ
suratasukhada baḷḷavaḷḷiyenipa baḷḷimāḍadiṁ mahāvinōda nīḍadiṁ
kanakaśailamenisi negaḻda bhūmipāla bhavanadiṁ samasta vastu bhuvanadiṁ // ViVi.58 [ragaḷe]

antu mūṟu lōkada celvellamaṁ vidhātranondeḍege teraḷcidante samasta
vastu vistāra hāramāgirda hastinapurave nijavaṁśāvaḷambamāge negaḻda
bharatakulatilakara vaṁśāvatāramentādudendoḍe—

jaḷaruhanābhana nābhiya
jaḷa budbudadoḷage surabhi parimaḷa miḷitō
lluḷitāḷijala[ja]māytā
jaḷa[ja]doḷogedaṁhiraṇyagarbha brahmaṁ // ViVi.59 [kandaṁ]

kamalōdbhavanamaḷina hr̥
tkamaladoḷogedar‌ surēndradhārakarāvā
gamaḷarnegaḻdirdarpula
hamarīcyatryaṅgiraḥ puḷastya kratugaḷ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]


[p. 13]
antu hiraṇyagarbha brahma manassambhavadoḷ puṭṭidaṟuvarmakkaḷoḷage
marīciya magaṁ kaśyapananēka bhuvanōtpatti nāṭakakke sūtradhāranādanātana
maganavāryavīryaṁ sūryanātanindavyavacchinnamāgi banda vaṁśaṁ
sūryavaṁśamembudāytu—

atriya piriya magaṁ bhava
natraya saṅgītakīrti sōmaṁ sakala
kṣatrakulapūjyanamaḷa ca
ritraṁ prōddāma sōmavaṁśalalāmaṁ // ViVi.61 [kandaṁ]

ā sōmavaṁśajar pala
rāsukaraṁ berasu negaḻda jasadiṁ jagamaṁ
bāsaṇisi pōdoḍadhika vi
ḷāsaṁ dauṣyanti bharatanembaṁ negaḻdaṁ // ViVi.62 [kandaṁ]

cāru caritraṁ bharatana
pāraguṇaṁ tanna pesaroḷamardeseye yaśō
bhāraṁ kulamuṁ katheyuṁ
bhāratamene negaḻdanantu negaḻvudubhūpar // ViVi.63 [kandaṁ]

bharatananēkādhvara bhara
nirataṁ jasamuḻiye kaḻiye bhūpar palarā
darisida dharaṇī bharamaṁ
dhariyisidaṁ pratimanembanapratima balaṁ // ViVi.64 [kandaṁ]

antā pratimaṅge sutar
śantanu bāhlika vinūta dēvāpigaḷō
rantedhare pogaḻe negaḻdara
nanta baḷa‌r parabaḷa prabhēdana śaurya‌r // ViVi.65 [kandaṁ]


[p. 14]
avaroḷage dēvāpi nava yauvana prārambhadoḷe tapaścaraṇa parāyaṇanādaṁ
pratimanuṁpratāpa prasara prakaṭapaṭuvāgi palavu kālamarasugeydu saṁsārāsāratege
pēsi tapōvanakkabhimukhanāgalbagedu—

kantuśara bhava[na]nāpriya
kāntā bhrūvibhrama grahāgrahavaśadiṁ
bhrāntisadupaśānta manaṁ
śantanugittaṁ samasta rājyaśrīyaṁ // ViVi.66 [kandaṁ]

śantanugamamaḷa gaṅgā
kāntegameṇṭaneya vasu vasiṣṭhana śāpa
bhrāntiyoḷe bandu nirjita
kantuvenalkantu puṭṭidaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ // ViVi.67 [kandaṁ]

antu bhuvanakkellamāyamumaḷavumaṟimaṇmuṁ puṭṭuvante puṭṭi
navayauvanaṁ neṟeya neṟeye—

sālaprāṁśu viśālalōlanayanaṁ prōdyadvr̥ṣaskandhanu
nmīlatpaṅkajavaktranāyata samagrōrasthaḷaṁ dīrgha bā
hālambaṁ bhujavīrya vikramayutaṁgaṅgātmajanmaṁ jaya
śrīlōlaṁjamadagnirāmamuniyoḷ kaltaṁ dhanurvidyeyaṁ // ViVi.68 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu kaltu munname cāpavidyeyoḷārindamītanebhārgavanenisida
bhārgavaṅge tāne bhārgavanāgi yuvarājakaṇṭhikā parikalita kaṇṭhaluṇṭhanumāgi
pramāṇa nija bhuja daṇḍadaṇḍitārāti maṇḍalanumāgi gāṅgēyaṁ
sukhadoḷarasugeyyuttirpannegamitta gaṅgādēśadoḷuparicaravasuvembarasaṁ puṭṭida
girijeyemba kanneyanātaṁ kaṇḍu kaṇbēṭaṅgoṇḍu maduveyaṁ nindondu divasa
mindranōlagakke pōgi r̥tukālaprāpteyāgirda nallaḷallige baral paḍeya
dākeyaṁ nenedindriya kṣaraṇeyādoḍadanondu kadaḷīpatradoḷ pudidu tanna
naḍapida giḷiya kaiyoḷōpaḷalligaṭṭidoḍadaṁ tarparagiḷiya nondu
[p. 15]
giḍuganeḍegoṇḍu jaguneyaṁ pāyvāgaḷugibagi māḍidāgaḷadaṟa kaiyiṁ barduṅki
toṟeyoḷage biḻdoḍadanondu bāḷemīnnuṅgi garbhamaṁ tāḷdidoḍondu
divasamā mīnanorva jālagāṟaṁ jāladoḷ piḍidalligarasappa dāśanalliguydu
tōṟidoḍadaṁ vidārisi nōḻpannegaṁ bāḷeya garbhadoḷirda bāḷeyaṁ bāḷanumaṁ
kaṇḍettikoṇḍu matsyagandhiyuṁ matsyagandhanumendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍapi
yamunānadītīradoḷirpannegamalligorme brahmara mommanappa vr̥dda
parāśara munīndranuttarāpathakke pōguttuṁ bandu toṟeya taḍiyoḷōḍamaṁ
naḍeyisuva matsyagandhiyaṁ kaṇḍemmanī toṟeyaṁ pāyisembuduṁ sāsirvarēṟi
doḍalladīyōḍaṁ naḍeyadembudamāmanibara biṇpumappemēṟisendoḍante
geyvenendōḍamēṟisi naḍeyisuvalli divya kanneyanaḻkartu nōḍi—

manadoḷ sōltu munīndranākeyoḍalī durgandhavōpanteyō
janagandhitvamanittu kāṇḍa paṭadantirpannegaṁ māḍi maṁ
janalampaḻkaṟanīye kūḍuveḍeyoḷ jñānasvarūpaṁ mahā
munipaṁ puṭṭidanantu divya munigaḷgēgeydoḍaṁ tīradē // ViVi.69 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu nīlāmbuda śyāmanuṁ kanakapiṅgaḷa jaṭābandhakaḷāpanuṁ daṇḍa
kapāḷahastanuṁ kr̥ṣṇa mr̥gatyakparidhānanumāgi vyāsabhaṭṭārakaṁ puṭṭuvudu
mātananoḍagoṇḍu satyavatige punaḥ kanyābhāvamaṁ dayegeydu parāśaraṁ
pōdanittal—

mr̥gayā vyājadinorme śantanu toḻaltarpaṁ paḷañcalke ta
nmr̥gaśābākṣiya kampu taṭṭi madhupambōlsōltu kaṇḍoldu na
lmege dibyambiḍivantevōl piḍidu nīn bā pōpamendaṅge me
llage tatkanyake nāṇci bēḍuvoḍe nīvemmayyanaṁ bēḍirē // ViVi.70 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 16]
embuduṁ śantanu poḻalge maguḻdu vandavarayyanappa dāśarājanallige
kūsaṁ bēḍa pergaḍegaḷanaṭṭidoḍe gāṅgēyaṁ doreya piriya maganuṁ
kramakramārhanumirdantenna magaḷaṁkuḍevemmamagaḷge puṭṭidātaṁ rājya
kkoḍeyanuṁ piriya maganuṁ kramakkarhanumappoḍe kuḍuvemene tadvr̥ttāntamaṁ
mantrigaḷiṁ śantanu kēḷdu—

kramamaṁ vikramadinde tāḷduva magaṁ gāṅgēyanirdante nō
ḍa maruḷ śantanu tannadondu savigaṁ sōlakkamittaṁ nija
kramamaṁ tannaya bēṭadākeya magaṅgembondapakhyāti lō
kamanāvartise biḻdoḍenna kulamuṁ takkūrmeyuṁ māsadē // ViVi.71 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu tanna nāṇgāpane bagedatanu paritāpitaśarīranumāgi śantanu
karaṅgerdegiḍe tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ gāṅgēyanaṟidu—

ennaya dūsaṟiṁ nr̥pati bēḍidudaṁ kuḍalolladaṅgajō
tpanna vimōhadindaḻidapaṁ pati sattoḍe satta pāpame
nnannarakaṅgaḷoḷ taḍeyadaḻdugumēvudu rājyalakṣmi pō
tannaya tandeyendudane koṭṭu vivāhamaninde māḍuveṁ // ViVi.72 [utpalamālike]

endu niścayisi gāṅgēyaṁ dāśarājanallige vandātana manada toḍarpaṁ
piṅge nuḍidu—

nīḍiradīvudī nija tanūjeyanī vadhugāda putraroḷ
kūḍuge rājyalakṣmi moṟeyaltenagantadu peṇḍirembaroḷ
kūḍuvanallenindu modalāgire nikkuvamendu rāgadiṁ
kūḍidanuydu satyavatiyaṁsatiyaṁ patiyoḷnadīsutaṁ // ViVi.73 [utpalamālike]

antu śantanuvuṁ satyavatiyumanyonyāsaktacittarāgikelavu kālamirpanne
gamavara bēṭadakandalgaḷante citrāṅgada vicitravīryaremba makkaḷ puṭṭi mahā
pracaṇḍaruṁ pratāpigaḷumāgi baḷeyuttirpannegaṁ śantanu paralōka prāptanādoḍe
gāṅgēyaṁ taducita paralōka kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi munne tanna nuḍida nuḍivaḷiyemba
[p. 17]
prāsādakkadhiṣṭhānaṅgaṭṭuvante citrāṅgadaṅge paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi rājyaṁgeyisuttu
mirpannegamorva gandharvanoḷe citrāṅgadaṁ dvandvayuddhamaṁ poṇarci
kurukṣētramaṁ kaḷambēḻdu kādi sattoḍe vicitravīryanaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ
dharābhāradhurandharanaṁ māḍi—

sakaḷa kṣatriya mōhadiṁ nijabhuja prārambhadiṁ pōgi tā
gikelar‌ nondoḍekādi rājasutaroḷtannaṅkadondugrasā
yakadiṁ nāyakaraṁ paḍalvaḍisutuṁ tāṁ tandanandambeyaṁ
bikeyambāleyaremba bāleyaranēṁbhīṣmaṁ yaśō bhāgiyō // ViVi.74 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu tandu tanna tammaṁ vicitravīryaṅgā mūvarkanneyaraṁ
pāṇigrahaṇaṅge yvāgaḷellariṁ piriyāke ninnanallade peṟaranollenendirdoḍe
mattinirvarumaṁ maduveyaṁ māḍi gāṅgēyanambeyanintendaṁ—

atra surēśvarāvasathamitta mahītaḷamutta pannagō
dātta samasta lōkamaṟidantire pūṇdenagāgadaṅgajō
tpatti sukhakkesōlalaḻiguṁ puruṣavratamīgaḷabbeyeṁ
dattigeyemba mātanenagēnenalakkumo paṅkajānanē // ViVi.75 [utpalamālike]

endu nuḍida gāṅgēyana nuḍiyoḷavasaramaṁ pasaramaṁ paḍeyade tanage
kiṟiyanduṅguraviṭṭasālvalanembarasanallige pōgi nīnennaṁ kaikoḷa
vēḻkumendoḍātanintendaṁ—

baṇḍaṇadoḷennanōḍisi
koṇḍuydaṁ ninnanā saritsutanānuṁ
peṇḍatiyenādenadaṟiṁ
peṇḍir peṇḍiroḷadentu berasuvarabalē // ViVi.76 [kandaṁ]

endu sālvalaṁ tanna paribhavadoḷāda siggaṁ sālvinamuṇṭu
māḍidoḍātana manamanoḍambaḍisalāṟade paraśurāmanallige pōgi bhīṣmanenna
[p. 18]
svayaṁvaradoḷ neredarasumakkaḷellarumanōḍisikoṇḍu bandenna[ṁ]maduveyaṁ
nilalolladaṭṭi kaḷedoḍenna devasamuṁ javvanamumaḍaviyoḷage pūta pūvinante
kiḍalīyadātananennaṁ pāṇigrahaṇaṁ geyvantu māḍu māḍalāṟadoḍe kiccaṁ
dayegeyvudendambe kaṇṇanīraṁ tumbe—

nayamaṁnambuvoḍenna pēḻva satiyaṁ kaikoṇḍanaṁtalladu
rṇayamaṁ naccuvoḍennanugra raṇadoḷ mēṇ mīṟi mārkoṇḍanā
raye kajjaṁ peṟatilla śantanu sutaṅgennaṁ karaṁ nambidaṁ
beyoḷennabevalaṁ vivāhavidhiyaṁ māḻpeṁ peṟar māḻparē // ViVi.77 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu nāgapurakke varpa paraśurāmana baravaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ kēḷdirvandu
kanaka rajata pātraṅgaḷoḷarghyamaṁ koṭṭu poḍamaṭṭu—

besanēnendoḍe pēḻvenenna besanaṁ kaikoḷvudī kanneyaṁ
pasurvandar paseyembivaṁ samedu nīṁ kaikoḷ koḷalkāgadeṁ
besakaṁ cittadoḷuḷḷoḍīgaḷivaremmācāryareṁdōvadē
rvesanaṁ māṇade kaidugoḷḷeraḍaṟoḷ meccittenēnendapay // ViVi.78 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu nuḍida paraśurāmana nuḍiyaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ kēḷdenage vīraśrīyuṁ
kīrtiśrīyumalladuḻida peṇḍir moṟeyalli nīvidanēkāgrahaṁ geyvireṁ
doḍentumemmoḷ kādalvēḻvudendu—

keḷardandugra raṇāgrahapraṇayadindāgaḷ kurukṣētamaṁ
kaḷavēḻdirvarumaindra vāruṇade vāyavyādi divyāstra saṁ
kuḷadindorvaranorvareccu nija pīṭhāmbhōjadiṁ brahmanu
ccaḷipannaṁ piridondu saṅkaṭamanī trailōkyadoḷ māḍidar // ViVi.79 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 19]
atarkyaṁ vikrāntaṁ bhujabalamasāmānyamadhikaṁ
pratāpaṁ pōgītaṅgeṇeye divijarvāyupathadoḷ
śitāstraṅgaḷpoṁ[ka]ṅgiḍisesugidaṁ bhārgavanidēṁ
pratijñāgāṅgēyaṅgadiradidirnilvannaroḷarē // ViVi.80 [śikhariṇi]

antu gāṅgēyanoḷ paraśurāmaṁ kādi basavaḻidusiralappoḍamāṟade
mūrchevōgirdanaṁ kaṇḍambeyembadaṇḍurumbe ninage vadhārthamāgipuṭṭuve
nakkendukōpāgniyindamagniśarīreyāgi drupadana mahādēvige maganāgi puṭṭi
kāraṇāntaradoḷ śikhaṇḍiyāgirdaḷitta bhīṣmara bembaladoḷ vicitravīryanu
mavāryavīryanumāgi kelavu kālaṁ rājyalakṣiyaṁ tāḷdi rājayakṣmataptaśarīranātmaja vigatajīviyāgi paralōka prāptanādoḍe gāṅgēyanuṁ
satyavatiyumatyanta śōkānala dahyamāna mānasarkaḷāgi ātaṅge paralōkakriyegaḷaṁ
māḍi rājyaṁ naṣṭarājamādudarkemammalamaṟugi yōjanagandhi
sindhuputrananintendaḷ—

maganembantu dharitri ninnanujaraṁ kaikoṇḍu muṁ pūṇda na
nnige bannaṁ baralīyadārtesagidī vikhyātiyuṁ kīrtiyuṁ
mugilaṁ muṭṭidudalte namma kuladoḷ makkaḷpeṟar nīnē ja
ṭṭiganai munninoraṇṭuvēḍa maganēkaikoḷ dharābhāramaṁ // ViVi.81 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu ninnanāninitaṁ kaiyoḍḍi bēḍidenenda satyavatigamarāpagā
nandananintendaṁ—

kiḍugume rājyaṁ rājyada
toḍarpadēvāḻte nanniyanuḍiyaṁ
kiḍe negaḻe nānumeraḍaṁ
nuḍidoḍe hari hara hiraṇyagarbhar nagarē // ViVi.82 [kandaṁ]


[p. 20]
himakaranātma śītaruciyaṁ dinanāyakanuṣṇa dīdhiti
kramamanagādhavāridhiyeguṇpaniḷāvadhu tanna tiṇpanu
ttamakulaśailamunnatiyanēḷidavāge bisuḻpoḍaṁ bisu
[ḻkema]bisuḍeṁmadīya puruṣavratamondumanīgaḷambikē // ViVi.83 [campakamāle]

endu tanna nuḍida pratijñeyanēgeyduṁ tappidanilla—

raṅgattaraṅga vārdhica
yaṅgaḷ tantammamēreyaṁ dāṇṭuvoḍaṁ
gāṅgēyanuṁ pratijñā
gāṅgēyanumorme nuḍidudaṁ tappuvarē // ViVi.84 [kandaṁ]

antacalita pratijñārūḍhanāda gāṅgēyananēgeydumoḍambaḍisalāṟade
satyavati tānumātanumāḷōcisi niścita mantrarāgi kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyananaṁ nenedu
barisidoḍe vyāsamunīndranēgeyvudēnaṁ tīrcuvudendoḍe satyavatiyintendaḷ
hiraṇyagarbha brahmariṁ taguḷdavyavacchinnamāgi banda sōmavaṁśamīgaḷemma
kulasantatigamārumilladeḍe vaṟidu kiḍuvantāgirdudadu kāraṇadiṁ nimma tammaṁ
vicitravīryana kṣētradoḷambikegamambālegaṁ putrarappantu varaprasādamaṁ
dayegeyvudene antegeyvenendu—

tridaśa narāsurōraga gaṇa prabhu niścita tattvayōgi yō
gada balamuṇmi poṇmi nile putra varārthigaḷāgi tanna ka
ṭṭidiroḷe nindaraṁ nayade nōḍe munīndrana divya dr̥ṣṭi maṁ
tradoḷe podaḻdudā satiyarirvaroḷaṁ nava garbha vibhramaṁ // ViVi.85 [campakamāle]

antu divya saṁyōgadoḷirvaruṁ garbhamaṁ tāḷdar mattorva maganaṁ
varamaṁ bēḍendambikege pēḻdoḍākeyuṁ vyāsabhaṭṭārakanallige pōgalalasi tanna
sūḻāyteyaṁtannavole kaygeydu baravaṁ bēḍalaṭṭidoḍākege varadanāgi
vyāsamunīndraṁ satyavatigaṁ bhīṣmaṅgamintendanenna vara prasāda kāladoḷennaṁ
[p. 21]
kaṇḍambike kaṇṇaṁ muccidaḷappudaṟindākege dhr̥tarāṣṭranemba maganatyanta
sundarāṅganāgiyuṁ jātyandhanakkumambāle madrūpamaṁ kaṇḍu mogamaṁ
pāṇḍuraṁ māḍidaḷappudaṟindākege pāṇḍurōga saṅgatanumanēka bhadra lakṣaṇa
lakṣitanumatyanta pratāpanumāgi pāṇḍurājanemba maganakkumambikeya
sūḻāyteyappāke darahasita vadanāravindeyāgi baravaṁ kaikoṇḍaḷappudaṟindākeya
magaṁ viduranembananaṅgākāranumācāravantanuṁ buddhivantanumakkumendu pēḻdu
munipuṅgavaṁ pōdanittaṁ—

varambaḍeda santasaṁ manadoḷāgalonduttarō
ttaraṁ baḷeva māḻkeyiṁ baḷeva garbhamaṁ tāḷdiyā
daraṁ berasu pettarandu dhr̥tarāṣṭra vikhyāta pāṁ
ḍurāja vidurarkaḷaṁ kramade mūvaruṁ mūvaraṁ // ViVi.86 [pr̥thvi]

ā vividha lakṣaṇaṅgaḷo
ḷāvarisida kulada balada caladaḷavigaḷoḷ
mūvarumanādi puruṣar
mūvarumenalalladattamattēnembar‌ // ViVi.87 [kandaṁ]

antavarge jātakarma nāmakaraṇānnaprāśana caulōpanayanādiṣōḍaśa
kriyegaḷaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ tāṁ muntiṭṭu māḍi śastra śāstraṅgaḷoḷati pariṇataraṁ
māḍi maduveyaṁ māḍalendu dhr̥tarāṣṭaṅge gāndhārarāja saubalana
magaḷappa gāndhāriyaṁ śakuniyoḍavuṭṭidaḷaṁ tandukoṭṭu—

mattitta negaḻteya puru
ṣōttamana pitāmahaṅgeśūraṅgemagaḷ
mattagajagamane yadu vaṁ
śōttameyene kunti kuntibhōjana maneyoḷ // ViVi.88 [kandaṁ]


[p. 22]
baḷeyuttirpannegamā
naḷināsyeya geydudondu śuśrūṣe manaṁ
goḷe koṭṭaṁdurvāsaṁ
viḷasita mantrākṣaraṅgaḷaṁ dayeyindaṁ // ViVi.89 [kandaṁ]

antu koṭṭaydu mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanāhvānaṅgeydu ninna bagege banda
pōlveya makkaḷaṁ paḍeveyendu besasidoḍondu divasaṁ konti—

puccavaṇaṁ nōḍuvene
nnicceyoḷī muniya varada mahimeyanenutaṁ
duccastani gaṅgege śapha
rōccaḷita tarattaraṅgegorvaḷe bandaḷ // ViVi.90 [kandaṁ]

bandu suranadiya nīroḷ
mindinanaṁ nōḍi ninna doreyane magana
kkendāhvānaṅgeyyalo
ḍaṁ dal dharegiḻidanandu daśaśatakiraṇaṁ // ViVi.91 [kandaṁ]

antu nabhōbhāgadiṁ bhūmibhāgakkiḻidu tanna munde nindaravinda
bāndhavanaṁ nōḍi nōḍi—

koḍagūsutanada bhayadiṁ
naḍuguva kannikeya bemara nīrgaḷa ponalo
ḻkuḍiyaloḍagūḍegaṅgeya
maḍu karegaṇmidudu nāṇa pempēṁ piridō // ViVi.92 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷādityanākeya manada śaṅkeyamaṁ naḍuguva meyya naḍukamumaṁ
kiḍenuḍidintendaṁ—

barisida kāraṇamāvudo
taruṇi munīśvarana mantramē doreyendā[ṁ]
maruḷiyeneyaṟidumaṟiyade |
barisideninnēḻimendoḍāgadu pōgal // ViVi.93 [kandaṁ]


[p. 23]
muṁ bēḍida varamaṁ kuḍa
dambujamukhi putranenna doreyaṁ ninaga
kkembudumodavida garbhado
ḷambujamitranane pōlva maganogetandaṁ // ViVi.94 [kandaṁ]

oḍavuṭṭida maṇikuṇḍala
moḍavuṭṭida sahaja kavacamamardire tannoḷ
toḍardireyuṁ bandākeya
naḍukamanoḍarisida[nā]gaḷā bā[likeyā] // ViVi.95 [kandaṁ]

antu naḍanaḍa naḍugi jaladēvategaḷappoḍaṁ manaṅgāṇbarendu nidhāna
manīḍāḍuvante kūsaṁ gaṅgeyoḷīḍāḍi bandaḷitta gaṅgādēviyumā kūsaṁ
muḻugalīyade tanna teregaḷemba naḷitōḷgaḷinoyyanoyyane taḻkaisi tare
gaṅgātīradoḷirpa sūtanembavaṁ kaṇḍu—

bāḷa dinēśa bimbada neḻal jaladoḷ nelasittomēṇ phaṇīṁ
drāḷayadindamurcidaphaṇāmaṇi maṅgaḷa raśmiyō karaṁ
mēḷisidappudennerdeyanendu bodillene pāydu nīroḷā
bāḷananādamādarade kaṇḍosedaṁ nidhigaṇḍanantevōl // ViVi.96 [utpalamālike]

antu kaṇḍu manaṅgoṇḍettikoṇḍu manege tandu rādheyemba tanna nallaḷa
sōṅkiloḷ kūsaniṭṭoḍāke rāgisi sutana sūtakamaṅkoṇḍāḍe—

aguḻdiralā kuḻiyoḷ to
ṭṭage nidhigaṇḍante vasudhegasadaḷamāytā
maga[na]ndamendu[lōgar]
bagedire vasuṣēṇanemba pesarāytāgaḷ // ViVi.97 [kandaṁ]

antu vasuṣēṇanālō
kāntambaramaḷavi baḷeye baḷadesakamadō
rante janaṅgaḷakarṇō
pāntadoḷogedeseye karṇanembanumādaṁ // ViVi.98 [kandaṁ]


[p. 24]
āgiyātaṁ śastraśāstra vidyeyoḷati pariṇatanāgi navayauvanārambhadoḷ—

poḍedudu billa jēvoḍeye mīṟuva vairi narēndraraṁ siḍi
lvoḍedavolaṭṭi muṭṭi kaḍidikkidudādeḍaraṁ nirantaraṁ
kaḍikaḍidittaponne budhamāgadhavandi janakke koṭṭa kō
ḍeḍarade bēḍiresp="#ed">mōḍimidu cāgada bīrada mātu karṇanā // ViVi.99 [campakamāle]

antu bhuvana bhavanakkellaṁ negaḻda karṇana pogaḻteyaṁ negaḻteyumanindraṁ
kēḷdu munde tannaṁśadoḷ puṭṭuvarjunaṅgamātaṅgaṁ dvandva yuddhamuṇṭembudaṁ
tanna divya jñānadindamaṟiduvintalladītananātaṁ gelal bāradendu—

bēḍidoḍe balada bariyuva
nīḍāḍugumugidu karṇanendāgaḷe kai
gūḍida vaṭuvākr̥tiyoḷe
bēḍidanā sahaja kavacamaṁ kuṇḍaḷamaṁ // ViVi.100 [kandaṁ]

bēḍidudanaridukoḷḷene
bēḍidudaṁ muṭṭalāgadenagene negaḻda
llāḍade koḷḷendaridī
ḍāḍidanidraṅge kavacamaṁ rādhēyaṁ // ViVi.101 [kandaṁ]

enduṁ pōgendane mā
ṇendane peṟatondanīvenendane nondaḥ
endane seragillade piḍi
yendanidēṁ kaliyo cāgiyō ravitanayaṁ // ViVi.102 [kandaṁ]

antu tanna sahaja kavacamaṁ nettar pana pana pariye tidiyugivantugidu
koṭṭoḍindranātana kalitanake mecci—

sura danuja bhujaga vidyā
dhara narasaṅkuladoḷāranādoḍamēnō
garamuṭṭe kolgamidu nija
virōdhiyaṁ dhuradoḷendu śaktiyanittaṁ // ViVi.103 [kandaṁ]


[p. 25]
antindranitta śaktiyaṁ kaikoṇḍu nijabhujaśaktiyaṁ prakaṭaṁ māḍalendu
rēṇukānandananallige pōgi—

kūriseguru śuśrūṣeyo
ḷā rāmananugra paraśu pāṭita ripu vaṁ
śārāmananiṣuvidyā
pāraganenisidudu balme vaikartananā // ViVi.104 [kandaṁ]

antu dhanurdharāgragaṇyanāgirdondu divasaṁ tanna toḍeya mēle
taleyaniṭṭu paraśurāmaṁ maṟedoṟagidā prastāvadoḷā munige munisaṁ
māḍalendindranupāyadoḷaṭṭida vajrakīṭaṅgaḷ karṇaneraḍuṁ toḍeyumanuḷiya
nūṟi koḍantiyoḷ beṭṭidantattamittamurci pōgeyumadanaṟiyadante guruge
nidrābhighātamakkumendu taleyanugurusuttu mireyire—

ativiśadaviśālōru
kṣatadindoṟedanitu jaḍeyumaṁ nāndi manaḥ
kṣatadoḍaneḻcarisidudu
tthitamāvandasra miśragandhaṁ muniyaṁ // ViVi.105 [kandaṁ]

anteḻcattu nettara ponaloḷ nāndu naneda maiyyumaṁ toydu taḷpoyda
jaḍeyumaṁ kaṇḍī dhairyaṁ kṣatriyaṅgalladāgadu pārvanendennoḷ pusidu
viddeyaṁkaikoṇḍudarke daṇḍaṁ peṟatilla ninagānitta brahmāstramemba divyāstra
mavasāna kāladoḷ besakeyyadirkendu śāpavanittanantu karṇanuṁ śāpahatanāgi
maguḻdu bandu sūtana maneyoḷirpannegamittal kuntigavaramāvanappakuntibhōjanuṁ svayambaraṁ māḍe—

sogayipa tamma javvanada tamma vibhūtiya tamma tamma ce
lvugaḷa vilāsadurmegaḷoḷāvevagāgipevendu banda ce
nnigarumanāsekāṟarumanollade celviḍidirda rūpu dr̥
ṣṭigevare pāṇḍurājanane kunti manambuge māle sūḍidaḷ // ViVi.106 [campakamāle]


[p. 26]
antu svayambaradoḷ neṟedarasumakkaḷoḷappukeyda kuntiyoḍane
madrarājana magaḷ śalyanoḍavuṭṭida mādriyumanonde paseyoḷirisi gāṅgēyaṁ
vidhātraṁ muṇḍāḍuvante tāṁ maduveyaṁ māḍi—

taḷirgaḷasaṁ mukundaravamettida muttina maṇṭapaṁ manaṁ
goḷipa vitānapaṅkti pasurvandaloḷoldeḍeyāḍuveydeyar
baḷasida vēda pāragara sandaṇiyembivaṟiṁ vivāha maṁ
gaḷamadu kuntimādrigaḷoḷaccariyādudu pāṇḍurājanā // ViVi.107 [campakamāle]

tuṟugeme nīḷda purvu niḍugaṇ poṟeyallade baṭṭitappa bā
ydeṟetanurēkhegoṇḍa koraloḍḍida parmole teḷvasiṟ karaṁ
neṟeda nitambavimbuvaḍeḷdoḍenakkaravaddi(?)tāne pō
kiṟudoḍeyendu dhātri pogaḻguṁ pogaḻvannare kunti mādrigaḷ // ViVi.108 [campakamāle]

antākegaḷirvarumeraḍuṁ keladoḷire kalpalategaḷeraḍaṟa naḍuvaṇa
kalpavr̥kṣamirpantirda pāṇḍurājaṅge dhr̥tarāṣṭranaṅgahīnanendu vivāhadosageyoḍane
paṭṭabandhadosageyaṁ māḍi nelananāḷise—

mīṟuvavembamāṇḍaḷikarīyadarembadaṭar‌vayalge me
yduṟuvavemba pūṇigaraḍaṅgikunuṅgisiḍildu jōldu kā
ypāṟenabhakke pāṟidudu gaṇḍara nettiyoḷotti bāḷani
nnūṟugumendoḍēṁ pirido tējada daḷḷuri pāṇḍurājanā // ViVi.109 [utpalamālike]

besakeydattu samudra mudrita dharācakraṁ pratāpakkagu
rvise gōḷuṇḍegoḷuttumirdudu diśācakraṁ podaḻdājñegaṁ
pesargaṁ munnamerūpuvōduduviyaccakraṁ samantembinaṁ
jasamāpāṇḍuramādudā nr̥paroḷārā pāṇḍurājambaraṁ // ViVi.110 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu pāṇḍurājanadhika tējanumavanata vairi bhūbhr̥tsamājanumāgi
negaḻuttirdondu divasaṁ tōpina bēṇṭeyanāḍalaḻtiyiṁ pōgi—


[p. 27]
iniyaḷanaḻteyinde mr̥gimāḍi manōja sukhakke sōltalaṁ
pinenereyalke divyamuniyuṁ mr̥gamāgi maraldu kūḍe me
llane mr̥gamendusārdu neṟanaṁ naḍe nōḍi narēndraneccu bhōṁ
kane mr̥gacāriyaṁ tanage māṇade tandanadondu māriyaṁ // ViVi.111 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ praḷayaduḷkamuḷkuvante tanneccambu munikumārana kaṇṇoḷa
merdeyoḷa mukke pēḻimennanāvaneccanemba muniya munida saramaṁ kēḷdu
billanambumanīḍāḍi tanna munde nindirda bhūpanaṁ muni nōḍi—

sannatadiṁ ratakkeḷasi nallaḷoḷōtoḍagūḍidennaniṁ
tanneyameccudarke peṟatilladudaṇḍamoṟaldu nallaḷoḷ
nīnnaḍenōḍiyuṁ bayasi kūḍiyumāgaḍe sāveyāgi pō
ginnene raudra śāpa paritāpa viḷāpadoḷā mahīśvaraṁ // ViVi.112 [utpalamālike]

enna geydakāmākrāntakkekāma kr̥tamēṁ piridaltu—

etta vanametta mr̥gayā
vr̥ttakamī tapasiyetta mr̥gameṁdentā
netteccenātmakarmā
yattaṁpeṟataltidellamaghaṭitaghaṭitaṁ // ViVi.113 [kandaṁ]

endu cintisuttuṁ poḻalge maguḻduvandu gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭravidurarkaḷge
tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ pēḻdu samasta vastugaḷaṁ dīnānāthajanaṅgaḷge sūṟegoṭṭu
nija parivāramaṁ barisi—

sāramanaṅgajaṅgamalatālalitāṅgiyarindaltesaṁ
sāramidembudinnenagetappudu tanmuni śāpadindami
nnārumidarke vakrisadiriṁ vanavāsadoḷirpenendu du
rvāra parākramaṁ taḷare bārisi vārisi kunti mādriyar // ViVi.114 [utpalamālike]

benna bennane bare binna binnane pōgi—


[p. 28]
tuṅga vanya mataṅgaja dantāghāta nipātita sallakī
bhaṅgamaṁ maṇimauktika nīḷa sthūḷa śilā pravibhāsitō
ttuṅgamaṁ muni mukhya mukhāmbhōjōdara nirgatamantra pū
tāṅgamaṁ nr̥paneydidanudyacchr̥ṅgamanā śataśr̥ṅgamaṁ // ViVi.115 [khacaraplutaṁ]

ā parvatada vipuḷa vanōpakaṇṭhaṅgaḷoḷ tāpasakanyeyar naḍapideḷalate
gaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugi sāmavēda dhvaniyoḷ moreva tumbigaḷumaṁ paṇteṟagida
tadāśramada tarugaḷa mēgirdu pugil pugilenditta bannimirimemba pombaṇṇada
kōgilegaḷumaṁ munikumārarōduva vēdavēdāṅgaṅgaḷaṁ tappuviḍidu jaḍidu
baggisuva padumarāgada baṇṇadaragiḷigaḷumaṁ surabhigaḷa toreda molegaḷanuṇbavaṟa
maṟigaḷaṁ pōge nūṅki kūṅki molegaḷanuṇba kiśōra kēsarigaḷumaṁ tammoḍane
nalidāḍuva kiśōrakēsarigaḷaṁ piḍidu tegeva karikaḷabhaṅgaḷumanāgaḷāpaḷuvaṅgaḷinde
pāyva puligaḷa maṟigaḷoḷ paridāḍuva taruṇa hariṇaṅgaḷumaṁ mattaṁ mutta
kuruḍatavasigaḷa kaiyaṁ piḍiduydavaraguhegaḷaṁ pugipa poṟamaḍipa capaḷa
kapigaḷumaṁ hōmāgniyaneṟaṅkeya gāḷiyiṁ nandalīyaduripuva rājahaṁse
gaḷumaṁmunigaṇēśvararoḍanedāḷivūgoyvoḍane varpa gōḷāṅgūḷaṅgaḷumaṁ
nōḍi tapōvanada tapōdhanara tapaḥprabhāvakke cōdyambaṭṭu—

vinayadinitta bannimirimembavoliñcaradindamoyyano
yyane maṟidumbigaḷa morevuvaḻkaṟoḷoldeṟapantetaḷta pū
vina posagoñcaliṁmaranidēnesedirduvo kaltuvāgadē
vinayamanī tapōdhanara kaiyoḷeśākhigaḷuṁnagēndra[dā] // ViVi.116 [campakamāle]

endu meccuttumenage nelasiralī tapōvaname pāvanamendu tapōvanada
munijanada paramānurāgamaṁpercisikāmānurāgamaṁ bercisi
tadāśramadoḷāśramakke guruvāgi pāṇḍurājanirpannegamitta dhr̥tarāṣṭrana
[p. 29]
mahādēviyappa gāndhāri nūrvarmakkaḷaṁ paḍevantu parāśara munīndranoḷ
barambaḍedaḷembudaṁ kunti kēḷdu tānuṁ putrārthi[ni]yāgal bagedu—

visasanadoḷ virōdhi nr̥paraṁ taṟidoṭṭalumarthigarthamaṁ
kasavina lekkamendu kuḍaluṁ vipuḷāyatiyaṁ digantadoḷ
pasarisaluṁ karaṁ neṟeva makkaḷanīyade nōḍe nāḍe nō
yisidapudikṣupuṣpadavolennaya niṣphala puṣpadarśanaṁ // ViVi.117 [campakamāle]

endu cintākrānteyāgirda kuntiyaṁ kaṇḍu pāṇḍurājanēkānta
doḷintendaṁ—

cinteyidēno santatige makkaḷe neṭṭane bārteyappoḍi
nnintiravēḍa divya munipuṅgavaraṁbagedīrpinaṁ nijā
tyanta pativratā guṇadinarcisi meccisu nīṁ diganta vi
śrānta yaśarkaḷaṁ vara tanūbhavaraṁ paḍe nīṁ taḷōdari // ViVi.118 [utpalamālike]

endoḍe kontiyintendaḷenna kannikeyā kāladoḷ nānenna māvaṁ
kontibhōjana maneyoḷ baḷevandu durvāsa mahāmuniyaremma manege niccakkaṁ
barparavarenna vinayakkaṁ bhaktigaṁ besakeyvudarkaṁ mecci mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanaydu
varavittarīyaydu mantrakayvarmakkaḷaṁ ninna bagege bandavara nāhvānaṁ geyyalavara
pōlveya makkaḷaṁ paḍeveyendu besasidoḍīgaḷenna puṇyadiṁ dorekoṇḍu
doḷḷittembudaṁ divya muni vākyamamōgha vākyamakkumadarkēnuṁ
cintisalvēḍendoḍante geyvenendu tīrtha jalaṅgaḷaṁ mindu daḷimbavanuṭṭu
muttina toḍigegaḷaṁ toṭṭu darbhaśayanadoḷirdu—

jñānadinirdu niṭṭipoḍe divya munīndrana koṭṭa mantra saṁ
tānamanōdiyōdi yamarājananadbhuta tējanaṁ sarō
jānane jānadiṁ barise bandu yamaṁ besanāvudāvudā
tmānugatārthamendoḍenagīvudu ninnane pōlva putranaṁ // ViVi.119 [utpalamālike]


[p. 30]
embuduṁ tathāstuvendu tannaṁśamanākeya garbhadoḷavatarisi yamabhaṭṭāraka
nantardhānakke sandanannegamā kāntege—

himadhavaḷātapatramane pōle mukhēnduva beḷpu pūrṇa kuṁ
bhamane nirantaraṁ gele kucaṅgaḷatōrpupatākeyondu vi
bhramamane pōle purvina poḍarpoḷakoṇḍudavaḷge garbha ci
hname gaḷa garbhadarbhakana sūcipa mundaṇa rājyacihnamaṁ // ViVi.120 [campakamāle]

antukontiyagarbhabhāramuṁ tāpasāśramadanurāgamumoḍanoḍane
baḷeye bandhujanada manōrathaṅgaḷumombattaneya tiṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane neṟeye—

vananidhiyindaṁ candraṁ
vinatōdaradiṁ garutmanudayācaḷadiṁ
dinapanogevante puṭṭida
nanivārya sutējanenipaninajana tanayaṁ // ViVi.121 [kandaṁ]

puṭṭuvuduṁ dharmamumoḍa
vuṭṭidudītanoḷe dharmanaṁśadoḷītaṁ
puṭṭidanendā śiśugose
diṭṭudu muni samiti dharmasutanene pesaraṁ // ViVi.122 [kandaṁ]

antu pesaraniṭṭu parakeyaṁ koṭṭu—

santasadinirdu makkaḷa
santatigī doreyarinnumāgadoḍentuṁ
santasamenagillendā
kānte suta bhrānte munninantevolirdaḷ // ViVi.123 [kandaṁ]

mantrākṣara niyamadinabhi
mantrisi barisidoḍe vāyudēvaṁ bandēṁ
mantraṁ pēḻene kuḍu ripu
tantrakṣayakarananenage hitanaṁ sutanaṁ // ViVi.124 [kandaṁ]

embudumadēviridittenendu viyattaḷakkogedoḍātanaṁśamākeya
garbhasarōvaradoḷage candrabimbadante sogayise—


[p. 31]
trivaḷigaḷuṁ virōdhinr̥parutsavamuṁ kiḍevanduvānanēṁ
duva kaḍuveḷpu kūsina negaḻteya beḷpuvolāytu munneba
ḷḷuva naḍutōrpa meyyanoḷakoṇḍudupoṅgoḍanaṁ tamāḷa pa
llavadoḷe muccidandadoḷe cūcukamāntudukarpanākeyā // ViVi.125 [campakamāle]

ā sudatiya mr̥du pada vi
nyāsamumaṁ śēṣanānalāradesuydaṁ
bēsaṟinendoḍegarbhada
kūsina baḷedaḷaviyaḷavanaḷevarumoḷarē // ViVi.126 [kandaṁ]

antugarbhanirbharapradēśadoḷarātigaḷgantakālaṁ dorekoḷvante prasūti
kālaṁ dorekoḷe—

śubha tithi śubha nakṣatraṁ
śubha vāraṁ śubha muhūrtamene gaṇakaniḷā
prabhuvogedanuditakāya
prabheyogedire daḷita śatrugōtraṁ putraṁ // ViVi.127 [kandaṁ]

bhīmaṁ bhayaṅkaraṁ peṟa
tē mātī kūsinandamītana pesaruṁ
bhīmane pōgene munijana
mīmāḻkeyināytu śiśuge pesaranvarthaṁ // ViVi.128 [kandaṁ]

antu bharatakulatilakarappirvarmakkaḷaṁ pettu konti santasadantama
neydirpudumatta dhr̥tarāṣṭrana mahādēviyappa gāndhāri kēḷdu tanna garbhaṁ
taḍedudarke kinisi kiṅkirivōgi—

santatige piriya makkaḷa
nāṁ taḍeyade paḍevenendoḍenniṁ munnaṁ
kontiye paḍedaḷ garbhada
cinteyadinnēvudendu basiṟaṁ posedaḷ // ViVi.129 [kandaṁ]


[p. 32]
posedoḍe pālgaḍalaṁ magu
ḻdasurar posedalli kāḷakūṭāṅkuramaṁ
dasadaḷamogedantogeduvu
basiṟiṁnūṟondu piṇḍavaruṇākīrṇaṁ // ViVi.130 [kandaṁ]

avaṁ kaṇḍu kinisi kirceḻdivellavaṁ poṟage bisuṭu bannimembuduṁ
vyāsabhaṭṭārakaṁ bandu gāndhāriyaṁ baggisi—

odavuge ninna santatige nūrvarudagra sutarkaḷonde ga
rbhadoḷene kemmanintu posedikkide polladugeydeyendu mā
ṇade muni nūṟupiṇḍamumanāgaḷe tīvida kammanappa tu
ppada koḍadoḷ samantu maḍagiṭṭoḍe sr̥ṣṭige cōdyamappinaṁ // ViVi.131 [campakamāle]

antu nūrvaroḷorvanagurbu parbi parakalise sampūrṇa vayaskanāgi
ghr̥ta ghaṭavighaṭanumāgipuṭṭuvuduṁ—

pratimegaḷaḻtuvumoḻagidu
dati rabhasade dhātri desegaḷuriduvu bhūta
pratatigaḷāḍiduvoḷaṟidu
vatiramyasthānadoḷ śivānivahaṅgaḷ // ViVi.132 [kandaṁ]

antogedanēkōtpātaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍu mundaṟiva cadura viduranintendaṁ—

ītane namma kulakkaṁ
kētudalānaṟivenalladandēkinitu
tpātaṁ tōrpuvu bisuḍuvu |
dītana peṟaguḻida sutare santatigappar // ViVi.133 [kandaṁ]

endoḍaṁ putramōha kāraṇavāgi dhr̥tarāṣṭranuṁ gāndhāriyu mēgeydu
moḍambaḍadirdoḍutpāta śāntika pauṣṭika kriyegaḷaṁ mahā brāhmaṇarindaṁ baḷeyisi
baddavaṇamaṁ bājisi maṅgaḷamaṁ pāḍisi kūsiṅge duryōdhananendu pesaraniṭṭu
mattina kūsugaḷgellaṁ duśyāsanādiyāgi nāmaṅgaḷaniṭṭu parakeyaṁ koṭṭu—


[p. 33]
sukamirpannegamitta kunti śataśr̥ṅgādrīndradoḷ divya bā
lakaninnorvananugra vairimadavanmātaṅga kumbhārdamau
ktika lagnōjjvala bāṇanaṁpravilasadgīrvāṇa dātavya sā
yaka sampūrṇa kaḷāpravīṇananiḷā bhāra kṣamākṣūṇanaṁ // ViVi.134 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu sarva lakṣaṇa sampūrṇanappa magananamōghaṁ paḍevenembu
dyōgamanettikoṇḍu pāṇḍurājanuṁ tānuṁ—

eṟagiyumorme divya munigārtupavāsamanirdumorme ko
ydaṟikeya pūgaḷiṁ śivananarcisiyuṁ biḍadorme nōntumō
daṟivara pēḻda nōmpigaḷanorme palarmeyumintu tamma me
ymaṟevinamirvaruṁ namedarēnavargādudo putradōhaḷaṁ // ViVi.135 [campakamāle]

alasade māḍi bēsaṟade sālgumidennade meysogakke paṁ
balisade niddegeṭṭuniḍujāgaradoḷtoḍardēka pādadoḷ

salisidarantu nōnade guṇārṇavanaṁ paḍeyalke tīrgumē // ViVi.136 [campakamāle]

antondu varṣambaraṁ bharaṅgeydu nōntu pūrvakramadoḷondu

sulipal miñcinagoñcaluṭṭa dugulaṁ gaṅgānadī phēnamu
jjvala muktābharaṇaṁ tarattaraḷatārōdāra bhā bhāramaṁ
galatālālitasāndra candanarasaṁ beḷdiṅgaḷembondu paṁ
bala bambalge[ḍe]yāge beḷpasadanaṁ kaṇgoppitā kānteyā // ViVi.137 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu tanna kaikoṇḍa beḷpasadanadoḷ kīrti śrīyaṁvākśrīyumana

neneda manaṁ peṟaguḻida
ttene beḷaguva ratnadīpti suradhanu negeda
ttene neydilgoḷanalarda
ttene kaṇgaḷa baḷagamāgaḷindraṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.138 [kandaṁ]


[p. 34]
besanēnēgeyvudo nina
gosedēnaṁ kuḍuvudendoḍendaḷ makkaḷ
osageyanenagīvudu ni
nnesakada masakamane pōlvamaganaṁmaghavā // ViVi.139 [kandaṁ]

embudumākeya bageda bageyoḷoḍambaḍuvante kulagirigaḷa biṇpumaṁ
dharātaḷada tiṇpumanādityana tējadaguntiyumaṁcandrana kāntiyumaṁ madanana
saubhāgyamumaṁ kalpataruvinudāraśaktiyumanīśvarana prabhuśaktiyumaṁ javana
ballāḷtanamumaṁ siṁhada kalitanamumanavaravaradesegaḷiṁ tegedondumāḍi
kontiya divya garbhōdaramemba śukti puṭōdaradoḷtanna divyāṁśavemba
muktāphalōdabinduvanindraṁ saṅkramisi nijanivāsakke pōdanannegamitta
kontiyumandina beḷagappa jāvadoḷ sukhanidreyāgi—

kuḍivudanēḻumambudhiyamaṁ kulaśailakuḷaṅgaḷaṁ tagu
ḷdaḍarvudanondu bāḷa ravi tannaya sōgila mēge rāgadiṁ
poḍarvudanante dikkarigaḷambujapatrapuṭāmbuviṁ beḍaṁ
gaḍasire majjanambugipudaṁ sati kaṇḍosedaḷ niśāntadoḷ // ViVi.140 [campakamāle]

antu kaṇḍu munikumārarōduva vēdaninādadiṁ vigatanidreyāgi
pāṇḍurājaṅgamalliya munijanaṅgaḷgamaṟipidoḍavarā kanasugaḷge
santōṣambaṭṭu—

kuḍivudaṟindamabdhigaḷanabdhiparīta mahīśanaṁ tagu
ḷdaḍarvudaṟiṁ kulādri parivēṣṭitanaṁ taruṇārkananaḻkaṟiṁ
poḍarvudaṟindamendumuditōditanaṁ digibhaṅgaḷeṇṭumo
ḷpoḍarisi majjanambugise kaṇḍudaṟiṁ kamalābhirāmanaṁ // ViVi.141 [campakamāle]

intappa maganaṁ nīnamōghaṁ paḍeveyendu munijanaṅgaḷ pēḻva
śubhasvapnaphalaṅgaḷoḍanoḍane garbhacihnaṅgaḷuṁ tōṟe pagevara peṇḍira
[p. 35]
mogaṅgaḷumākeya kucacūcukaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane kandiduvākeya vaḷitra
yaṅgaḷuṁ pagevara śaktitrayaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane keṭṭuvākeya bāsegaḷuṁ pagevara
bāḻvāsegaḷumoḍanoḍanasiyavāduvākeya mandagamanamuṁ pagevara
manaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍanalasikeyaṁ kaikoṇḍuvākeya naḍuvina baḍatanamuṁ pagevara
siriyumoḍanoḍane keṭṭuvā samayadoḷ—

urcida bāḷoḷātma mukhabimbamanaḻtiye nōḍaluṁ manaṁ
perci dhanurlatā guṇa ninādamanālisi kēḷalu manaṁ
bercade siṁha pōtakamanōvalumākeya dōhaḷaṁ karaṁ
percidudā guṇārṇavana mundaṇa bīramanandetōrpavōl // ViVi.142 [utpalamālike]

mattamēḻuṁ samudraṅgaḷa nīranondumāḍi mīyaluṁ vēḷāvana
latāgr̥hōdara puḷinasthaḷa parisarapradēśadoḷ toḻalalumaḻtiyāge—

baḷeda nitambadekāñcī
kaḷāpamaṁ kaṭṭalaṇame neṟeyadidenda
ggaḷisi kuḷikegaḷinēṁ ka
ṇgoḷisidudōsubhageyāda sudatiya garbhaṁ // ViVi.143 [kandaṁ]

antu tekkane tīvida meyyoḷalarda sampageyaralante beḷarta baṇṇaṁ
guṇārṇavaṅge māḍida baṇṇadante sogayisi baḷedu—

tuḍugegaḷoḷ sarigeyumaṁ
kaḍuviṇṇittenisi naḍedumōraḍiyanaṇaṁ
naḍeyalumāṟade kemmane
biḍadārayvanitumāge baḷedudu garbhaṁ // ViVi.144 [kandaṁ]

antā baḷeda garbhadoḷ sampūrṇaprasavasamayaṁ dorekoḷe grahaṅgaḷellaṁ

doḷ—


[p. 36]

udayisuvudumamr̥tāṁśuvi

tridaśakarāhatiyinoḍane suradundubhigaḷ // ViVi.146 [kandaṁ]

antu moḻaguva suradundubhigaḷuṁ parasuva jayajaya dhvanigaḷuṁ

dēvara paṟegaḷa ravadoḷ
dēvara surivarala sariya beḷsariyoḷ ta
ddēva vimānāvaḷiyoḷ
tīvidudormodale gaganadiṁdhare madhyaṁ // ViVi.147 [kandaṁ]

antu hiraṇyagarbhabrahmaṁ modalāge vyāsa kaśyapa vasiṣṭha vālmīki viśvāmitra
jamadagni bhāradvājāgastya pulastya nārada pramukharappa divya munipatigaḷumēkādaśa
rudraruṁ dvādaśādityarumaṣṭavasugaḷumaśvinīdēvaruṁ modalāge mūvatta
mūdēvaruṁ indraṁ berasu vaimānika dēvaruṁ neredu pāṇḍurājanumaṁ
kuntiyumaṁ parasi kūsiṅgejanmōtsavamaṁ māḍi—

nōḍuvanā brahmaṁ muṁ
ḍāḍuvanamarēndranindranaccaraseyare
ḻdāḍuvarendoḍe pogaḻa
lvēḍa guṇārṇavana janmadinada beḍaṅgaṁ // ViVi.148 [kandaṁ]

antu piridumosageyaṁ māḍi dēvasabheyuṁ brahmasabheyumoḍanirdu
nāmakaraṇōtsava nimittaṅgaḷappa nāmaṅgaḷoḷītaṁ sakala bhuvana saṁstūyamānaṁ
[p. 37]
cāḷukyavaṁśōdbhavaṁ śrīmadarikēsari vikramārjunanudāttanārāyaṇaṁ
pracaṇḍa mārtāṇḍanudāra mahēśvaraṁkadanatriṇētraṁ manujamāndhātaṁ pratijñā
gāṅgēyaṁ śaucāñjanēyanakaḷaṅkarāmaṁ sāhasabhīmaṁpratyakṣa jīmūta vāhanaṁ
jagadēkamallaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ atirathamathanaṁvairigajaghaṭāvighaṭanaṁ vidviṣṭa
vidrāvaṇanarāti kāḷānaḷaṁ ripukuraṅgakaṇṭhīravaṁ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ parākrama dhavaḷaṁ
samaraikamēru śaraṇāgata jalanidhi vinayavibhūṣaṇaṁ manunidānananūnadāni
lōkaika kalpadrumaṁ gajagamanarājaputranārūḍhasarvajñaṁ gandhēbhavidyādharaṁ
nr̥paparamātmaṁ vibudha vanajavanakaḷahaṁsaṁsurata makaradhvajaṁ sahajamanōjaṁ
āndhrīkucakaḷaśa pallavaṁ karṇāṭī karṇapūraṁ lāṭīlalāmaṁ kēraḷīkēḷi
kandarpaṁ saṁsārasārōdayaṁ maṟuvakkadallaḻaṁ nōḍuttegelvaṁ pāṇbaraṅkusaṁ
ammanagandhavāraṇaṁ paḍemecce gaṇḍaṁpriyagaḷḷaṁguṇanidhi guṇārṇavaṁ sāmanta
cūḍāmaṇiyendintivu modalāge palavumaṣṭōttara śatanāmaṅgaḷaniṭṭu viśēṣā
śīrvacanaṅgaḷiṁ parasi—

saptasamudra mudrita dharātaḷamaṁ besakeysu mīṟida
ddr̥pta virōdhi sādhanamanāhavadoḷ taṟidoṭṭu viśvadi
gvyāptayaśōviḷāsinigevallabhanāgu nirantara sukha
vyāptige nīne mottamodalāgarikēsari lōkamuḷḷinaṁ // ViVi.149 [utpalamālike]

śrīgagaluramaṁ kīrti

yāgisi nīṁ nelasu nēsaṟuḷḷinamarigā // ViVi.1 [kandaṁ]

emba parakegaḷa ravadoḷ
tumbenabhō vivaramamaramunijanamamarēṁ
draṁ berasu taḷardudāduda
ḷumbaṁ manadosage kuntigaṁ tatpatigaṁ // ViVi.2 [kandaṁ]

antu guṇārṇavana puṭṭidosageyoḷosagemaruḷgoṇḍu kuntiyuṁ
pāṇḍurājanumire mādri tanage makkaḷilladudarke virakteyāgi posedu bisuṭa
raktāśōka pallavadante karaṁ koragi cintisutirdoḍākeyabinnanādamogadandamaṁ
kaṇḍu kunti karuṇisi putrōtpatti nimittaṅgaḷappa mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanupadēśaṁ
geydoḍākeyuṁ tadukta kriyeyoḷaṁ niyama niyamiteyāgi—

āhvānaṁgeydaśvini
dēvaranavaritta varadoḷavaraṁśame saṁ
bhāvise garbhadoḷamaḷara
nā vanajadaḷākṣi paḍedu santativettaḷ // ViVi.3 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷā pāṇḍurājanā kūsugaḷge jātakarmamaṁ munigaḷiṁ baḷeyisi
nakula sahadēvarendavargamaḷvesaraniṭṭu putra sampūrṇa manōrathanāgirpinamayvar
kūsugaḷumēḻgevāḍivada candranantuttarābhivr̥ddhiyoḷ sogayisi baḷeye
bharatakulakke viśada yaśōṅkuraṅgaḷuṁ bandhujanakke puṇyāṅkuraṅgaḷuṁ vandijanakke
kalpavr̥kṣāṅkuraṅgaḷumarātijanakke kāḷakūṭāṅkuraṅgaḷumaṁ pōltu pañcāṅga
mantra[ṁ]svarūpadoḷ mūrtimantaṁ gaḷādante sogayisi baḷeye—


[p. 39]
toḍardamarda bāḷavaṇṇada
tuḍuge paḷañcaleva pañca jaḍe nosaloḷoḍaṁ
baḍuvaraḷeleyivaṟiṁ ce
lviḍidirdudu bāḷa kēḷi dharmātmajanā // ViVi.4 [kandaṁ]

antātaṁ baḷeyevaḷeye—

naḍeva taḷarnaḍeyoḷ puḍi
vuḍiyāduvu śilegaḷoḍedu karigaḷ bhīmaṁ
piḍidaḍardoḍe bāyviṭṭe
lvaḍagāduvu muddadantu sogayisavēḍā // ViVi.5 [kandaṁ]

munivanamane bisuṭuvumuṁ
muniyara sōṅkiloḷe baḷeda siṅgaṅgaḷ mu
ddinoḷaḍarva piḍiva gurduva
manegeḻevanitarkamalasimarudātmajanā // ViVi.6 [kandaṁ]

antātaṁ baḷeye—

bēḍadudaṁ bēḍuva puḍi

paredaḍarda dhūḷi kiṟunage

ḷdagalada celvina molleya
muguḷgaḷaniḷisire gaṇārṇavaṁ sogayisidaṁ // ViVi.9 [kandaṁ]


[p. 40]
karikaḷabhaṅgaḷa śiśu kē

tiripi piḍiyuttumarigaṁ
paridāḍuvasamavaya[skaro]ḷsogayisidaṁ // ViVi.10 [kandaṁ]

deyvabalaṁ sogasikemuṁ
geyva balaṁ bāḷa kāladoḷ toḍarda poḍa
rdayvara bālakriyeyuṁ
muyvaṁ nōḍisitu tāyumaṁ tandeyumaṁ // ViVi.11 [kandaṁ]

antā kūsugaḷ nija jananī janakara manamaniḻkuḷigoḷisiyumarātijanaṅgaḷa manamanasuṅgoḷisiyuṁ baḷeye baḷeye—

alardadirmutte pūta posa mallige kampanavuṅkutirpa teṁ

gile nanedōṟi nuṇpeseva māmaranormodalalladuṇmuvu
yyala posagāvaraṁ pugiloḷēnesedatto basanta māsadoḷ // ViVi.12 [campakamāle]

āgaḷā basantarājana baraviṅge guḍigaṭṭidante baḷvaḷa baḷeda miḷirvaśōkeya
taḷirgaḷumātana baraviṅge tōraṇaṅgaṭṭidante banda māmaraṅgaḷanaḍardu
toḍardeḷakombugaḷviḍidu maradiṁ marakke dāṅguḍiviḍuva mādhavīlategaḷumātana
baraviṅge neṟeye sogayise keygeyva nallaḷante naneya birimuguḷgaḷa tuṟuga
ḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugida kalpalategaḷumātana baraviṅge baddavaṇaṁ bājipante bhōrgaredu
moreva tumbigaḷumātana baraviṅge raṅgavaliyikkidante puḷinasthaḷaṅgaḷoḷudirda
kaḻivūgaḷumātana baraviṅge vanavanite mecci neṟeye keygeydante niṟiniṟigoṇḍu
sogayisuva niṟigana niṟidaḷira goñcalgaḷumātana mēlvāye rāgisi rōmāṅkura
mogedantogeda kaḷikāṅkuraṅgaḷumātanaṅgasaṅgadoḷ kāmarasamuguvantuguva
soneyasōnegaḷumanoḷakoṇḍu tadāśramada nandanavanaṅga[ḷ]janaṅgaḷa
nanaṅgaṅgetoḻtuvesaṅgeysiduvu—


[p. 41]
birayiya miḻtuveṁmididoḍalladaṇaṁ muḷisāṟadendu pa
lmoredapanilli manmathanidaṁ pugaliṁgaḍimendu bēṭakā
ṟaraniradūṟi sāṟi jaḍivanteseguṁ sahakāra kōmaḷāṁ
kura parituṣṭa puṣṭa parapuṣṭagaḷadhvani nandanaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.13 [campakamāle]

kaviva madāḷiyiṁ masuḷanāgi payōjarajaṅgaḷoḷ kavi
lgavilanuvāgi banda malayānilanūdeteraḷva cūta pa
llavada teraḷke tadvana viḷāsiniyuṭṭa dukūladondu pa

pōgade pāḍutirpaḷiye br̥ṁhitamāgire candrakānti kā
ypāgire bīsuvondelare bīsuvudāgire kāygaḷindamiṁ

antu toṭṭa pūduḍuge madanana toṭṭa pūgaṇegeṇeyāgire—

miḷirva kuruḷgaḷoḷ toḍardu dēsiyanāvagamīva cenna pū
gaḷanavanoyyanōsarisutuṁ vadanābjada kampanāḷduṇal
baḷasuva tumbiyaṁ piḍida neydiloḷoyyane sōvutuṁ beḍaṁ
goḷakoḷe sorkidaṅgaja mataṅgajadantire barpa mādriyaṁ // ViVi.17 [campakamāle]

tāpasāśramadiṁ poṟamaṭṭante banamaṁ toḻalva pāṇḍurājaṁkaṇḍu—

sogayise toṭṭa pūduḍuge mellerdeyoḷ taḍamāḍe gāḍidi
ṭṭigaḷoḷanaṅgarāgarasamuṇmuvinaṁ naḍe nōḍi nōḍi to

[p. 42]
ṭṭage koḷe mēle pāydavaḷanappidanā vibhu tanna śāpamaṁ
bageyademiḻtudēvateyanaḻkaḷurkeyinappuvantevōl // ViVi.18 [campakamāle]

antappuvuduṁviṣamaviṣavalliyanappidante taḷta nallaḷa mr̥dumr̥ṇāḷa

bigidamardirda tōḷ saḍile jōle mogaṁ mogadindamoyyago

llage maṟasondidandadoḷe jōlda nijēśananā latāṅgi to

endu paṟipaṭṭa suyyumaṁ kōḍuva meyyumaṁ kaṇḍu paralōka

tāpasana śāpamembudu
pāpada rūpaṟitumaṟiyadantēke manaṁ
gāpaḻidu bandu muṭṭide
yōpane nīnenna pāpakarmiya meyyaṁ // ViVi.20 [kandaṁ]

nīnninna sāvanadanena

ninnoḍane vandu dinadoḷ
ninna manōrathamanarasa neṟapade māṇeṁ // ViVi.21 [kandaṁ]

unnata dhavaḷacchatra

ḷennarasananintubidiyetandikkuvudē // ViVi.22 [kandaṁ]

baḻiyane makkaḷ bhōrgare

ṭveḻale naḍunaḍuge kaṇṇīr
gaḻagaḻanormodalesuriye paritandāgaḷ // ViVi.24 [kandaṁ]

antu tanna nallana kaḷēvaramaṁ taḻkaisikoṇḍu tanna sāvaṁ paricchēdisi

aḍaviyoḷennumanennī
naḍapida śiśugaḷumanirisi nīṁ pēḻade pō
doḍamēnō ninna baḻiyane
naḍetarpeṁ ninnarasa bisuṭentirpeṁ // ViVi.25 [kandaṁ]

endu nīnī kūsugaḷaṁ kaikoṇḍu naḍapu nallananenagoppisānātanādu

enagindinondu sūḻuma
niniyaṁ dayegeydanenna sūḻaṁ ninagā
nenitādoḍamīvenema
ttanayarkeyyeḍepalumbadir‌ peṟapeṟavaṁ // ViVi.26 [kandaṁ]

endu tapōvanada munijanamuṁ vanadēvatājanamuṁ tannaṇmaṁ
pogaḻe mādri pāṇḍurājanoḍanedāhōttaradante(?) kirciṅgekuladoḷaṁ
caladoḷamāvakanduṁ kundumillade tannoregaṁ doregamārumillenisidāgaḷ
kunti śōkākrānteyāgire tapōvanada tapōvr̥ddharākānteyanintendu santaisidar—

kaḻidavargaḻvudaḻtoḍavarēḻvoḍamantavariṁ baḻikke tā
muḻivoḍamēḻarantavaraṇaṁ tamagaṁ bardukilla dharmamaṁ

[p. 44]
gaḻiyisikoḷvudonde cadurintuṭu saṁskr̥ti dharmamēke bā
yaḻivudidēke cintisuvudēke palumbuvudēke nōvudō // ViVi.27 [campakamāle]

antumallade—

biḍadaḻalva bandhujanado
ḻkuḍiyada kaṇṇīra pūramā prētamanō
gaḍisade suḍuvudu gaḍami
nnuḍuguvudī śōkamaṁ sarōjadaḷākṣi // ViVi.28 [kandaṁ]

nīnintu śōkākrānteyāgi saṁsāra sthitiyanaṟiyadajñānigaḷante
vipraḷāpaṅgeydeyappoḍī kūsugaḷ manamikkiyumerdeyikkiyuṁ kiḍuvarendanē
kōpaśāntavacanaṅgaḷindamākeyubbegamanāṟe nuḍidumalliya munijanamellamā
kūsugaḷumaṁ kuntiyamaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu nāgapurakke vandu gāṅgēya
dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷgamambālegaṁ pāṇḍurājana vr̥tāntamanaṟipidoḍāgaḷ—

tuṟugida himabindugaḷiṁ
deṟagida nava vanajavanadavōl śōkadinaṁ
doṟeva nayanōdabinduvi
neṟagidudormodale bandhumukha vanajavanaṁ // ViVi.29 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ putra snēhadindati praḷāpaṅgeyvambāleyumaṁ bandhu jana
nirīkṣaṇadiṁ śōkaṁ maṟukaṇisebāyaḻidu paḷayisuva kuntiyumaṁ gāṅgēya
dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷumaṁ satyavatīdēviyumaṁ santaisi pāṇḍurājaṅge
jaḷadānādikriyegaḷaṁ nirvartisi tadanantaradoḷaduve nirvēgamāge vyāsavacana
doḷ satyavatiyumambikeyumambāleyuṁ saṁsāraviśīrṇeyarāgi munivanamanā
śrayisidaritta gāṅgēyanayvar kūsugaḷumaṁ tanna toḍeye toṭṭilāgi
naḍaputtamire duryōdhana prabhr̥tigaḷ nūrvaruṁ dharmaputrādigaḷayvaruṁ
sahapāṁsukrīḍitarāgi—

oḍanāḍiyumoḍanōdiyu
moḍavaḷeduṁ guḷḷegoṭṭi baṭṭuḷiseṇḍuṁ
poḍeseṇḍembivanāḍu
ttoḍavaḷedar tammoḷeḷase tantaṅgeḍegaḷ // ViVi.30 [kandaṁ]


[p. 45]
antā kūsugaḷ kūsāṭavāḍuttirdondu divasaṁ maragerasiyāḍalendu
munde tamma page parvuvantepannirmattarparvidālada marada modalge vandu
bhīmanaṁmaṟemāḍikōlanīḍāḍi palavu sūḻ kāḍi—

paridanibarumoḍanaḍardire
maranaṁ muṭṭalke paḍeyadanibargaṁ kiṁ
kirivōgi bhīmasēnaṁ
maranaṁ piḍidalgepaṇvolanibarumudirdar // ViVi.31 [kandaṁ]

antu biḻdu sulida moḻakālgaḷuṁ kaḻalda palgaḷumelvaḍagāda
meyguḷumuḍida keygaḷumāgi berasaḻuttuṁ bandu gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭrarge
kāraṇambēḻdoḍavarinditta bhīmanoḍanāḍadirimendu mudugaṇgal bārise tamma
nonda siggiṅganibarumondāgi pōgi poṟavoḻala marada keḷage maṟasondida
bhīmananaḍasi piḍidu nūrvaruṁ gaṇṭalaṁ meṭṭi—

pāvugaḷaṁ koḷisi mahā
grāvamanuṟadaḍasi kaṭṭi koraḷoḷ gaṅgā
dēviya maḍuvinoḷaḻdida
rāvarisade tamma kulamanaḍigaḻduvavōl // ViVi.32 [kandaṁ]

antaḻduvuduṁ gaṅgādēviya varaprasādadoḷ viṣama viṣadharaṅgaḷ
pariye koraloḷ toḍarda śileyaṁ paṟidīḍāḍi gaṅgeya nīraṁ tōḷoḷ
tuḷuṅki maguḻdu bandaṅge viṣada laḍḍugeyanikkiyumenitānumupadravaṅgaḷoḷ
toḍarikkiyuṁ gelalāṟade manamikkiyumerdeyikkiyumirdarantayvar kūsugaḷgaṁ
gāṅgēyaṁ caulōpanayanādi kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi sukhamirpannegamitta
gaṅgādvāradoḷ māyāpuramemba r̥ṣyāśramadoḷ gautamanembaṁ brahmar̥ṣi
tapaṅgeyyutirpinamā r̥ṣige billumambuṁverasorva magaṁ puṭṭidanātaṅge
śaradvatanendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍape baḷedu tapaṅgeyvātanallige jalakrīḍā
nimittadindindranaccarase jalacareyembavaḷ bandoḍākeyaṁ kaṇḍu kāmāsakta
cittanāgi kūḍi—


[p. 46]
ogeda śarastambadoḷi
rbagiyāgi manōja rāgarasamugutare to
ṭṭage bisuṭu billanambuma
nagaldanāśramadinudita lajjāvaśadiṁ // ViVi.33 [kandaṁ]

annegamā tapōvanakke bēṇṭeyāḍalbanda śantanuvinoḍaneyavarā
śarastambadoḷ parikalisirda munīndranindriyadoḷogeda peṇgūsumaṁ
gaṇḍugūsumanavaṟa keladoḷirda divya śarāsana śaraṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇḍu koṇḍupōgi
śantanuge tōṟidoḍātanumā śiśudvayamaṁ nija gajapurakkuydu kr̥peyiṁ
naḍapidanappudaṟiṁ kr̥panuṁ kr̥peyumendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍaputtirpannegamavarayyaṁ
śaradvatanallige bandu kiṟiyātaṅge caulōpanayanādi kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi
dhanurvidyōpadēśaṅgeyye sarva vidyā viśāradanādanā kr̥pācāryara pakkadoḷ
kūsugaḷaṁ vidyābhyāsaṅgeyse—

bareyade banda suddageyesūtramanonde muhūrtamātradiṁ
barisidudantu sūtrisida sūtradavr̥tti nijātmavr̥ttivōl
pariṇamisittu mattuḻida vidyegaḷōjarecaṭṭarembinaṁ
nereduvu tannoḷār gaḷaguṇārṇavanantukuśāgrabuddhigaḷ // ViVi.34 [campakamāle]

antu pañcāṅga vyākaraṇada vr̥ttibhēdamappachandovr̥ttiyoḷaṁ
śabdālaṅkāra niṣṭhitamappalaṅkāradoḷaṁ vyāsa vālmīki kaśyapa prabhr̥ti viracitaṅgaḷappa
mahākāvyaṅgaḷoḷaṁ nāndīparōca[nā]prastāvanētivr̥ttasandhi pravēśa
viṣkambha kapōtikā vyāḷikādi lakṣaṇōpētaṅgaḷappa nāṭakaṅgaḷoḷaṁ padineṇṭu
dharmaśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ nālku vēdadoḷamāṟaṅgadoḷamaydu teṟada
mantraṅgaḷoḷamāṟuṁdarśanadoḷaṁ pratyakṣānumāna pramāṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ bharata
praṇīta nr̥tyaśāstradoḷaṁnāradādi praṇīta gāndharvavidyāviśēṣaṅgaḷoḷaṁ
gajāgamajña rājaputra gautama vādvākipāḷa kaśyapasupatiśrīharṣādi purāṇa
puruṣaviracitaṅgaḷappahastiśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ citrakarma patracchēda graha gaṇita
[p. 47]
ratnaparīkṣegaḷoḷaṁ dārukarma vāstuvidyāpūrvayantraprayōgavi[ṣā]pa
haraṇasarabhēda ratitantēndrajāla vividha vidyegaḷoḷamanēkākṣara svarūpaṅgaḷoḷaṁ
cāpa cakra paraśu kr̥pāṇa śakti tōmara musala musuṇḍi bhiṇḍivāḷa mudgara
gadādi vividhāyudhaṅgaḷoḷamati pravīṇanumārūḍha sarvajña mahēndra
jāṇa(?)[nu]māgi —

uḷḷōdugaḷoḷagenitaṟi
vuḷḷargaṁtiḷipalariyadenipeḍegaḷumaṁ
teḷḷagiretiḷipuguṁ besa
goḷḷa guṇārṇavana lekkamaṁpokkamumaṁ // ViVi.35 [kandaṁ]

endu lōkamellaṁ pogaḻte negaḻda pogaḻtegaṁ negaḻgegaṁ tāne
guṟiyāgi—

mānasadoḷ haṁseyavōl
mānasavāgvanite tanna mānasadoḷivaṁ
mānasanendagalade nile
mānasanādaṁ sarasvatīkaḷahaṁsaṁ // ViVi.36 [kandaṁ]

antadayvaruṁ samasta śastra śāstra prayōga pravīṇarāge dharmaputraṁ
dharmaśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ śrutismr̥tigaḷoḷaṁ pravīṇanādaṁ bhīmasēnaṁ vyākaraṇa
doḷārindamaggaḷa[ṁ]kuśalanādaṁ nakulaṁ kunta śastradoḷati pravīṇanumāgi
aśvavidyeyoḷārindaṁ piriyanādaṁ sahadēvaṁ jyōtirjñānadoḷati pariṇatanādaṁ—

baḷeduvu tōḷgaḷekkeyinamaḷ baḷevantire muyvugaḷ kuḷā
caḷaśikharaṅgaḷaṁ masuḷevanduvu parvida vakṣamī kṣamā
taḷa kuḷalakṣmigāytu kuḷamandiramendu mahītaḷaṁ manaṁ
goḷe neṟedattudātta nava yauvanamormeye dharmaputranā // ViVi.37 [campakamāle]

antu sogayisuva rūpinoḷ ponna baṇṇadantappa tanna meyya
baṇṇamaḷavalladoppe—


[p. 48]
kuḷagiriyaṁ sarōjanilayaṁ manujākr̥tiyāge māḍidaṁ
toḷavenipantuṭappa posa baṇṇadoḷondida pārijātama
ggaḷamesedoppuvante taḷiriṁ muguḷiṁ navayauvanaṁ manaṁ
goḷe karamoppidaṁ daśa sahasra madēbha baḷaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ // ViVi.38 [campakamāle]

antoppuva gaṇḍa gāḍiyoḷindra nīladantappa baṇṇaṁ kaṇgevare—

śaradada candranaṁ vimala candrike bāḷadinēśanaṁ tamō
harakiraṇaṁ kiśōra hariyaṁ navakēsara rāji mikka di
kkariyananūna dāna pariśōbhe manaṅgoḷe porduvante suṁ
dara navayauvanaṁ neṟeye porde guṇārṇavanoppi tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.39 [campakamāle]

antu navayauvanaṁ neṟeye neṟeye niṟi niṟigoṇḍa guṇārṇavana
talenavirgaḷ lāvaṇyarasamaniḍidiḍidu tivida kamalāsanana beralaccugaḷannavāduvu
mūṟuṁ lōkada mūṟu paṭṭamanāḷalke takka lakṣaṇa sampūrṇamappa sahaja
manōjana lalāṭa[ṁ]paṭṭaṅgaṭṭida nosalge lakṣaṇamanaṟasalvēḍembantādudu karbina
billa koṅkinante koṅkiyuṁ paravaniteyarerdege koṅkilladeyuṁ sogayisuva
surata makaradhvajana parvugaḷ kāmadēvana vijaya vaijayantigaḷantāduvu nīḷpaṁ
beḷpumaṁ tāḷdi paravaniteyara desege kisugaṇcidante kisu serevaridu sogayisuva
śaucāñjanēyana kaṇgaḷembaralambugaḷ gaṇikājanaṅgaḷerdeyaṁ naṭṭu keṅkamādaṁ
tāduvu ripujanada perciṅgaṁ parāṅganā janadamecciṅgaṁ mūgiṟivante
sogayisuva gandhēbha vidyādharana mūgu tanna suyya kampanallade peṟara
kampanāsevaḍadantādudu posa javvanada mumbaṇṇadantekarpaṁkaikoṇḍu
katturiyalbaredantappa vikrānta tuṅgana mīsegaḷātana tīvra pratāpānaḷa
dhūmalēkheyantāduvu puḷiyoḷaleda pavaḷada baṭṭinante sogayisuva
saṁsārasārōdayana bimbādharamanaṅgarāgarasa duruḷiyantādudu rasadāḍimadabittumaṁ posa muttumaṁ mukkuḷisidantappa vibudhavanajavana kaḷahaṁsana
dantapaṅktigaḷamr̥takiraṇana kāntigaḷaniḷisuvantāduvu maḍidu tandiṭṭa posaneydila
kāvanāvagaṁ gelda ratnakuṇḍalaṅgaḷa poḷapanoḷakoṇḍante nasunēlva karṇāṭī
[p. 49]
karṇapūranapālegaḷuṁ sarasvatiyāḍuva līlāndōḷadantāduvu baḷvaḷa
beḷedeḷagauṅginante lōkada celvellamanoḷakoṇḍu rēkhegoṇḍa lāṭīlalāmana
pariṇaddha kandharaṁ yuvarāja kaṇṭhikābharaṇamaṁ kaṭṭuvudarke nōntu tanna celvanallade
peṟara celvanāsevaḍadantādudu kulada calada maimeyoḷ tannane nōḍida
santōṣadoḷutsāhamādante sogayisuva samaraikamēruvina bhujaśikharaṅgaḷ
kula śikhariśikharaṅgaḷantāduvu vyāḷagajaṅgaḷumanaṅkada bardeyarumanugibagi
māḍida santōṣadoḷ baḷvaḷa baḷeda vikrāntatuṅgana niḍudōḷgaḷ gaṇikājanakke
kāmapāśaṅgaḷumarātijanakke yamapāśaṅgaḷumāduvu raktāśōka pallavadante
toḷatoḷaguvāndhrī kucakalaśa pallavana karataḷapallavaṅgaḷ samada gajakumbha
sthaḷāsphāḷana karkaśaṅgaḷāduvu poḍarva pagevaranuṟadekoṇḍasantōṣadoḷaṁ
śrīyanoḷakoṇḍa santōṣadoḷaṁ tekkane tīvida kēraḷīkēḷi kandarpanagaluraṁ
lakṣmige kulabhavanamuṁ nivāsabhavanamumādudu poḍarva maṇḍaḷikara manadante
karamasidāda parākramadhavaḷana madhyapradēśaṁ nārāyaṇaṁ tannāḷdaṁ māḍi
tānāḷmāḍiyuṁ tānaḷḷāḍeyuṁ bardeyara manavanaḷḷāḍisuvantādudu
gambhīraguṇadoḷamāvartana siddhiyoḷaṁ jaḷanidhiyane pōlva śaraṇāgata jaḷanidhiya
nimna nābhi celviṅge tāne nābhiyādudu siṁha kaṭitaṭamaniḷisuva ripukuraṅga
kaṇṭhīravana kaṭitaṭamoldu nōḍuva gāḍikārtiyara kaṇge kāmanaḍḍaṇadante
doḍḍittāgi mīṟuvudvr̥tta vr̥ttateyanīḻdukoṇḍantudvr̥ttaṅgaḷāduvu
udāttanārāyaṇanūru yugmaṅgaḷ māniniyara manōgajaṅgaḷaṁ kaṭṭalkālāna
stambhaṅgaḷāduvu antapūrvaṅgaḷāgi toḷaguva kiṟudoḍegaḷuḍuvaḍardannamārūḍha
sarvajñana doḍḍamārgaṅgaḷeḷavāḻeyadiṇḍinoḷ sāṇegaṭṭidantāduvu
gū[ḍha]gulphapārṣṇigaḷanoḷakoṇḍa manujamāndhātana poṟa aḍigaḷ virōdhi
bhūpāḷaranaḍigeṟagisida santōṣadoḷunnataṅgaḷādante kūrmōnnataṅgaḷāduvu
nosalaṁ suṭṭi tōrpannavappuṅguṭaṅgaḷoḷ miñcaṁ kīlisidante toḷagi poḷeva
pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana pādanakhaṅgaḷ gaṇḍara peṇḍirañjidaḷkida mogamaṁ nōḍalke
kannaḍigaḷannavāduvu posatalarda kendāvareya kempumaṁmelpumaniḻkuḷigoṇḍu
[p. 50]
toḷaguvarikēsariya pādataḷaṅgaḷaḍigeṟagidari narapālara makuṭamāṇikyamarīcijāla
bāḷātapaṅgaḷanaledu keṅkamādantāduvu posavesaṟageya baṇṇadante sogayisuva
sāmanta cūḍāmaṇiya meyya baṇṇaṁ vidhātranemba cittāriya varṇakramaṅgeyda
kadaḷīgarbhaśyāmamemba baṇṇadantādudu—

manadoḷoṟaldu jōldaḷipi nōḍaloḍaṁ seṟegeydu kaṇṇumaṁ
manamumanaṅgajanmaralambugaḷiṁdemaruḷci banda mā
vina banadoḷ teraḷci poḷevindumarīcigaḷinduruḷci pū
vina paseyoḷ poraḷcidanaḷurkeya bardeyaraṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.40 [campakamāle]

antu nakula sahadēvar sahitamayvaruṁ navayauvanada paramasukhamaneydi
santōṣadinirdaritta gaṅgādvāradoḷ bharadvājanemba brahmar̥ṣi—

snānārthamondu kaḷaśama
nā niyama nidhānaneḻale piḍidamaḷina gaṁ
gānadige vandu surata ni
dhāniyanamarēndragaṇikeyaṁ muni kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.41 [kandaṁ]

antu kāṇbudumamr̥tābdhiyembaccaraseya kanakakāñcīkaḷāpadoḷ
toḍarda dēvāṅga vastraduḷḷuḍeyoḷuliva sūsakadanūlatoṅgalveraseḻalva mundaṇa
sōge kārgālada sōgeyante sogayise—

ādelara sōṅkinoḷ teṟa
pādoḍe beḷpeseye maseda madanana bāḷaṁ
tāduvu poḷevoḷdoḍeteṟa
pāderdeyaṁ naṭṭuvandutanmunipatiyā // ViVi.42 [kandaṁ]

antu kantuśaraparavaśanāgi dhairya kṣaraṇeyumindriya kṣaraṇeyu
moḍanoḍanāge—

māṇade sōrvindriyamaṁ
drōṇadoḷāntalliyogeda śiśuvaṁ kaṇḍī

[p. 51]
drōṇadoḷe puṭṭidītaṁ
drōṇane pōgendu pesaraniṭṭaṁ munipaṁ // ViVi.43 [kandaṁ]

antu bharadvājanātmatanūjaṅge pesaraniṭṭu tanna keḷeyaṁ pāñcāḷa
dēśadarasaṁ pr̥ṣatanembanātana magaṁ drupadanumaṁ drōṇanumanoḍagūḍi
yajñasēnanemba brahmar̥ṣiya pakkadoḷ bilviddeyaṁ kalalvēḻdoḍe drōṇanuṁ
drupadanuṁ dhanurdharāgragaṇyarāge bharadvājaṁ drōṇaṅge kr̥pana taṅgeyappa
śāradvateyaṁ tandu maduveyaṁ māḍidoḍātaṅgamākegaṁ triṇētranaṁśadoḷorva
magaṁ puṭṭi—

divijāśvatthāmadoḷī
bhuvanaṅgaḷ naḍuge śiśu saraṅgeydoḍe na
kkavayavade kumbhasambhava
nivanaśvatthāmanendu pesariḍe negaḻdaṁ // ViVi.44 [kandaṁ]

antu negaḻdu tammayyana kaiyoḷ dhanurvidyōpadēśadoḷ
dhanurdharāgragaṇyanumāgi sanda[ṁ]drupadanuṁ tanna rājyadoḷ ninda[ṁ]drōṇanuṁ
tanage baḍatanamaḍase aśvatthāmananoḍagoṇḍu nāḍu nāḍaṁ toḻaldu
paraśurāmanallige vandaṁ—

kṣitiyoḷaguḷḷa bhūbhujara bittu modalgiḍe munnamēkaviṁ
śati parisaṅkhyeyiṁ tavisi sarvanivēdakamemba yajñadoḷ
kṣiti pogaḻvannamittu gurudakṣiṇeyāgire kaśyapa prajā
patige samudra mudrita dharitriyanondaḻiyūranīvavol // ViVi.45 [campakamāle]

antu valkalāvr̥ta kaṭitaṭanumāgirdajaṭākalāpanumāgi tapōvanakke
pōpa bhārgavaṁ dravyārthiyāgi banda kumbhasambhavanaṁ kaṇḍu kanakapātrakkupāya
millappudaṟiṁ mr̥tpātradoḷarghyamettipūjisi—

oḍameyanarthigittenavanītaḷamaṁ gurugittenīgaḷoṁ
daḍakeyumilla kaiyoḷeredaṁ śrutapāraganentu santasaṁ
baḍisuveninnidondu dhanuvirdudu divyaśarāḷiyirdudi
lloḍame samantu pēḻivaṟoḷāvudanīvudo kumbhasambhavā // ViVi.46 [campakamāle]


[p. 52]
embuduṁ drōṇanenage vidyādhaname dhanamappudaṟiṁ divyāstraṅgaḷaṁ
dayegeyvudene vāruṇa vāyavyāgnēyapaurandarādi pradhānāstraṅgaḷaṁ kuḍe
koṇḍu paraśurāmanaṁ bīḻkoḍu tannoḍanāḍiyappa keḷeyaṁ drupadaṁ
chatrāvatiyoḷarasugeydapanendu kēḷdā poḻalge vandu drupadanaramaneya
bāgiloḷ nindu paḍiyaṟanaṁ karedu nimmoḍanāḍida keḷeyaṁ drōṇanemba pārvaṁ
bandanendu nimmarasaṅgaṟiye pēḻembudumātanā māḻkeyoḷe bandaṟipuvuduṁ
drupadaṁ rājyamadirāmadōnmattanuṁ garvagrahavyagracittanumāgi mēgillade—

antembanārge piriduṁ
bhrāntu dalēṁ drōṇanembanēṁ pārvane pē
ḻentenage keḷeyanē nūṁ
kantappananaṟiyenendu sabheyoḷ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.47 [kandaṁ]

antu nuḍidudaṁ paḍiyaṟaṁ bandāmāḻkeyoḷaṟipe drōṇa
nottambadindoḷagaṁ pokku drupadanaṁ kaṇḍu—

aṟiyire nīmumāmumoḍanōdidevembudanaṇṇa ninnanā
naṟiyenadelli kaṇḍeyo mahīpatigaṁ dvijavaṁśajaṅgamē
taṟa keḷeyintu nāṇiligarappare mānasaremba mātugaḷ
neṟagoḷe kumbhasambhavananā drupadaṁ kaḍu siggu māḍidaṁ // ViVi.48 [campakamāle]

antu māḍidudumalladī nāṇili pārvananeḻedu kaḷeyimembuduṁ
drōṇanintendaṁ—

nuḍi taḍavappudondu mogadoḷ maṟukaṁ dorekoḷvudondu nā
ṇgeḍeguḍadirpudondu nuḍigaḷ moṟeyaṁ maṟeyippudondu ka
ḷguḍidavarandamintu siri sārtaresārvudadarke sandeyaṁ
baḍade jalakkanīgaḷaṟideṁ siri kaḷḷoḍavuṭṭitembudaṁ // ViVi.49 [campakamāle]

endu sairisade—


[p. 53]
khaḷa noḷaviṅgekuppevaramembavolāmbaramuṇṭe ninnadoṁ
daḷavoḍanōdidondu beragiṅge kolalkenagāgadī sabhā
vaḷayadoḷennanēḻisida ninnananākuḷamenna caṭṭariṁ
taḷaveḷagāge kaṭṭisade māṇdoḍe kemma[ne]mīsevottenē // ViVi.50 [campakamāle]

endārūḍhapratijñanāgi nāgapurakke vandu tamma bhāvaṁ kr̥pana maneyoḷa
pagatapariśramanāgirdondu divasaṁ pāṇḍavaruṁ kauravaruṁ poṟavoḻaloḷ—

neredisutiretōlvulleya
niradadu biḻdoḍe purāṇa kūpadoḷadani
nnaridu tegevandamendava
rire baḷasiyumalli kaṇḍu nakkaṁ drōṇaṁ // ViVi.51 [kandaṁ]

bharatakuḷatiḷakarir‌ vara
śarāsana vyagrahastarir‌ baḷayutarir
neredinibarumī lakṣyama
niradakkaṭa sarade tegeyalārtirumillā // ViVi.52 [kandaṁ]

endu tanna maganappaśvatthāmanaṁ karedī lakṣyamaṁ tegeyembudu
mātanantegeyvenendu naiṣṭhikamemba muṣṭiyoḷaṁ puṅkhānupuṅkhamemba śara
sandhānadoḷavayavadoḷe tegedoḍanibaruṁ cōdyambaṭṭu gāṅgēya
dhr̥tarāṣṭrargaṟipidoḍe nadītanūjaṁ bhāradvājaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi pūrva
sambhāṣaṇārghyametti madhuparka vētrāsana tāmbūla dānādigaḷiṁ santasaṁ baḍisi
tadīya kula vidyāvr̥ttigaḷaṁ besagoṇḍu—

madamaṁ mukkuḷisirdibhaṅgaḷanudagrāśvaṅgaḷaṁ takkina
ggada bāḍaṅgaḷanāydu koṭṭu taṇideṁ pō sālgumembannamaṁ
didiroḷ nūṟaṟuvar kumārarumaniṭṭī kūsugaḷ yōgyara
ppudaninnolvoḍe śastravidyegovajaṁ nīnāgu kumbhōdbhavā // ViVi.53 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embudumantegeyvenendu kalaśajananibara mogamaṁ nōḍi—


[p. 54]
ī neredinibarumenduda
nēnīvire pēḻimendoḍanibarumirdar
maunavratade guṇārṇava
nānīveṁ nimma bayasi bēḻpudanendaṁ // ViVi.54 [kandaṁ]

embudumā mātiṅge mecci jagadēkamallanaṁ toḍeyanēṟisikoṇḍu
kumbhasambhavaṁ gāṅgēyananintendaṁ—

inibaroḷagītanorvane
dhanurāgamadeḍege kuśalanakkumadarkēṁ
kinisadiriṁ munnaṟipide
nene bhīṣmanalampu mige muguḷnage nakkaṁ // ViVi.55 [kandaṁ]

antu drōṇācāryanācāryapadaviyaṁ kaikoṇḍu pāṇḍava kauravarge
caturaṅga dhanurvēdamumaṁ divyāstraṅgaḷumaṁ śakti tōmara musala musuṇḍi
bhiṇḍivāḷa mudgara gadādi vividhāyudhaṅgaḷumaṁ gaja ratha turaga padāti
yuddhaṅgaḷumanupadēśaṁ geyyuttumireyire—

yādava vaṁśajaruṁ nā
nā dēśa narēndraruṁ ghaṭōdbhavana dhanu
rvēdamane kalal bandā
ḷādar vidyāprabhāvamā dorete valaṁ // ViVi.56 [kandaṁ]

drōṇaṁ gaḍamiṣuvidyege
jāṇaṁ gaḍamendu kēḷdu kauravargellaṁ
prāṇaṁ barpākr̥tiyoḷe
bāṇāsana bāṇapāṇi karṇaṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

antu bandu vairigajaghaṭāvighaṭananoḷ vighaṭisi bilgaltu—

keḷeyuṁ guṟiyuṁ goṭṭiyu
maḷavige piridāge tanage duryōdhananoḷ
muḷisuṁ nōvuṁ kaluṣamu
muḷumbamene tanagarātikāḷānaḷanoḷ // ViVi.58 [kandaṁ]


[p. 55]
antu karṇaṁ guṇārṇavanoḷ seṇasi pageyanabhyāsaṅgeyvante
vidyābhyāsaṅgeyye—

manadoḷogedanyajanmada
munisadu kaṇṇiṁ tuḷuṅke sairisadavanu
rvina kalitanakke duryō
dhananuṁ bhīmanoḷe seṇasi gadeyaṁ kaltaṁ // ViVi.59 [kandaṁ]

antu bhāradvājanāgāmika saṅgrāmaraṅgakke pātraṅgaḷaṁ sameyisuva
sūtradhāranante śastravidyābhyāsaṁ geysuttire dēśādhīśvararappa palambar‌
rājakumārara naḍuve tārāgaṇaṅgaḷa naḍuvaṇa sakaḷa kaḷādharanante śastrakaḷādharanāgi
tannumaṁ gelevanda sāmanta cūḍāmaṇiya śarapariṇatiyanārayalendu—

chāyā lakṣyamanoḍḍiyu
māyada nīroḷage tannanaḍasida negaḻaṁ
bāyaḻivinamisisiyumare
hōyaja bāppendu hariganaṁ guru pogaḻdaṁ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]

antu pogaḻdu tanna pagevanappa drupadananītanamōghaṁ gelal neṟegumendu
niścaisi—

aṇuginoḷenna caṭṭaroḷagītane jeṭṭiganendu viddeyaṁ
guṇakaṟugoṇḍu koṭṭenage santasamappinamīva ninna da
kṣiṇeyadu bēgamā drupadanaṁ gaḍa kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi taṁ
daṇiyaramoppisintidane bēḍidenāṁ parasainyabhairavā // ViVi.61 [campakamāle]

embudamī besanadāvudu gahanamendu pūṇdu pōgi—

oḍavandaṅkada kauravar drupadanambēṟiṅge meyyoḍḍado
ḍḍoḍedōḍuttire sūse bīḻva talegaḷsūḻpaṭṭanāgaḷ javaṁ
piḍidīḍāḍuva māḻkeyante palaraṁ kondikki meymuṭṭevaṁ
deḍeyoḷ māṇaduruḷci kaṭṭi ripuvaṁ mundikkidaṁ drōṇanā // ViVi.62 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷā kumbhasambhavaṁ parākramadhavaḷana parākramakke mecci kadampaṁ karci
drupadanaṁ tanna mañcada kāloḷ kaṭṭavēḻdu taleya mēle kālanavaṣṭambhadiṁ nīḍi—


[p. 56]
sirimeyyoḷagandaṟivire
neraviyoḷāraṟivarorme kaṇḍaranaṟiya
lkaridemmaṁ baḍapārvara
narasare nīmīgaḷaṟiviraṟiyiro pēḻiṁ // ViVi.63 [kandaṁ]

endu sāye sarasaṁ nuḍidu mattamintendaṁ—

ādi kṣatriyarē nī
mādityananiḷipa tējarirpārvana kāl
mōde naḍutaleyalirpudu
mādudu nimagendu nuḍidu kāypinoḷodedaṁ // ViVi.64 [kandaṁ]

odedu ninnaninitu paribhavambaḍisidudu sālguṁ ninnaṁ kolalāgadu
kondoḍe mēlappa pagegañji kondantāgirkumendu kaṭṭida kaṭṭugaḷellamaṁ tāne
biṭṭu kaḷedu pōgembuduṁ drupadaṁ paribhavānaḷanaḷavalladaḷure ninnaṁ kolvanna
norva maganumaṁ vikramārjunaṅge peṇḍatiyappannaḷorva magaḷumaṁ paḍedalladire
nendu mahā pratijñārūḍhanāgi pōdanitta bhāradvājaṁ pāṇḍava kauravarkaḷa meyyoḷe
viddeyaṁ neṟeye saṅkramisida tanna vidyāmahimeyaṁ meṟeyalke bāhlīka
bhūriśravassōma datta gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷgintendaṁ—

neṟeye dhanurvidyeya ka
ṇdeṟevinegaṁ kaltanimma makkaḷa meyyoḷ
meṟedappenenna viddeya
naṟidoykane neredu nōḻpudanibarumīgaḷ // ViVi.65 [kandaṁ]

endoḍantegeyvamendanibarumoḍambaṭṭu poṟavoḻaloḷuttara
diśābhāgadoḷ sama caturasramāge nelananaḷedu kallaṁ pullumaṁ sōdisi śubhadina
śubhamuhūrtadoḷ—

gaṭṭisi sindhuradoḷ nela
gaṭṭisi cembonna neleya caupaḷigegaḷoḷ
kaṭṭisi paḻayigegaḷanaḷa
vaṭṭire biyamalli moḻage palavuṁ paṟegaḷ // ViVi.66 [kandaṁ]


[p. 57]
antu sameda vyāyāma raṅgakke gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidura sōmadatta
bāhlīka bhūriśravādi kulavr̥ddharuṁ kunti gāndhārigaḷuṁverasu bandu kuḷḷire—

arasiyaranaṇugaraṁ bē
ḻparumaṁmonegāṟaraṁ pragītaranimbā
gire caupaḷigegaḷoḷ ku
ḷḷirisidaroḍaneseye nereda purajana sahitaṁ // ViVi.67 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ kumbhasambhavaṁ—

posa muttina tuḍige poda
ḻdeseye dukūlāmbaraṁ nijāṅgadoḷ saṁ
desedire beḷmugilindaṁ
musukida nīlādri barpa teṟadoḷ bandaṁ // ViVi.68 [kandaṁ]

antu bandu raṅgabhūmiya naḍuve nindu—

negaḻdire puṇyāha svara
mogedire paṭu paṭaha kāhaḷā ravavāgaḷ
pugavēḻdaṁ vividhāstra
pragalbharaṁ tanna caṭṭaraṁ kaḷaśabhavaṁ // ViVi.69 [kandaṁ]

antu pugavēḻvuduṁ di
gdantigaḷuṁ kulanagaṅgaḷuṁ gaḍaṇaṅgoṁ
ḍentu kavitarkamante ne
laṁ taḷarvinegaṁ pracaṇḍa kōdaṇḍadharar // ViVi.70 [kandaṁ]

antu dharmaputranaṁ muntiṭṭu bhīmārjuna nakula sahadēvaruṁ
duryōdhananaṁ muntiṭṭu yuyutsu duśyāsana dussaha dussaḷa jarāsandha satyasandha
nissaharājasandha vinda anuvinda durmati subāhu dusparśana durmarṣaṇa
durmukha duṣkarṇa vikarṇa viviṁśati sulōcana sunābha citra upacitra nanda
upananda sucitrāṅgada citrakuṇḍala suhasta dr̥ḍhahasta pramāthi dīrghabāhu
mahābāhu pratima supratima sapramāthi durdharṣaṇa duṣparājaya mitra upamitra
cauḷōpa dvandvahasta pratīpa supratīpa prahasta pratāpa pramada sadbāhugaḷ
modalāgi nūrvaruṁ bandu—


[p. 58]
gadeyoḷ billoḷ gajadoḷ
kudureyoḷaṁrathadoḷastrakauśalade beḍaṁ
godaviretōṟidaravaro
rmodale janaṁ pogaḻe negaḻe jaḷanidhi ninadaṁ // ViVi.71 [kandaṁ]

antavariṁ baḻiyaṁ—

āda muḷisindamāgaḷ
mōduva bage baḷeye piḍida gadegaḷinipaṁ
tādudu suyōdhanōgra vr̥
kōdararormodale śikharamuḷḷeraḍagamaṁ // ViVi.72 [kandaṁ]

antirvarumorvarorvaroḷ seṇasi bahuprayōga gadā kauśalamaṁ
tōṟalendu—

geḍevaccirvar managoṁ
ḍoḍanoḍanōrantu taguḷdu jhēṅkarisidoḍe
lvaḍagāge mōdalendi
rdeḍeyoḷ guru tanna magananeḍevugavēḻdaṁ // ViVi.73 [kandaṁ]

antu mēredappal bageda mahāsamudraṅgaḷeraḍaṟa naḍuve
kulagiriyirpantirdaśvatthāmanaṁ kaṇḍirvarumeraḍuṁ desege tolagi nindāgaḷ—

ā dūrvāṅkura varṇado
ḷādamoḍambaṭṭa kanaka kavacaṁ rāja
tkōdaṇḍamamarda doṇe ka
ṇgādame bare bandu munde nindaṁ harigaṁ // ViVi.74 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ kumbhasambhavanuliva janada kaḷakaḷa ravamumaṁ moḻaguva
paṟegaḷumaṁ bārisi—

ītaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ vi
khyāta yaśaṁ vairigajaghaṭāvighaṭananiṁ
tītana sāhasamupamā
tītamidaṁ nōḍimendu neravige nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.75 [kandaṁ]


[p. 59]
ā prastāvadoḷ—

oḍegumajāṇḍaminninisu jēvoḍedāgaḷe bommanuṁ manaṁ
giḍugumadēvudendu miḍidoyyane jēvoḍedāgaḷambanaṁ
[bo]ḍanoḍanīmbuvembanitu sandeyamappinamastra jāladiṁ
taḍeyade pañjarambaḍedanandu viyattaḷadoḷ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.76 [campakamāle]

mattamaindra vāruṇa vāyavyāgnēya pārvatādi bāṇaṅgaḷaṁ tuḍe—

kaviduvu kāḷa nīḷa jaḷadāvaḷi vāridhigaḷ dharitriyaṁ
kaviduvu gāḷigaḷ praḷayakālamanāgisalende lōkamaṁ
kaviduvu mokkaḷaṁ kaviduvugra layāgnigaḷante beṭṭugaḷ
kaviduvivembanittu bhayamāytu guṇārṇavanastrakauśalaṁ // ViVi.77 [campakamāle]

āgaḷā parākramadhavaḷana śarapariṇatiyaṁ kaṇḍu duryōdhanana mogaṁ
talenavira gaṇṭiṁ kiṟidāge drōṇa bhīṣma kr̥pa vidura prabhr̥tigaḷa mogamaralda
tāvareyiṁ piridāge—

toḷaguva tējaṁtoḷatoḷa
toḷaguva divyāstramamarda kōdaṇḍamasuṁ
goḷisemanaṅgoḷise bhayaṁ
goḷisesabhāsadaranuṟade karṇaṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.78 [kandaṁ]

bandu drōṇācāryaṅge poḍamaṭṭu śaradhiyiṁ divyāstraṅgaḷa
nurcikoṇḍu—

arigana bilbalmayoḷaṁ
deraḍillade bagedamuḷisumēvamumerdeyoḷ
barediretōṟidanāyata
karaparighaṁkarṇanātma śarapariṇitiyaṁ // ViVi.79 [kandaṁ]


[p. 60]
antu tōṟeyumerdeya muḷisu nālagege vare sairisalāṟade vidviṣṭa
vidrāvaṇananintendaṁ—

saṅgatadinīgaḷintī
raṅgame raṇaraṅgamāge kāduvamaḷavaṁ
poṁgadiridircadēṁ gaḷa
raṅgambokkāḍuvante peṇḍire gaṇḍar // ViVi.80 [kandaṁ]

embudumatirathamathananintendaṁ—

ī nereda gurujanaṅgaḷa
māniniyara munde karṇa polladu nuḍidai
nīnennī niḍudōḷgaḷa
tīnaṁ maḻgisuveyappoḍānolladanē // ViVi.81 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ drōṇanuṁ kr̥panumeḍege vandu karṇananintendar—

ēvada muḷisina kāraṇa
māvudo nīṁ ninna tāya tandeya deseyaṁ
bhāvisade karṇa nuḍivaṁ
tāvudu samakaṭṭu ninagamarikēsarigaṁ // ViVi.82 [kandaṁ]

embudumā mātiṅge maṟuvātuguḍalaṟiyade pandeyaṁ
pāvaḍardantummane bemaruttumirda karṇanaṁ duryōdhanaṁkaṇḍudrōṇanumaṁ
kr̥panumanintendaṁ—

kulamembuduṇṭe bīrame
kulamallade kulamanintu pikkadiriṁ nī
molidelli puṭṭi baḷediro
kulamirdude koḍadoḷaṁ śarastambadoḷaṁ // ViVi.83 [kandaṁ]

endu nuḍidu karṇananīgaḷe kulajanaṁ māḍi tōrpenendu keyyaṁ
piḍidoḍagoṇḍu pōgi kanakapīṭhada mēle kuḷḷirisi kanaka kaḷaśadaltīvidagaṇyapuṇya
tīrthōdakaṅgaḷaṁ caturvēdapāragarindabhiṣēkaṅgeysi—


[p. 61]
maṅgaḷavaṟegaḷ śubha vaca
naṅgaḷ camarīruhaṅgaḷā śvētaccha
traṅgaḷamardeseye karṇaṁ
gaṅgamahītaḷa vibhūtiyaṁ neṟeyittaṁ // ViVi.84 [kandaṁ]

antittu nityadānakke dēva sabaḷada padineṇṭu kōṭi ponnumanittu
nīnenagondanīyalvēḻpudendu—

poḍamaḍuvar jīyembar
kuḍu dayegeyyēṁ prasādamembivu peṟaroḷ
naḍegemma ninnayeḍeyoḷ
naḍeyalvēḍenage keḷeyanai rādhēyā // ViVi.85 [kandaṁ]

endu bēḍikoṇḍu karṇanaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu pōgi dhr̥tarāṣṭraṅgaṁ
gāndhārigaṁ poḍamaḍisidāgaḷ—

intu suyōdhanaṁ ninage māḍida rājya vibhūtigunte mu
yvāntiradir guṇārṇavaninastamayakkidu sālgamīgaḷeṁ
bantevolandu mundaṟidu tanna magaṅge samantu buddhivē
ḻvantevo[latta]lastagiriyaṁmaṟegoṇḍudu sūrya maṇḍalaṁ // ViVi.86 [utpalamālike]

āgaḷ duryōdhananaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu dhr̥tarāṣṭra karṇa śalya śakuni
saindhava prabhr̥tigaḷ nelaṁ mūriviṭṭantesabhākṣōbhamāge taḷerdu nānā vidha
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi nija nivāsaṅgaḷge pōdaritta dharmaputranaṁ mundiṭṭu bhīmārjuna
nakula sahadēvaruṁ gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidura prabhr̥tigaḷ nānā vidha
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi bare purajanaṅgaḷellamōrōrvarane piḍiyaccuviḍidu nuḍiye
kelaranāgatamanaṟiva buddhiyoḍeyarintembar—


[p. 62]
avarivarannarinnarenavēḍarikēsarigāmpanilla mī
ṟuva taledōrpa gaṇḍaraṇamilleḍeyoḷ geḍevaccugoṇḍu pāṁ
ḍavaranakāraṇaṁ keṇakidī posa poḻtaṟoḷāda kircu kau
ravargidu nāḍeyuṁ tiṇukanāgisadēṁ gaḷa saytu pōkumē // ViVi.87 [campakamāle]

endorvarorvarondondane nuḍiyuttuṁ pōge beḷaguva kaidīvigegaḷ
kaḻtaleyaṁ taledōṟalīyade pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana tējōṅkuraṅgaḷ beḷaguvante
beḷage pāṇḍavar nijanivāsakke pōdarāgaḷ—

eseva nijavaṁśamaṁ pe
rcisuva guṇārṇavanoḷunte seṇasalkendi
rpa suyōdhanaṅgemuḷisiṁ
kisugaṇcidateṟadinamr̥takaranudayisidaṁ // ViVi.88 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ duryōdhanaṁ bhīmasēnana ballāḷtanadaḷavumaṁ vikramārjunana
divyāstra kauśaḷamumaṁ kaṇḍu tannerdeyuṁ poḷḷumaranaṁ kircaḷurvantoḷagoḷa
gaḷure sairisalāṟade karṇanaṁ karedāḷōcisi tammayyanallige pōgi poḍamaṭṭu
kaṭṭēkāntadoḷintendaṁ—

piriyar‌ nīmire pāṇḍurājane valaṁ muṁ paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭe bhū
bharamaṁ tāḷdidanīgaḷātana sutar tāmāgaḷē yōgyarā
gare paṭṭakke taguḷdu pālaneṟevir pāviṅge dāyādyaraṁ
piriyarmāḍidiremma sāvumuḻivuṁ daivēccheyāytāgadē // ViVi.89 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

adalladeyuṁ—

male taledōṟadendudanekoṭṭudaḍaṅgamaḍaṅgi bandoḍo
kkaligavesarge pūṇdudu kuṟumbu taṟumbade mikka śatru maṁ
ḍaḷikare mitramaṇḍaḷikarādaranākuḷamindu nāḷe mā
rmaledaranikki nammaneḻedikkugumī neleyiṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.90 [campakamāle]

antu vikramārjunaṁ bilgoḷaluṁ bhīmasēnaṁ gadegoḷalu
māmpudaridupāṁśuvadhade keyge māḍuvuduttamapakṣamantumalladeyuṁ—


[p. 63]
svāmyārtha svāmya vikrāntaṁ marmajñaṁ vyavasāyinaṁ
ardharājyaharaṁ bhr̥tyaṁ yō na hanyātsa hanyatē // ViVi.90 [anuṣṭubh]

embudarthaśāstra sadbhāvaṁ—

mēṇkulamilleyō namage dāyigarallarośastravidyeyoḷ
pūṇkegaḷilleyō dharege munnavarayyane mukhyanallanō
jāṇkiṟidāgavēḍa manadal nimagayya vidhātr̥yōgadiṁ
kaṇkuruḍādoḍēno kuruḍāgalevēḻpude nimma buddhiyuṁ // ViVi.91 [utpalamālike]

endu tanna manadoḷoḍambaḍe nuḍida magana mātaṁ dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ
manadegoṇḍu—

ēnerdegoṇḍa kajjamane pēḻdeyō cintisutirpenānumē
nānumupāyamaṁ bagevarantavargaḷ ninagende kanda pēḻ
nīnire paṭṭamuṁ nelanumappudanolvene vairigaḷge nī
nēnumadarke cintisadirilliralīvene pāṇḍuputraraṁ // ViVi.92 [utpalamālike]

endu duryōdhananaṁ bīḍiṅge pōgalvēḻdu pāṇḍavarayvarumaṁ barisi
dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ toḍeyanēṟisikoṇḍu duryōdhananappoḍe pollamānasanātanuṁ
nīmumondeḍeyoḷire kisuṟuṁ kalahamumenduṁ kundadadukāraṇaṁ gaṅgānadiya
dakṣiṇa taṭadoḷ vāraṇāvatamembudu poḻal kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayakke tiḷakamappaṁ
tirdudallige pōgi sukhamirimendoḍantegeyvemendu bīḻkoṇḍu bīḍiṅgevandu
gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidurarkaḷgaṁ kuntigaṁ tadvr̥ttāntamanaṟipidarannegamitta
duryōdhananavara pōganaṟidu purōcananemba tanna manadannanappa pergaḍeyoḷ
lākṣāgr̥hōpāyamaṁ carcisi vāraṇāvatamanondē divasadoḷeydu vantāge
rathamaṁ samakaṭṭi nālku lakka balamaṁ nerambēḻdu kaḷipidanāgaḷ—

uditōditanai nīṁ nina
gudayadamēludayamendu negaḻdarigaṅga
bhyudayamanaṟipuva teṟadiṁ
dudayācaḷa cumbi bimbaninanudayisidaṁ // ViVi.93 [kandaṁ]


[p. 64]
ā prastāvadoḷ maṅgaḷa pāṭhakara maṅgaḷa vr̥ttōccāraṇegaḷindaṁ
pāṇḍavarayvarumunmīlitanayanarāgi nityaniyamaṅgaḷaṁ nirvartisi maṅgaḷavasadanaṁ
goṇḍu mahābrāhmaṇar parasuva parakegaḷumanikkuva sēsegaḷumanāntukoḷuttuṁ
palavuṁ teṟada prayāṇa paṭahaṅgaḷeseye śubha lakṣaṇa lakṣitaṅgaḷappājānēya
kāmbhōja vājirājigaḷoḷ pūḍida divya rathaṅgaḷanēṟi divyabāṇāsana
bāṇapāṇigaḷāgi nijaparijanaṁ berasu gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidurar kaḷiputtuṁ
bare purajanaṅgaḷellaṁ neredavara pōgiṅgaḻaldu sairisalāṟade—

manadoḷalampu poṇme nuḍiduṁ naḍe nōḍiyumāṭapāṭamuṁ
binadamumārumaṁ maṟeyisuttire bīdigaḷoḷ viḷāsado
ḍḍenisi toḻalva pāṇḍavara pōginoḷunte beḍaṅgugeṭṭu ha
stinapura[mi]ndu rakkasana tinda poḻalgeṇeyāgadirkumē // ViVi.94 [campakamāle]

endu kaṇṇanīraṁ negape—

parasuva pauravr̥ddhara kulāṅganeyarkaḷa sādhu vādadoḷ
berasi samantu sūsuva jalārdralasaddhavaḷākṣataṅgaḷoḷ
berasida taṇpanetti kavidettida bāsigadondu kampinoḷ
poredu madāḷigaḷverasu bandudadondanukūla mārutaṁ // ViVi.95 [campakamāle]

antu poḻalaṁ poṟamaḍe baḻiyane taguḷdu barpa tammoḍanāḍigaḷappa
mēḷadasabbavada nageya tegaḻinavaranemma baḻiyaṭṭidandu bannimendu priyaṁ
nuḍidirisi kiṟidantaraṁ bandondu tāvaregeṟeya modaloḷ nindu bhīṣma drōṇa
kr̥pa vidurarkaḷanemage takka buddhiyaṁ pēḻdu maguḻimene—

naḍapiyumōdisiyuṁ bi
lviḍiyisiyuṁ keccuvirda kūrmegaḷerdeyaṁ
naḍe pāṇḍusutaragalkege
niḍusuydar drōṇa bhīṣma kr̥pa vidurarkaḷ // ViVi.96 [kandaṁ]


[p. 65]
āgaḷ viduraṁ kelanaṟiyadantumavaraṟivantu[ṁ]sāmānya sthitiyoḷe
baṭṭeya nañjina kircina desege karaṁ prayatnapararāgimendoḍante geyvemendavara
niralvēḻdu payaṇambōgi—

poḷapina kiraṇada gāḷiya
poḷapane sairisadakusuma daḷa sukumārar
taḷardu neleyindamāgaḷ
koḷadiṁ poṟamaṭṭa haṁsegaḷgeṇeyādar // ViVi.97 [kandaṁ]

āgi tāvādigarbhēśvararappudaṟiṁ taḷardeḍeyeḍeya maraṅgaḷa toṟegaḷa
bāḍaṅgaḷa pesargaḷaṁ besagoḷuttuṁ mahāgrahāraṅgaḷa mahājanaṅgaḷa koṭṭa ponna
jannaviraṅgaḷumanavara parakeyumaṁ keykoḷuttumavarge bādheyāgadantu kāpaṁ
niyamisuttuṁ kālūrgaḷa gaṇḍara peṇḍira naḍeyuḍeya nuḍiya muḍiya gāmpiṅge
muguḷnage naguttumalligalligoḍeda keṟegamaḻidāyatanakkaṁ dhanamanittu
jīrṇōddhāraṅgaḷaṁ māḍisuttuṁ bīḍudāṇaṅgaḷoḷikkida baḷḷigāvaṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ
naneya jompaṅgaḷoḷaṁ viśramisuttuṁ bandu—

eḍaṟaṟidīva kalpataruvendu vanīpaka kōṭi santasaṁ
baḍe poḍevondakāḷa viḷayāśaniyendu virōdhigaḷ manaṁ
giḍe biyamuṁ parākramamumoppire tannoḍavuṭṭida‌r samaṁ
toḍavare vāraṇāvatamaneydidanammanagandhavāraṇaṁ // ViVi.98 [campakamāle]


idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ
dvitīyāśvāsaṁ
