śrī vīraśrī kīrti
śrī vākśrīyemba peṇḍiragalade tannoḷ
bhāvisida peṇḍirenisida
sauvāgyada hariganemmanēnoldapanō // ViVi.1 [kandaṁ]

emba bageyoḷ subhadre pa
lumbi manambasade tanuvanāṟisalalariṁ
tumbigaḷiṁ taṇṇelariṁ
tumbida tiḷigoḷadineseva banamaṁ pokkaḷ // ViVi.2 [kandaṁ]

taḷataḷisi poḷeva māvina
taḷirgaḷaśōkegaḷa misupa lategaḷa nele ba
ḷvaḷa baḷeda bēṭaduruḷiya
baḷagamidendeḷeyaḷeḷasi taḷaveḷagādaḷ // ViVi.3 [kandaṁ]

koḷada taḍiviḍidu beḷedeḷa
daḷirgaḷaśōkegaḷa lateya manegaḷoḷe teṟaṁ
boḷevalara basade suḻivaḷi
gaḷa baḷagada danige kinisi kiṅkiṟivōdaḷ // ViVi.4 [kandaṁ]

surayiya biri muguḷgaḷa pore
voreyoḷpoṟevorakanalladalluguva rajaṁ
boredu parakalisidaḷikuḷa
parikaramumanatanu śikhiya kiḍigaḷe gettaḷ // ViVi.5 [kandaṁ]

antu naneya koneya taḷira niṟidaḷira muguḷa birimuguḷa miḍiya
kiṟumiḍiya bilmiḍigaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugida banamaṁ pokkalliyuṁ meyyanāṟisalāṟade
pūta cūta lategaḷoḷ taḷpoydaposa muttina bāsaṇigeyoḷ bāsaṇisida biri
muguḷgaḷoḷ tuṟugidadirmutteya suttinoḷesedupāśrayambaḍeda sāndra
candrakāntada śileyanoḷagumāḍi—


[p. 122]
idiroḷ kaṭṭida tōraṇaṁ niṟidaḷir pūgoñcalandettame
ttida pūmāle parāga rāgamuditāśā bhā samudyanmadhū
nmada bhr̥ṅga dhvani maṅgaḷa dhvaniyenal sālvanegaṁ tāne ta
kkudu kāmaṅge vivāhamaṇṭapamenalkā mādhavī maṇṭapaṁ // ViVi.6 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

ā mādhavī latāmaṇṭapamaṁ kāmana ḍāmarakkaḷḷi vanadurgaṁ buguvante
pokkadaṟoḷage kappuravaḷukina jagaliyanagalitāgi samedu candanadeḷadaḷirgaḷaṁ
pāsi malligeyalargaḷaṁ pūvāsi mr̥ṇāḷanāḷadoḷ sameda sarigegaṅkaṇaṅgaḷumaṁ
yava kaḷikegaḷoḷ sameda kaṭisūtramumaṁ sāra karpūradoḷ viracisida
hāramumaṁ kariya neydila kāvinoḷ bhāvisida nūpuramumanadaṟa
birimuguḷgaḷoḷ citrisida karṇapūramumaṁ biḷiya tāvareyeḷagāvinasiya
nūloḷ kōda tōra malligeya birimuguḷa sarigeyumaṁ kappuravaḷukina
lambaṇamumaṁ toṭṭu kuḷirkoḻpa candana rasamanerdeyoḷaṁ meyyoḷaṁ
taḷkiṟidu kariya karbina kāvineḷa mainda vāḻeyeleya bijjaṇigegaḷiṁ bīsalvēḻdu
taṇpugeyye manada meyya santāpadoḷ bisusuydubisupinoḷanitumaṁ geldu—

kendaḷirvāsusēkadatovalgeṇeyāytu mr̥ṇāḷa nāḷavoṁ
doṁda[ḍe]votti pattiduvu sūsuva śītaḷa vāri maiyyane
ytandiradetta battiduvu tacchaśikānta śiḷātaḷaṁsiḍi
ldandoḍedattidēṁ bisido bēṭadabeṅkemr̥gāṅka vaktreyā // ViVi.7 [utpalamālike]

arigana bēṭadonde posa bēṭada kēsuriyindameyde da
ḷḷuri negedandukendaḷira pāsugaḷiṁ kuḷirvālinīrgaḷiṁ
turipade sūsutuṁ keḷadiyarnadiputtire nōḍe dāhamo
ttarisidudondu ponna salagirpavolirdudu mey subhadreyā // ViVi.8 [campakamāle]

madana davānalārci tanuvaṁ suḍe taḷtemeyoḷ paḷañci bī
gida beḷarvāyoḷuccaḷisi tuṅga kucaṅgaḷa poyloḷettaluṁ

[p. 123]
kedaṟi vaḷitrayaṅgaḷa toḍarpugaḷoḷ toḍardoyyanoyyane
ydiduvu vilōlanētra jalabindugaḷākeya nimna nābhiyaṁ // ViVi.9 [campakamāle]

nagemogamaṁ podaḷdalarda tāvareyemba vimōhadiṁ mogaṁ
bugaloḍamā taḷōdariya suygaḷa beṅkeyoḷiccegeṭṭuto
ṭṭage koḷe munde biḻdu maguḻdā satiyikkida kaṇṇa nīra dhā |
regaḷoḷe nāndelarci podaḷdormeye pāṟiduvunmadāḷigaḷ // ViVi.10 [campakamāle]

antā bāle kāyda puḍiyoḷage bisuṭṭeḷavāḻeyante surata
makaradhvajanoḷāda bēṭadoḷ mammala maṟugurtirdaḷatta manuja manōjanuṁ
madanaparitāpakkāṟadummaḷisi madhumathanana kaṇṇaṁ bañcisi vijr̥mbhamāṇa nava
naḷina parikarākr̥ṣṭa madhukara ramaṇīyapuḷina parisara pradēśa nivēśita virahi
jananicaya nicita mānasōnmatta kāminī gaṇḍūṣa sīdhu sēka puḷakita vakuḷa
mukuḷa vidaḷita manōharāśōka latā[ra]maṇīramaṇīya nūpura[rava]ramyamanaviraḷa kusumadhūḷī dhūsarapuḷina dhavaḷita dharātaḷamanutphulla
pallava līlāyamāna mattakōkilōllāsita śīkarōddāma durdina
vanamaneydevandu—

biridalaroḷ teṟamboḷeva tumbi taḷirteḷamāvu māvinaṁ
kurumane karci biccaḻipa kōgile kampanavuṅki pottu ni
ttariperalembivēvuvo madīya manōgata kāma rāga sā
garadodaviṅge nallaḷa vilōkana candrikeyonde sāladē // ViVi.11 [campakamāle]

enuttuṁ bandu birida birimuguḷgaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugidaśōkalateyanaḻkartu
nōḍi—

alaralargaṇ muguḷ nage maḍal toḍe tumbi kuruḷ taḷir taḷaṁ
gole molekempu kempukone seḷḷugurgaḷ kuḍi tōḷ nayaṁ nayaṁ
nele nele bhaṅgi bhaṅgipadavaṇ beḷarvāy peṟatallidentō kō
mala late pēḻimenniniyaḷaṁ maṟegoṇḍudo sūṟegoṇḍudō // ViVi.12 [campakamāle]


[p. 124]
endu kiṟidānuṁ bēgamaṟimaruḷādantā lateyoḷ paḻigāḷegaṅgādi
barevare kāmadēvanimmāvina naneya[na]mbugaḷumanavaṟa balmiḍiyane miṭṭe[yumaṁ]māḍi tannanēsāḍi kāḍe—

asiyaḷanolgumollanaṇamennade rūpane nōḍi kūḍalā
ṭisi parideydi pattidalargaṇgaḷanēnumanennadantupē
kṣisi manamellamaṁ kavardapaṁ tanuvaṁ baḍamāḍi kāḍi daṁ
ḍisidapanaṅgajanmana kavarteya daṇḍada pāṅgidentuṭo // ViVi.13 [campakamāle]

endu nandanavanōpakaṇṭhaṅgaḷoḷanaṅgaśaravaśanāgi toḻaldu nōḍuttuṁ
tanna manadoḷintendu bageguṁ—

uriverdeyāṟe cintipa manaṁ guḍigaṭṭe maraldu nōḍuva
ccariyoḷe becca kaṇmalarge santasadāgaramāge bēṭadoḷ
birivoḍaloyyanaṅkurise saipinoḷintenagīgaḷī vanāṁ
taradoḷe kāṇalakkumo madīya manōratha janmabhūmiyaṁ // ViVi.14 [campakamāle]

endu bageyuttumākeyirda mādhavīmaṇṭapakke mogasi palara palavuṁ
teṟada bēṭada paḍemātugaḷaṁ kēḷdalliyārānumemmandigarirdarakkumenuttuṁ barpa
gandhēbhavidyādharanaṁ subhadre bhōṅkane kaṇḍu—

paḍideṟevandadindamerdeyuṁ teṟedattu podaḷda saṅkeyiṁ
naḍukamumāgaḷubbadigamādudu sādhvasadiṁ bemar bema
rveḍegaḷinuṇmi poṇmidudu kaṇ naḍe nōḍade tappu nōḍi nā
ṇeḍeyoḷamādudā satige nōḍaloḍaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanaṁ // ViVi.15 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ suratamakaradhvajanumanaṅgāmr̥ta payōdhiyoḷ mūḍi
muḻugāḍidarante kiṟidu bēgamanirdu tanniṁ tāne cētarisi subhadreya rūpanā
pādamastakambarameyde nōḍi tannoḷāda bēṭadoḷ baḍavaṭṭumēḻgevāḍivada
sasiyante sogayisuvasiyaḷaṁ kaṇḍu—


[p. 125]
sarasa mr̥ṇāḷanāḷavaḷayaṅgaḷoḷujjvaḷa vr̥tta mauktikā
bharaṇa gaṇaṅgaḷoḷ śaśikaraṅgaḷoḷāṟade bēṭadoḷ kana
lduriverde nōḍa nōḍaloḍanāṟidudēnamardinde toydu ka
ppuravaḷukindajaṁ kaḍedu kaṇḍaripaṁvalamenna nallaḷaṁ // ViVi.16 [campakamāle]

vr̥tta kucaṅgaḷindudirda candanadoḷ taḷirvāsu beḷpanā
ḷdattu dukūladondu maḍivāsidamāḻkevolāytu meyyani
kkuttire patti kendaḷirgaḷaccugaḷacciṟidante kāmana
ccottida bēṭadaccugaḷa māḻkeyoḷirdudu mey subhadreyā // ViVi.17 [utpalamāle]

adaṟinīkeyumenageraḍaṟiyada nalla manandōṟuvudu salge dōṟuvudu
māvudu dōsamendāke kuḷḷirda taḷira sejjeyoḍane kuḷḷirpuduṁ nāṇci
pogalendeḻda kanneyaṁ cūtalatikeyemba keḷadi jaḍidu kuḷḷirisi gandhēbha
vidyādharananintendaḷ—

madanana kāypu māṇge sarasīruhajanmana meccu tīrge kō
ḷgudi manadindamindu poṟamāṟuge candrakaraṅgaḷindu ta
ṇṇiduverdegakke kendaḷira sejjeyajiñjiṇipōke ninna kū
ṭadoḷinidakke matsakhige bēṟe paḷāḷadoḷēṁ guṇārṇavā // ViVi.18 [campakamāle]

beḷaguva sāndracandra kiraṇāḷigaḷōḷigaḷindamettamu
jjvaḷisuviruḷgaḷaṁ kaḷedumeyde taḷirteḷamāvumaṁ manaṁ
goḷe naḍe nōḍiyuṁ kiviyanindoḷadiñcarakāntumintu kō
maḷeyasu mattamīyoḍaloḷirdudidemmaya saipu bhūpatī // ViVi.19 [campakamāle]

embannegaṁ suratamakaradhvajana subhadreya viraha paritāpadoḷāda paḍemātaṁ
karṇaparampareyiṁ kēḷdu santasambaṭṭu cakri, cakrikāvartiyappudaṟindā
vanāntarāḷakkorvane bandu mādhavī maṇṭapamaṁ pokku avarirvara nāṇumaṁ
naḍukamaṁ pattuviṭṭu nuḍidu—

kuḍalirpaṁ baladēvanennanujeyaṁ duryōdhanaṅgānoḍaṁ
baḍenīvaḻtiyadāgaḷuṁ ninage dal padmāsanaṁ tāne nē

[p. 126]
rpaḍisal kūḍidanirpudaltu nayaminnī poḻtepoḻtāge nī
noḍagoṇḍuyvudu kanneyaṁ taḍeyadir vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇā // ViVi.20 [mattēbhavikrīḍitam]

antu pōgevōge baladēvananumatadoḷ peṟagaṁ taguḷva yādava
balumuṇṭappoḍadanambugāṇisal nīne sālveyuḻidudaṁ māṇisalāne sālveniduve
muhūrtavāgi naḍevudendu śaibya baḷāhaka mēghavarṇa sugrīvaṅgaḷemba nālku
kuduregaḷoḷ pūḍida divya rathamanesagal dārukanemba sārathiyanīvudumā
rathamaṁ manōrathamberasēṟi cūtalatikeverasu subhadreyanēṟalvēḻdudātta
nārāyaṇaṁ nārāyaṇana parasida parakegaḷumaṁ keykoṇḍu bīḻkoṇḍindraprasthada
baṭṭeyoḷ sukha prayāṇaṅgeydanannegamitta baladēvaṁ subhadreyaṁ sāmanta
cūḍāmaṇiyuydanembudaṁ kēḷdu—

uṟadennaṁ kuḍalirda kūsanoḍagoṇḍuyvātanaṁ tāgi ta
ḷtiṟiyal kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi taralinnārārparantappa po
ccaṟa sāmantare pōgimendu palaraṁ pēḻdāgaḷeytandaraṁ
toṟekoḷvantire koṇḍuvandariganeccugrēṣu dhārājaḷaṁ // ViVi.21 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ tanna pēḻda nāyakara sāvaṁ kēḷdu yādavabala jaḷanidhiverasu
viḷayakāla jaḷanidhiyanteteraḷalbageda baladēvanaṁ vāsudēvanintendaṁ—

kulamaṁ pēḻvoḍe sōmavaṁśatilakaṁbillāḷtanambēḻvoḍu
jvala tīvrāstranighāta pātita ripuvyūhaṁ balambēḻe dō
rvaladoḷ kēḷ ninagaṁ balasthanoḍeyaṁ kūsiṅge koṇḍuyvudē
calamēdōṣamadarke nīn muḷivudē nīn pēḻvoḍān sālenē // ViVi.22 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu baladēvana manadoḷāda muḷisemba kiccaṁ tanna mr̥du madhura
vacanaracanājalaṅgaḷaṁ taḷiduna[di]pidanitta vikramārjunanuṁ katipaya
dinaṅgaḷindanēka sahakārāśōkānōkahanandanavanaprasthamanindraprasthamaneydevandu
munname tanna baravanaṟidu poḻaloḷaṣṭaśōbheyaṁ māḍi tanagidirvanda kontiya
[p. 127]
dharmaputra bhīmasēnādigaḷa pādapadmaṅgaḷaṁ tanma karakamalaṅgaḷindarcisi
tadīyāśīrvacanaṅgaḷanāntu tanage poḍamaṭṭa nakula sahadēvaraṁ parasi punaḥ
punarāliṅganaṅgeydu muhurmuhurāḷōkanaṅgeyyuttuṁ bandu divijēndra
viḷāsadiṁ poḻalaṁ puge—

parasuva purajanadodavida
parakegaḷambudhininādamaṁ mige tamma
yvarumoḍane meṟedu paramā
nurāgadiṁ bandu pokkarandaramaneyaṁ // ViVi.23 [kandaṁ]

antu rājamandiramaṁ pokku dharmaputrananagalda panneraḍumāsadoḷāda
digvijaya prapañcamumaṁ subhadrāharaṇamumaṁ puruṣōttamana parama
mitratvamumanaṟidu santasambaṭṭu tamma nibarumēkastharāgi—

eredintaṭṭalevēḻpa kanne baḻiyaṁ bandaḷ maruḷdambujō
daranintaṭṭidanintu nōntaroḷarē saipiṅge nāminniḷā
dharanuṁ yādava vaṁśajarverasu barpantaṭṭi māḻpaṁ manō
haramappantu vivāhamaṅgaḷamanendandaṭṭidar dūtaraṁ // ViVi.24 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

aṭṭidoḍavar‌ pōgi baladēvanumaṁ vāsudēvanumaṁ kaṇḍu tamma
banda kajjamanoḍambaḍisi yādavarverasu mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bare baravanaṟidu
pāṇḍavarayvarumidirvōgi yathōcita pratipattigaḷiṁ kaṇḍu poḻalgoḍagoṇḍu
bandu śubhadina nakṣatra yōgakaraṇaṅgaḷaṁ niṭṭisi—

pasurvandar pase vēdapāraga ravaṁ kaṇbēṭaduddāniyaṁ
pasaraṁ geydavolappa poccaṟa mahā sāmanta sīmantinī
prasaraṁ maṅgaḷa tūryanādameseyuttirpannegaṁ cakri rā
gisi keynīreṟedaṁ guṇārṇava mahīpālaṅgamā kanneyaṁ // ViVi.25 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 128]
antavarirvara bēṭememba lateya beḷasiṅge poynīreṟevante keynīrēṟedu
biyamaṁ meṟedu—

toṭṭa tuḍugegaḷ kaustubha ratnamanōronde masuḷise pālgaḍaloḷ
puṭṭidāneyanānegaḷ gelevare kuduregaḷ kudureyaṁ kīḻmāḍe
toṭṭa madanana pūgaṇegeṇeyāge gaṇikeyar gaṇidamaṁ bageyadintu
koṭṭaṁ taṅgege baḻivaḻiyendintu sarvasvamellamaṁ puruṣōttamaṁ // ViVi.26 [piriyakkaraṁ]

antu baḻivaḻigoṭṭimbaḻiyaṁ dharmaputraṁ baladēvananenitānumucita
pratipattigaḷiṁ santasambaḍisi dvārāvatige kaḻipidanā vivāhōtsavānantaradoḷ—

taḷirgaḷa pāsinoḷ poraḷutirdaḻalaṁ kiḍe sōṅke sōṅkugaḷ
kaḷeduvu meyya suyya padaveṅkegaḷaṁ bigiyappidappugaḷ
kaḷeduvu nāṇumaṁ kiṟidu jāṇumanaḻkaṟanīva cumbanaṁ
kaḷeduvugarmamaṁ kaḷeduvantavarirvara manmatha dravaṁ // ViVi.27 [campakamāle]

abhinava madalēkhā lālitaṁ vibhrama bhrū
rabhasa gativiḷāsaṁ dīpta kandarpa darpa
kṣubhitagaḷa nināda[ṁ]prasphuradgharma vāri
prabhavamesedudantā kāntegā kānta saṅgaṁ // ViVi.28 [mālini]

antu kāmadēvanuṁ ratiyuṁ vasiṣṭhanumarundhatiyumīśvaranuṁ
pārvatiyumenisi samarūpa samasatva samarataṅgaḷoḷe samānurāgamaṁ paḍeye
sukhamirpannegaṁ subhadrege garbhacihnaṅgaḷ tōṟe—

oṭṭajeyiṁ bhāratadoḷ
kaṭṭāḷgaḷaniṟidu tavisalā jeṭṭigaraṁ
puṭṭidanembavoladaṭaṁ
puṭṭidanabhimanyu kalitanaṁ puṭṭuvavōl // ViVi.29 [kandaṁ]


[p. 129]
antātaṁ puṭṭuvuduṁ tamage santasaṁ puṭṭi sukhamirpannegaṁ—

agaruva meccuvacca sirikaṇḍadoḷaggalisittusūḍu śa
yyegaḷa biyakke jōmpadalarvāsugaḷoḷ nelasittu pūta go
jjagegaḷa sinduraṅgaḷoḷagōgaragampane bīṟutirpa ma
lligeyoḷaralda sampageyoḷaggalisittu basantamāsadoḷ // ViVi.30 [campakamāle]

muṁ mahiyellamaṁ śiśira rājane biccatamāḷdanīgaḷā
taṁ miḍukalkesalliradepōpudadēkene kāmadēvani
ttaṁ madhu pettanī nelananintidupattaḷeyendu sāṟuvaṁ
daṁ mige karci pāṟiduvu kendaḷiraṁ giḷiviṇḍinōḷigaḷ // ViVi.31 [utpalamālike]

keḻagaṇa kendaḷir pudida mēgaṇa pandaḷirondidondu ke
ygaḻida pasurpumaṁ poḷeva kempumanāḷdire bēṭadoḷ kana
lduḻida viyōgiyaḷḷerdeyanāydadanāṭisalende manmathaṁ
ghaḻiyisi kempuvāsidavolirduvu māmaragaḷ basantadoḷ // ViVi.32 [campakamāle]

pareye pasurpu beḷpaḍare balmuguḷoḷ poredōṟe tamberal
porevoreyaṁ saḍilce naḍu poṅgire malligegaḷ basantadoḷ
biridoḍe nallaraṁ neneda nallara mellerdegaḷ basantadoḷ |
biriduvadento malligege nallara mellerde vēḷegoṇḍudō // ViVi.33 [campakamāle]

naneyeḷagampanettiyumaṇaṁ nanenāṟadaraldanēka kō
kanada vanaṅgaḷoḷ suḻidu taṇṇasamāgade kūḍe banda mā
vina posa pūvinoḷ poredu poṇmidakampu mogaṅgaḷaṁ caḷi
llene koḷe poyye tīḍidudu teṅkaṇa gāḷi vasantamāsadoḷ // ViVi.34 [campakamāle]

muguḷvadanādasampage maḍaltadirmutte maraldaralda ma
llige nanegarci kākaḷiyoḷāṇati geyva madāḷi pō pugal
pu[ga]lenutirpa pakki manamaṁ kavaruttire yōgigaṁ viyō
gigamuridāytu pokka pugilintu vasantakacakravartiyā // ViVi.35 [campakamāle]


[p. 130]
antu bhuvanakkellamosagevarpante banda vasantadoḷondu divasamannavāsa
dōlagadoḷudāttanārāyaṇanuṁ nārāyaṇanumirdalligorvaṁ—

toṭṭekkavaḍaṁ maravil
kaṭṭida paṇekaṭṭu bēṇṭevaṟe doreyoḷoḍaṁ
baṭṭasiya suragi daḷivada
toṭṭaṅgige tannoḷamare bēṇṭeyanorvaṁ // ViVi.36 [kandaṁ]

bandu poḍavaṭṭu kaṇḍiṁ
tendaṁ polanuḍugi banduduḍidudu pul kā
ḍuṁ daleleyikkeghaḷilene
ninduvu taṇiduvu mr̥gaṅgaḷettalumīgaḷ // ViVi.37 [kandaṁ]

suḻiyadu gāḷi mr̥gaṁ ke
yvaṟigaḷa mētadoḷe taṇidapuvu pandigaḷuṁ
paḻa navirikkiduvāḷaṁ
paḻu paridāḍal karaṁ beḍaṅgavanipatī // ViVi.38 [kandaṁ]

baravaṁkāḍaṁ bēgege
karamaṟideraḍuṁ mr̥gaṅgaḷuṁ taṇbuḻiloḷ
neredoḍavanduvu tappadi
darikēsari kaṇḍu meccuvai kōḷvāṅgaṁ // ViVi.39 [kandaṁ]

kāḍoḍamevēḷe saleke
ygūḍidudene neladoḷirda nelliya kāyuṁ
nōḍa nelamuṭṭalaḻtiyo
ḷāḍuvoḍī devasamalte bēṇṭeya devasaṁ // ViVi.40 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ bēṇṭejāṟallade bēṇṭeya mātaṁ binnapaṅgeyveṁ—


[p. 131]
āḍalāḍisal pāḻiyaṁ niṟisaluṁ parigoḷal tovalikkaloḷagambaral
kāḍa bēliyaṁ mārkāḍanaṟiyaluṁ mūḍigekakkumbaṁ suḻisi jōmpaṁ
bīḍu biḍuvimbu kadaḷi teṅgina tāṇaṁ jāṇiṁ nīrdāṇamendeḍe yaṟiduṁ
māḍal māḍisal paḍe mecce nīṁ balle nīṁ mecce hariga kēḷāne balleṁ // ViVi.41 [piriyakkaraṁ]

mr̥gadolavaramumanarasana
bageyumanaṟidalasadeḷasalōlagisal ne
ṭṭage ballanuḷḷoḍavana
lte guṇārṇava bēṇṭekāṟanōlagakāṟaṁ // ViVi.42 [kandaṁ]

mr̥gamaṁ gāḷiyanirkeyaṁ pakkeyaṁ gaṇidamaṁ kaṇḍiyaṁ mārkaṇḍiyaṁ
pugilaṁ pōgaṁ bāriyaṁ sanneyaṁ nūṟuvamarcuva nilveḍeyaṁ
bageyaṁ tegeyanallāṭamaṁ kāṭamaṁ nōvudaṁ sāvudanellandadiṁ
bagedāgaḷarasaroḷellakēḷnīṁ balle bēṇṭekāṟaroḷellavāne balleṁ // ViVi.43 [piriyakkaraṁ]

mattaṁ nelanuṁgāḷiyuṁ keyyuṁ mr̥gamumanaṟidu kālāḷoḷaṁ
kudureyoḷamoḷagaṁ baralāne ballenidu pervēṇṭeyandaṁ dīvada bēṇṭeyaṁ
binnapaṅgeyvoḍe gāḷiyuṁ kaḻivu[mu]ḻivuṁ kāpuṁ mēphuṁ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ
deseyuṁ koseyuṁ meccuṁ beccuṁ pōguṁ mēguṁ bedaṟuṁ[kedaṟuṁ]percuṁ
kundumanaṟidu kāṇaluṁ kāṇisaluṁ kaḍaṅgaluṁ kaḍaṅgisalumaḍaṅgisalumoḍḍalu
moḍḍisaluṁ pugisaluṁ migisaluṁ kāṇadudaṁ kāṇisaluṁ māṇadudaṁ māṇisalumē
ṟadudanēṟisaluṁ jāṇanāgi mūṟu kombumanāṟu nāṇpōgumaneraḻpajjeyumaṁ
mūṟu poḻtumaṁ mr̥gada mūṟiravumanāṟāraykeyumaṁ gāḷiyu
[mane]ṟaṅkeyumaṁ ballanāgi nambida baravumaṁ nambada baravumanaṟidu
maleyadudaṁ maleyisaluṁ maledudaṁ tolagisaluṁ nambadudaṁ nambisaluṁ
[p. 132]
nambidudaṁ biḍisalumoḷapuguvudarkeḍe māḍalumeḍeyāgada mr̥gamanavuṅkisalu
moldumollada nallarante miḍukisaluṁ paṇamuḍidaraṁ taḍḍaṁmāḍalumeseda
desegaḷgōḍisaluṁ kumārasvāmiya nimmaḍiyakeladoḷāne balleṁ—

baredante bennakarpese
dire sūcamanurci pullegāṭisi maleta
rperaleya sōlamanaḻtiyo
ḷarikēsari nindu nōḻpudondarasaltē // ViVi.44 [kandaṁ]

padamumanimbumanaṇamaṟi
yadadēvudu badde beḷmigaṁ pajjedaleṁ
budaneraḍumanaṟivātane
caduraṁ caduraṅge badde vajjegaḷoḷavē // ViVi.45 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ pandivēṇṭeya mātaṁ binnapaṅgeyveṁ—

nelanaṁ niṟugeyaṁ naḍevondu padamumaṁ sōvaḷi mēvaḷi bisuvaḷiyaṁ
balamaṁ śakunamanoḷḷittupāyamaṁ piḍivandītane vandi kuruḍu kuṇṭeṁ
dalasadaṟidintu balmege beraletti pajjeyaṁ nelegaḷaṁ kiḍalīyade
sileya mēlādoḍaṁ śakunamaṁ niṟipante niṟisuveṁ pandiyaṁ nīṁ meccaluṁ // ViVi.46 [piriyakkaraṁ]

mattaṁ pandivēṇṭeya nāyentappuvendoḍasiya naḍuvumagaluramuṁ
taḷtu kaṭṭida kiviyuṁ kavida purvuṁ tōramāginirmāṁsamappa kālgaḷuṁ nelanaṁ
muṭṭadugurgaḷumanuḷḷudāgi jātyaśvadante bēgamāgi kōḷi kāḷikāṟanante
baḻiyaṟiviḍidu tumbina nīranurcidāgaḷaḍe paridumanneyarāḷante kādiya
lasade sūḷeyantekōḷampaṭṭaṭṭisade takkanante nambisiyumottaradantotti
yumuriyaḷurvantaḷurdukoḷvudidu pandivēṇṭeya nāy mattaṁ
kiṟuvēṇṭeya nāya[ṅ]koṇḍuṁ jāṟiyuṁ nelanuṁ poḻtuṁ polanumanaṟidu
[p. 133]
baḻiyoḷ posatuṁ paḻadumanaṟidu pariyisal nīne balleyadanāne ballenendu
binnapaṅge yvenantumallade balmegaṁ basanakkaṁ saviyappa kiṟuvēṇṭeyuṁ pervēṇṭe
yumalla duḻida bēṇṭeyaṁ bēṇṭeyenneṁ—

pasivu dorekoḷgumuṇisugaḷinikeygumāvandadoḷ kanaldāda meyya
nasiyanāgipuduḷiduvappuvu bagegoḷalappudu mr̥gada meyyoḷ
nisadamesevudaṁ ballāḷa bilbalme tannoḷamisutelēsappudu
basanamendaṟiyadēḷisuva‌r bēṇṭeyaṁ bēṇṭeyebinadaṁ gaḷarasaltē // ViVi.47 [piriyakkaraṁ]

endu binnapaṅgeyda bēṇṭeyātaṅge mr̥ga vyāyāma kārtikēyaṁ mecci
meccugoṭṭutovalanikkendu munde pēḻdaṭṭi nārāyaṇanuṁ tānumantaḥpura
parivāraṁ berasu bēṇṭege poṟamaṭṭu pariya tāṇakke vandu bēliya keladoḷallade
peṟagaṇulipiṅgamuḷḷoḷakkaṁ geṇṭāgi bīḍaṁ biḍisi bēṇṭekāṟana sameda
makaratōraṇamumaṁ guṇaṇeya bāṇasina majjanada rāṇivāsada manegaḷumaṁ
naneya pandarumaṁ taḷira kāvaṇaṅgaḷumaṁmā[ḍa]daneleyacaupaḷigegaḷumanavaṟa
mēlirdeleyaḍakeyumaṁ teṅgineḷanīrumaṁ koḷalimbappantire māḍi naṭṭa kauṅgina
teṅgina maraṅgaḷumaṁpaṇverasunaṭṭa maindāvaḻegaḷumaṁ tovalverasu naṭṭālaṁ
gaḷumanamare māḍida biṭṭuḷiyakakkumba toḍambeya mūḍigeya kadaḷikeya
kaṇḍapaṭaṅgaḷumaṁ palavuṁ teṟada palavuṁ poṟeyāgi kaṭṭida balegaḷumaṁ
paḍigaḷanamarcibilluṁ kudureyuṁ kālāḷuṁ nāygaḷumaṁ tiṇṇamirisi keyyaṁ
nēṇumanaḷaviyoḷ kūḍi naḍeyalvēḻdu bēṇṭe vasadanaṅgoṇḍukaṇḍiya
bāgiloḷudāttanārāyaṇanuṁ nārāyaṇanumirdu pugila pulleya modalu
ramumaṁ peṟagaṇa pulleyanaḍuvumanaydaṟoḷ mūṟumaṁ mūṟoḷeraḍu
maneraḍaṟoḷondumaneccu billa balmeyaṁ meṟedu—


[p. 134]
mundaṇa migamaṁ kaḻipade
sandisi baḻigoḷva migamumaṁ kaḻipade tā
nondaḷavidappadeccu ba
lindamaniṁ billa balmeyaṁ pogaḻisidaṁ // ViVi.48 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ berci poḷeduparivapoḷevullegaḷumaṁ taleyaṁ kutti viśālambariva
karaḍigaḷumanaḍaṅgi pariva puligaḷumaṁ sōṅki pariveygaḷumaṁ taḍaṁmeṭṭi pariva
kaḍavina kāḍemmeya mareya piṇḍugaḷumanaḷavidappa dondondanisuvante
palavaneccu nelaṁ biriye gajaṟi garjisi pāyva siṅgaṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇḍu—

āsukaraṁ gaḍa tamagati
bhāsura mr̥garāja nāmamuṁ gaḍamendā
dōsakke muḷidu negaḻdari
kēsari kēsarigaḷanitumaṁ taḷtiṟidaṁ // ViVi.49 [kandaṁ]

iṟidavaṟa nettaroḷ ta
ḷkiṟidaṁ tannuramanuru gajaṅgaḷanāṭaṁ
daṟasi kolutirpuvembī
kaṟupinoḷarigambaraṁ gajapriyaroḷarē // ViVi.50 [kandaṁ]

antu nara nārāyaṇarirvarumanavarata śarāsāra śūnyīkr̥ta kānanamāgeccu
mr̥gavya vyāpāradiṁ baḻaldu manadante pariva jātyaśvaṅgaḷanēṟi barevare—

javamuḻidondu sōgenaviloyyane karkaḍegāsiyāgi pā
ṟuvudumidenna nallaḷa rati śramaviślathakēśapāśadoḷ
sava savanāgitōṟidapudembude kāraṇadindadaṁ guṇā
rṇavaniḍaloldanilla haya valgana sañcaḷa ratna kuṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.51 [campakamāle]


[p. 135]
antu bēṇṭeyanāḍi baḻaldu bēsageya naḍuvagaloḷ vanakrīḍegaṁjalakrīḍegamāsaktarāgi yamunānadī taṭa nikaṭavartigaḷādaralli—

saraḷa tamāḷa tāḷa haricandana nandana bhūja rājiyiṁ
surivalarōḷi tadvanalatāṅgiya sūsuva sēseyāytu bhr̥ṁ
ga ravamadondu maṅgaḷa ravakkeṇeyāytu manōnurāgadiṁ
karevavolāytu matte kaḷahaṁsaravaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanaṁ // ViVi.52 [campakamāle]

yamunānadī taraṅgama
namuṅki vanalateya manegaḷaṁ sōṅki vana
bhamaṇa pariśramamaṁ mu
nname kaḷedudu bandadondu mandaśvasanaṁ // ViVi.53 [kandaṁ]

antu kāḷindī jala śiśira śīkara vāri cāriyuṁ mr̥gayā paribhrama
śramōtthita svēda jala lavahāriyumāgi banda mandānilakke meyyanāṟisuttumā
puṇyanadiyaneydevandu tanna bāḷa nīrante kaṟaṅgi kargida nīraṁ nōḍi
vikramārjunaṁ kāḷāhimathanana mogamaṁ nōḍi—

tannoḷagaṇa pannaganaṁ
munnīn piḍidogeye kāyalāṟade piriduṁ
bannada karpesedudu toṟe
ginnuṁhara gaḷa tamāḷa nīḷacchaviyiṁ // ViVi.54 [kandaṁ]

taḍiviḍidu pūta lategaḷa
noḍanoḍanelaraleye biḍade surivalargaḷanaṁ
deḍeguḍade nūṅki mellane
taḍiyaṁ sārcidapudidaṟa bambalderegaḷ // ViVi.55 [kandaṁ]

vidaḷita nuta śatapatrada
paduvinoḷiradagalevōda haṁsananaṟasal
padedeḷasuva peṇṇañceya
pada koraliñcarada sarame savi kivigidaṟoḷ // ViVi.56 [kandaṁ]


[p. 136]
neṟeyalardambhōruhadala
rduṟugalanaledogeduveseye jaladēvategaḷ
niṟiviḍiduḍal nimircida
kuṟuvaḍiya taraṅgadante bambalderegaḷ // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

turagacayaṅgaḷantire taraṅgacayaṁ camarīruhaṅgaḷaṁ
tire kaḷahaṁse beḷgoḍegaḷantire beḷnore goṭṭi gāṇaraṁ
tire maṟidumbi mēḷadavarantire sārike rājagēhadaṁ
tire koḷanalli tāmarasarantire tāmarasaṅgaḷoppuguṁ // ViVi.58 [campakamāle]

endu bhāskara tanūjeyanubhaya taṭa nikaṭa kusuma nivaha tatparāgapaṭaḷa
piśaṅga tarattaraṅga sarōjeyaṁ mecci pogaḻdu jalakrīḍeyāḍal bagedu
tānumanantanumantaḥpura parivāraṁ berasu—

ottida taḷkettida taṟe
muttina posaduḍuge taḷira sōrmuḍi manamaṁ
pattisi jottise madanō
nmatteyaravayavade bandararasiyararebar // ViVi.59 [kandaṁ]

idu mr̥du kaḷahaṁsada rava
midu nūpura ninadamidu rathāṅgayugaṁ ma
ttidu kuca yugamidu sarasija
midu mogamenisidudu nereda peṇḍira taṇḍaṁ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]

antu madanana manōrājyamebarpante bandu taṇḍataṇḍade ramaṇīya
ramaṇījanaṁ berasu pañcaratnaṅgaḷiṁ kedaṟisi sāndina sausavada kuṅkumada katturiya
kadaḍaṁ kadaḍi—

nīlada beḷḷiya gāḍiyu
mī lalitāṅgiyara kaṇgepōltuṁ[nāṁ]ka
ṇgēḷidamāgirevendeḷa
vāḷegaḷōḍiduvu bāleyar puguvāgaḷ // ViVi.61 [kandaṁ]


[p. 137]
antu pokkāgaḷ—

ādale nīr guṇḍitteṁ
dīdaleyoḷe nindu satige harigaṁ tōṟu
ttādarade jānudaghnamu
rōdaghnaṁ kaṇṭhadaghnamembaḷavigaḷaṁ // ViVi.62 [kandaṁ]

antu jaguneya maḍuvaṁ tammarasiyara vikaṭa nitamba bimbaṅgaḷa
ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷamare bagidogeda molegaḷaḷḷēṟinoḷaḷḷāḍi taḷḷaṅkaguṭṭi
nīrāṭamāḍuvāgaḷ—

posatalardondu tāvareyegettu mukhābjamanondu tumbi cuṁ
bise sati berci peḷpaḷisi nōḻpudumākeya kaṇṇa beḷpugaḷ
pasarise tumbigaḷ kuvalayaṅgaḷaralduve gettu matteyuṁ
musuṟuvuduṁ guṇārṇavananāgaḷavaḷ bhayadindamuppidaḷ // ViVi.63 [campakamāle]

asiyaḷavuṅki kendaḷadoḷottuva nīr mogamaṁ paḷañce baṁ
cisalinisānumaṁ muḻugidāgaḍe bhōṅkane bandu bāḷemīn
musuṟi nirantaraṁ karduke satkaviyoḷ samanāgi mārgamaṁ
posayisi dēsiyaṁ posatu māḍidaḷorvaḷapūrva rūpadiṁ // ViVi.64 [campakamāle]

ā sakaḷa strī nivahada
pūsida mr̥gamadada muḍiyapūvina rajadiṁ
vāsisida nīra kadaḍiṁ
dāsavadoḷ sorki beṇṇḍumaguḻduvu mīṅgaḷ // ViVi.65 [kandaṁ]

muḍi biḍe paredesaḻgaḷa posa
duḍugeya muttugaḷa kucada sirikaṇḍada be
ḷpoḍanoḍanesedire jaguneya
maḍu gaṅgeya maḍuvaninisananukarisirkuṁ // ViVi.66 [kandaṁ]

antu nāḍeyuṁ poḻtu jalakēḷī līleyoḷ meṟedu nimirda kuruḷgaḷuṁ
kempēṟida kaṇgaḷuṁ beḷpēṟida bāydeṟegaḷuṁ paḷañcida baṇṇaṅgaḷumeseye
[p. 138]
sogayisuva nija vadhū janaṁ berasu poṟamaṭṭāgaḷ—

teṟapuvaḍedaṅgajaṁ ke
yseṟegoḷe nōṭakara manamanāgaḷ koḷadiṁ
poṟamaḍe jigiltu pattida
kuṟuvaḍigaḷe meṟeduvavara nāṇgaḷa teṟapaṁ // ViVi.67 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ maḍiya bhaṇḍārada māṇikya bhaṇḍārada niyōgigaḷ tandu
mundiṭṭa ponna paḍaligegaḷoḷoṭṭida dēvāṅga vastraṅgaḷumananēka vidhada
tuḍugegaḷumanenitānuṁ teṟada sugandha dravyaṅgaḷumanarasiyargamarasumakkaḷgamittu
tāmirvaruṁ uṭṭu toṭṭuṁ pūsiyuṁ neṟeye keygeydu divyāhāraṅgaḷa
nārōgisi keygaṭṭigoṇḍu tambulaṅgoṇḍimbaḻiyamacyutaṁ vikramārjunana
keyyaṁ piḍidukoṇḍu tanna bāla krīḍeya sāhasaṅgaḷaṁ tōṟalendu—

kondenavuṅki sanda khara dhēnukaraṁ muḷisindamilli kā
ḷindiya pāvanappaḷisideṁ piḍidī sileyalli mattamā
ṭandaranugra daityaranaḷurkeyinikkidenilli munnameṁ
dandu guṇārṇavaṅge madhu kaiṭabhahāritoḻaldu tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.68 [utpalamālike]

antā vanāntarāḷamaṁ toḻaldu tōṟuttirpannegamanūna dāniya
dānaduddāniya dānamanānalānallade peṟar‌ neṟeyarembante toṭṭane
kaṭṭidiroḷ—

urivuriyane talenaviranu
karisire santapta kanakavarṇamumuriyoṁ
duruḷivolire jaṭharānaḷa
nurivinamantorvanuriya baṇṇada pārvaṁ // ViVi.69 [kandaṁ]

antu varpanaṁ kaṇḍu sāmantacūḍāmaṇi tannoḷintendu bagedaṁ—


[p. 139]
tapaniyama niyatanī ba
rpa pārvanēnaḻti tanagadaṁ bēḍidoḍi
nnapagata duritar sampū
rṇa puṇyarānalladilla pēḻ peṟaroḷarē // ViVi.70 [kandaṁ]

embannegaṁ sāmantacūḍāmaṇiyaneydevandu nālkuṁ vēdaṅgaḷoḷ
nālkuṁ r̥caṅgaḷaṁ pēḻdu sita dūrvāṅkura vimiśraṅgaḷappa śēṣākṣategaḷaṁ koṭṭu
munde nindanaṁ nimage bāḻteyappudaṁ bēḍikoḷḷimene—

maṇi kanakādi vastugaḷanondumanollenavēvuvādavi
nnuṇisenagaḻti mey pasidujommanepōdapudenna vēḻpudaṁ
taṇiyuṇalīvoḍīvudene pārthanadēviridittenāvudu
ṇbuṇisene pēḻvenemba padadoḷ narakāntakanagnidēvanaṁ // ViVi.71 [campakamāle]

kāṇaloḍamaṟidu śaraṇāgatajaḷanidhiyaneyde vandanī bakavēṣi
ninnanēnaṁ bēḍidaṁ nīnītaṅgēnanitteyene—

pasiduṇavēḍidaṁ baḍavanānuṇalittenadalladilli dal
kusuriya mātugāṇenene kēḷdu murāntakanēṁ taguḷde yi
nnusiradirīva mātanivanuṇbudu khāṇḍavamītanagni muṁ
pusidivaninte pāyisidanindranoḷādi narēndrarellaraṁ // ViVi.72 [campakamāle]

ītanajamukhavyāghraṁ śvētakr̥ṣṇakārakanītana mātu mātallavendoḍā
mātu tannaṁ mūdalisidantāge vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇanintendaṁ—

eredana pempuvēḻvoḍanalaṁ poṇarvātana pempuvēḻvoḍā
surapati koṭṭa tāṇadeḍevēḻvoḍamā yamunānadī taṭāṁ
taramosedittanānereye kēḷdaniḷādhara nīnadarke mā
teraḍaṇamāḍalāgadidu saipinoḷallade kūḍi barkumē // ViVi.73 [campakamāle]

danujārī divijēndra śāśvataguṇā ninnaḷkadēṁbēḍidā
nanalaṁ tīrtha samīpamambunivaha vyāḷōḷa kāḷindiyā

[p. 140]
vanamuṁkēḷduvubhūtamaydumaṟiguṁ koṭṭirdudādantaṟiṁ
denagiṁ māṇbudu sūḻe khāṇḍavamanāṁ taḷvilladindūḍuveṁ // ViVi.74 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

otti taṟumbi ninda ripubhūjasamājada bērgaḷaṁ nabha
kkettade bandu tanna maṟevokkoḍe kāyade cāgadoḷpina
ccottademāṇpu bāḻva puḻuvānasanembanajāṇḍamembudoṁ
dattiya paṇṇoḷirpa puḻuvallade mānasanē murāntakā // ViVi.75 [utpalamālike]

endu maṟumātiṅgeḍeyilladantire nuḍida paḍemeccegaṇḍana gaṇḍavātumaṁ
nannivātumaṁ murāntakaṁ mecci—

samakaṭṭiṅgoregārumillariga kēḷ ninnoḷ samaṁ dhātriyoḷ
himakr̥dbhūdharadante ninna guṇa sandōhaṅgaḷaṁ kāṇala
kkume mattorvanoḷāgadentene samastōrvīdharāśēṣa śē
ṣamahānāgaphaṇāmaṇi dyutiyanēṁ khadyōtadoḷ kāṇbarē // ViVi.76 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

muniyisidaṁ karaṁ piriyanappudu bēḻpana bēḻpa vastu kāṁ
cana giriyindamaggaḷamenippudadādoḍamēno jīvamu
ḷḷinamiṟidarthamuḷḷinegamittu negaḻteyanāmpudemba peṁ
pina samakaṭṭu kaṇge doreyārarikēsari ninnavōl peṟaṁ // ViVi.77 [campakamāle]

endu tanage koṭṭa kōḍiṅgoḍambaṭṭa ditijakula dāvānalanu manarāti
kālānalanumananalaniṣṭārtha siddhiyakkumendu parasi manaḥpavana vēgadiṁ
pālgaḍalaneydi tanna baytiṭṭa divya sambhavaṅgaḷappa śvētāśvaṅgaḷoḷ pūḍida
divya rathamumaṁ dadhīci gaṇḍasthamappa gāṇḍīvavemba billumaṁ divya śaraṅgaḷoḷ
tekkane tīvida tavadoṇegaḷumaṁ tandenna pratijñeyaṁ tīrcuvoḍamindranaṁ
gelvoḍamivanamōghaṁ keykoḷalvēḻkumendoḍatirathamathananagnidēvaṅge poḍavaṭṭu
keykoṇḍu br̥handaḷanemba sārathiverasu rathamanēṟaloḍaṁ—

pāvakanaḻvi khāṇḍavanamanuṇḍapanarjunanūḍidappanai
rāvatavāhanaṁ neṟedu sādhana saṁyutanāmpanalli nā

[p. 141]
nā vidha yuddhamuṇṭenute śaibya baḷāhaka mēghavarṇa su
grīva hayaṅgaḷindesevudaṁ rathamaṁ hari tānumēṟidaṁ // ViVi.78 [utpalamāle]

antu dārukaṁ rathamaṁ cōdisaloḍaṁ—

cōdisuvudumirvara ratha
cōdakaravareraḍu rathada gāliya kōḷiṁ
dāda rajaḥpaṭalaṁ kavi |
dādame tīvidudu divija vadhuvira kaṇṇoḷ // ViVi.79 [kandaṁ]

anteydi yamunānadiya teṅkaṇa deseyoḷ nūṟu yōjana
dagaladoḷamanite nīḷadoḷaṁ neṟedu—

kakubhāśōka kadamba luṅga lavalī bhūjārjunānōkaha
prakaraṁ puṣpita hēma paṅkaja rajassaṁsakta bhr̥ṅgāṅganā
nikaraṁ sārasa haṁsa kōkiḷa kuḷadhvānōtkaraṁ celvanā
ytu karaṁsaktaniḷimpa dampatigaḷindā nandanaṁ nandanaṁ // ViVi.80 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

ene sogayisuva khāṇḍava vanamaṁ vanaruhanābhaṁ vikramārjunaṅge
toḻaldu tōṟi—

alaraṁ nōyisadoyyanoyyanaḷigaḷ baṇḍuṇpuvāṭandu baṁ
daleyalkaṇmadu gāḷi sūrya kiraṇānīkakkamendappoḍaṁ
salavilluddhata siddha khēcarare tāmāḷvēriyāgintu ni
ccalumōrantire kāvarī doretu kāpī nandanakkindranā // ViVi.81 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

orme toḻaldu nōḍi banamaṁ maghavaṁ śaci pūta cūtamaṁ
nermidaśōkavallariya pallavamondane koydu rāgadiṁ
sōrmuḍiyoḷ taguḷcidoḍe sūḻane bārisidaṁ dalendoḍiṁ
kūrmeya mātu meccuvanitarke baḷārimurāsurāri[yēṁ] // ViVi.82 [utpalamālike]


[p. 142]
intappa banamanidani
nnentanalananūḍalendu pūṇday muṁ pū
ṇdantūḍu pūḍu[śita]śara
santatiyaṁ billoḷēke nīṁ taḍedirpay // ViVi.83 [kandaṁ]

paramāṇuvanitu banadoḷ
carācaraṁ pōge taṇiyananalanadarkāṁ
neramappenugra kinnara
sura danujōragara kadanamēṁ ninagaridē // ViVi.84 [kandaṁ]

embudumante geyvenenna sāhasamaṁ nōḍimendu vikrānta tuṅganuttuṅga
bhujaparighaderaḍu deseyoḷaṁ tavadoṇegaḷaṁ bigidu gāṇḍīvamanēṟisi nīvi
jēvoḍedu divyāstraṅgaḷaṁ piḍidu keytīvikoṇḍagnidēvanaṁ nōḍi—

ōḍuge nimma meyya pasivānta virōdhigaḷenna keyyoḷa
ḻkāḍuge koḷḷimuṇṇimene kēḷdanalaṁ parasuttumā laya
krīḍeyoḷī carācaramumaṁ suḍuvandina meygamaggaḷaṁ
māḍi taguḷdu nīḷdu baḷedarviseparvidanā vanāntamaṁ // ViVi.85 [utpalamālike]

phaḷa karpūra lavaṅga luṅga lavaḷī hintāḷa tāḷī tamā
ḷa ḷatā sundara nandanakkaḷuremuṁ tannarcigaḷabandu mo
kkaḷamettaṁ suriyuttumirpa rasamaṁ muṁ pīrdukoṇḍaṁ manaṁ
goḷe saptārci podaḷdu nīḷdosageyindāpōśanaṅgoḷvavōl // ViVi.86 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

nanekoneya taḷira pūvina
banamanituṁ śikhegaḷaḷure beṅkeya poydu
rvinoḷe koragirda lategaḷa
konegoneyane dahananaḷurdu konegonegoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.87 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷā banamanindrana besadoḷ kāva kinnara kimpuruṣa garuḍa gandharva
siddha vidyādhara balamanitumondāgi vikramārjunanoḷ tāge—


[p. 143]
koṇḍapuduri banamanadaṁ
kaṇḍentiralakkumendu tāgida negaḻdo
ḷgaṇḍara gaṇḍōḍuvinaṁ
koṇḍuvu gāṇḍīvamukta bāṇa gaṇaṅgaḷ // ViVi.88 [kandaṁ]

antu kāde vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇana moneyambinambēṟiṅgaḷki hatavihata
kōḷāhaḷarāgi siddharasiddharāgeyuṁ kinnararinnāra maṟeyaṁ puguvameneyuṁ kiṁ
puruṣar kāpuruṣarante bāyaṁ biḍeyuṁ gandharvar garvamanuḻidondorvaraṁ
migeyōḍeyuṁ vidyādhararadhararāgeyuṁ pannagar pannatikeyiṁ bandāntoḍe—

nāgara khaṇḍaṅgaḷanā
nāgara khaṇḍadoḷe toḍare naranisuvudumā
nāgara khaṇḍaṅgaḷumaṁ
nāgara khaṇḍamumanaḷurdukoṇḍaṁ dahanaṁ // ViVi.89 [kandaṁ]

virahigaḷa suyya beṅkeyo
ḷiradoṇagiduvakkumīgaḷenalurivuriyiṁ
karimurikanāduvunmada
parabhr̥ta ṣaṭcaraṇa rājakīra kulaṅgaḷ // ViVi.90 [kandaṁ]

uri koḷe desegāṇade dese
varivaridu kujaṅgaḷaṁ paḍalvaḍisi bhayaṁ
berasoḷaṟe negedudā vana
kariśarabhakiśōra kaṇṭhagarjane banadoḷ // ViVi.91 [kandaṁ]

saṅgata dhūmāvaḷiyani
bhaṅgaḷe gettoḷaṟi pāydu poge puge kaṇṇaṁ
siṅgaṅgaḷaḷure garjisi
laṅgisi puḍapuḍane puḻgi sattuvu palavuṁ // ViVi.92 [kandaṁ]

mattamalli kelavu latāgr̥haṅgaḷoḷaṁ dhārāgr̥haṅgaḷoḷaṁ—


[p. 144]
oḍanaḷure kircu tōḷaṁ
saḍilisadā prāṇavallabha[r]prāṇamanaṁ
doḍagaḷedarōparōparo
ḷoḍasāyalpaḍedarinnavuṁ saypoḷavē // ViVi.93 [kandaṁ]

antu khāṇḍava vanamellamananalaṁ praḷaya kāḷānaḷanantaḷurdukoḷe baḷasi
bandu kāva nārāyaṇana sudarśanavemba cakrada kōḷumaṁ vikramārjunana
divāstraṅgaḷa kōḷumanagnidēvana śikhā kaḷāpada kōḷumanentānuṁ bañcisi bale
paṟida kōkanantorva vanapālakaṁ pōgi dēvēndrana kaṇḍu—

dēva binnapamindu khāṇḍavamaṁ kr̥śānu taguḷdu nā
nā vidhaṁ suḍe nōḍalārade taḷtadēvara kāpināḷ
dēva kinnara pannagāvaḷi moṭṭanappinameccu koṁ
dēvarendaṟidirdanorvanagurvu parvire dēvaraṁ // ViVi.94 [mallikāmāle]

eraḍu rathamoḷavu nōṭa
kkeraḍaṟoḷavanondu rathametōṭige palavā
gire paridu kaṇṇoḷinnuṁ
tiridapuduridapudu namma banamenitanituṁ // ViVi.95 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ pauḷōmīpati tanna divyajñānadoḷ nōḍi cakriyuṁ
vikramārjunanumappudanaṟidu gajaṟi garjisi viḷaya kāḷāmbudadante
moḻagumaṁ siḍila baḷagamanoḷakoṇḍa drōṇa mahādrōṇa puṣkaḷāvarta
suvartakaṅgaḷemba mugilgaḷaṁ besasidāgaḷavu vindhyācaḷa kūṭa kōṭigaḷe
kiḻteḻdubarpante bandu desegaḷellamaṁ musuri kaḻtalisi kavidu—

kaviduvu saptasāgara jalaṅgaḷe lōkamanīgaḷembinaṁ
kavidu mugilgaḷalli kaṟeyuttire pāvakanurkugeṭṭideṁ
tuvo todaḷāytu dānamene māruta bāṇade mēgha mālikā
nivahamaneccu kūḍe śarapañjaramaṁ paḍedaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.96 [campakamāle]


[p. 145]
antu puṅkhānupuṅkhamāge pāyva śarasandhānadoḷeḍevaṟiyadanteraḍuṁ
keyyoḷ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgadantise tuṟugi kavivambina maḻeye maḻeyaṁ
māṇise divyāstraṅgaḷiṁ nūṟu yōjanadaḷaviya khāṇḍavavana mellamaṁ taṭṭi
meḍaṟi maśaka mātramappoḍaṁ misukal chidramilladantāge śarapañjaradoḷ
mucci musukidāgaḷabhinava jīmūtavāhanana divyāstrada kōḷgiralāṟade
jīmūtaṅgaḷellaṁ teraḷdōḍidoḍagnidēva nāvageya kircinantoḷagoḷagaḷurdu—

vana khaga vana mr̥ga vana taru
vanacara vana vanaja nivahamuḷḷanituṁ sī
ranitumaṇamuḻidudilleṁ
binamuṇḍaṁ dahananaḷurdu khāṇḍavavanamaṁ // ViVi.97 [kandaṁ]

antā vana gahanamellaṁ dahanamayamāda prastāvadoḷ vismayamāge
mayanemba dānava viśvakarmaṁ negedurivurimālegaḷaṁ gadeyoḷ bīsuttuṁ
poṟamaḍe poṟamaḍalīyade—

ondu deseyoḷ taguḷva mu
kundana karacakramondu deseyoḷ narane
ccondu śaravondu deseyoḷ
kundade dahanārci sutti muttuva padadoḷ // ViVi.98 [kandaṁ]

śaraṇakkenagarikēsari
yeraḍu padāmbujamumīgaḷembudumāgaḷ
hari cakraṁ koḷḷade nara
śaramurcade dahana śikhegaḷaḷurade avanaṁ // ViVi.99 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ mayaṁ vismayambaṭṭu poḍavaṭṭu pōdanāgaḷā
vanāntarāḷadoḷirpa takṣakana maganappaśvasēnanemba pannagaṁ tanna tāyaṁ tanna bālamaṁ
karcelvēḻdu dahanārcigaḷiṁ barduṅki negedu pāṟuvāgaḷadaneraḻkhaṇḍamappina
mākhaṇḍaḷatanayanisuvuduṁ tanna bālamberasuriyoḷ biḻdu miḍumiḍu
miḍukutirda jananiyaṁ kaṇḍu pāvugaḷuḷḷa pageyaṁ maṟeyavembudaṁ nannimāḍi—


[p. 146]
page sāṟuvuduṁ kolleṁ
page sāṟida ninnanāra maṟeyaṁ pokkuṁ
pageyaṁ neṟapene neṟapuva
bageyoḷe pokkaṁ kaḍaṅgi karṇana doṇeyaṁ // ViVi.100 [kandaṁ]

antaśvasēnanardhāvalikamembamōghāstramāgi karṇana doṇeyoḷirdanitta
khāṇḍavavanadoḷage mandapālanemba munigamondu lāvagegaṁ puṭṭida nālkuṁ
lāvagegaḷagnisūktaṅgaḷanōduttumadiradidiraṁ bare mecci baravanagnidēvaṁ
bēḍikoḷḷimendoḍemmanvayakke nīn taṇṇideyāgendu bēḍuvuduṁ
tadastuvendanittalindraṁ tanna balamellamaḷkimeḷkidantādudembudaṁ kēḷdu—

maganenagendu pēḻ piḍidu kaṭṭade māṇpene pārthanaṁ dhari
trige guruvendu vajradoḷuruḷcade māṇpene cakriyaṁ karaṁ
bageyade goḍḍamāḍidarge takkudanīgaḷe māḻpenendu to
ṭṭage poṟamaṭṭanēṟi nijavāhanamaṁ divadiṁ surādhipaṁ // ViVi.101 [campakamāle]

antu dēvanikāyaṁ berasu yuddha sannaddhanāgi parasainya bhairavanoḷiṟivenemba
paḻuvageyoḷbhairavambāyvante bandu ninda purandaranallige sarasijasambhavaṁ
bandu mārkoṇḍu—

banamane kāyalendiṟiveyappoḍe munname pōdudandu pā
rthanoḷenagēvamemba bageyuḷḷoḍe ninnaya putranacyutaṁ
giniserde nōveyappoḍadu kūḍadu mūvaroḷorvanemma mā
tinite guṇārṇavaṅge kuḍu gellamanintide kajjadujjugaṁ // ViVi.102 [campakamāle]

endu kamalāsananāsedōṟi nuḍiduḷḷudane nuḍidoḍante geyvenendu—

surivaralondu beḷsariyadātma tanūbhavanuttamāṅgadoḷ
dorekoḷe nilladalli kusumaṁ kelavalluge tanna ratna vi
sphurita kirīṭamaṁ kavidu tāne naraṅge kirīṭi nāmamaṁ
sarasadināgaḷuccarisi sāhasamaṁ pogaḻdaṁ surādhipaṁ // ViVi.103 [campakamāle]


[p. 147]
antu pogaḻdu khāṇḍavana dahanadoḷāda pogeyoḷamalliya mahā
nāgaṅgaḷa viṣamberasu suyva suyya pogeyoḷaṁ kaṟaṅgi kaḻgida meyyumaṁ
pracaṇḍa gāṇḍīva vyāghātadoḷindranīlaṅgaḷanaḍasidantappa muṅgeyyumaṁ kaṇḍu
kr̥ṣṇanemba pesaraniṭṭanāgaḷ brahmaṁ brahmāyuvakkendu parasidanīśvaraṁ nīnudāra
mahēśvaranappudaṟiṁ ninagamenagamētaṟoḷaṁ vikalpamuṁ vicchinnamumillendanantu
mūdēvaruṁparasi nija nivāsaṅgaḷge pōdarāgaḷ—

anitinitennadānta sura pannaga kinnara sainyamellamaṁ
bina moneyoḷ paḍalvaḍe latābhavanaṁ kr̥takācaḷaṅgaḷeṁ
binitumavaḻgi taḻge nuḍiyaṁ nuḍidante negaḻcalagnidē
vananamarēndra nandanamanūḍidanandanarēndranandanaṁ // ViVi.104 [campakamāle]

āgaḷsvāhāṅganānāthaṁ sampūrṇa manōrathanāgi khaṭvāṅganembarasana
yajñadoḷātana tanda ghr̥ta samudramaṁ kuḍidoḍāda rōgamindu pōdudendu
nīroganāgi mahānurāgamberasu parasi pōdanāgaḷirvarumindra prasthakkeyde
vandu—

idirvare dharmajaṁ berasu tannoḍavuṭṭidareyde taḷtu ka
ṭṭida guḍi raṅgavalligaḷe dāṅguḍiyantire sūse sēseyaṁ
sudatiyarikke cāmaramanaṅganeyar nijakīrti lōkamaṁ
pudidire pokkanandu nija mandiramaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.105 [campakamāle]


idu vividhavibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja
varaprasādōtpanna prasannagambhīra vacana racana
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ
pañcamāśvāsaṁ


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 148]
[ṣaṣṭhāśvāsaṁ]

śrīge phaḷaṁ cāgaṁ vāk
śrīge phaḷaṁ sarvaśāstra pariṇati vīra
śrīge phaḷamāyavendiṁ
tāgaḷumaṟidesagidaṁ parākramadhavaḷaṁ // ViVi.1 [kandaṁ]

antu khāṇḍavavana dahana prapañcadiṁ baḻiyamarāti vana dahana tīvra
pratāpa gahanakke munnamaḷki paramaṇḍaḷikarittuṁ tettuṁ besakeyye kelavu divasamirdu
nārāyaṇanaṁ dvārāvatige kaḷipi—

tuṅga taraṅga bhaṅgura payōdhi parīta mahā mahītaḷā
liṅgita kīrti kēḷdu baḍa pārvana puyyalanorme kēḷdanā
vaṅgamagurvu parve javanoḷ seragillade pōgi tāgi taṁ
daṁ gaḍa vikramārjunane pārvara piḷḷeya pōda jīvamaṁ // ViVi.2 [utpalamālike]

endu lōkamellaṁ pogaḻe vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇanuṁ bhīma yudhiṣṭhira
nakuḷa sahadēvarumayvaruṁ berasondu divasamōlagaṅgoṭṭire dharmaputranallige
mayaṁ pañcaratna hiraṇmayaṁ caturaśraṁ mūṟuṁ yōjanadaḷaviya
sabhāmaṇṭapamanondu lakka rakkasavaḍeyiṁ pottu tarisi tanna nalmeyaṁ balmeyaṁ
meṟeyalendu dēvalōkadiṁ tandu mundiṭṭu—

idaṟandaṁ bisavandamondu teṟanaltentendoḍārayvoḍiṁ
tidaṟoḷ divya sarōvaraṅgaḷidaṟoḷ kalpāvanījaṅgaḷiṁ
tidaṟoḷ‌ nāṭakaśāle rayyamidaṟoḷ dēvāpsarōnr̥tyaviṁ
tidaṟantāgire nōḻpoḍārumaṟiyar māḍal sabhāgēhamaṁ // ViVi.3 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endennī prāṇamembudu vikramārjunana dayegeyda prāṇamenna
koṭṭudarke mārkoḷḷade koḷḷimendoḍante geyvevendu niścayisi dharmaputraṁ
gōlagaṅguḍaltakkudendadaṁ dharmaputraṅge koṭṭu parākramadhavaḷaṅge śaśāṅkaviśada
yaśame teraḷduruḷigoṇḍantirda śaṅkhamaṁ bāsaṇigegaḷedu—


[p. 149]
idanindranaṭṭidaṁ nina
gidaṟa pesar dēvadattamembudu ninaga
bhyudayakaraṁ śaṅkhaṁ riphu
hr̥daya kavāṭapuṭa vighaṭanaṁ nōḍarigā // ViVi.4 [kandaṁ]

endadaṁ vikramārjunaṅge koṭṭu munnaṁ ṣōḍaśa rājaroḷage
māndhātanembaṁ vidyādharanātana gadeyidu baḻiyamātanaṁ lavaṇanembasuraṁ kādi
kondu koṇḍoḍātanaṁ rāmacandrana tammaṁ śatrughnaṁ geldu tanage koṇḍu
samudrada naḍuvaṇa mainākaparvatadoḷ maḍagidoḍenagidaṁ varuṇadēvanitta
nintappudu—

adhika ripu nr̥pati baḷa nava
rudhira jaḷa sphurita raudramī gade pesariṁ
rudhiramukhiyembudendada
nadhika baḷasthaṅge bhīmasēnaṅgittaṁ // ViVi.5 [kandaṁ]

antittu baḻiyamavara dānasanmānādigaḷiṁ mayaṁ rāga rasamayanāgi
santasambaṭṭu pōdanitta mattondu divasamā sabhāmaṇṭapadoḷ dharmarājaṁ
tanna nālvar tammandiroḍane dēvēndralīleyindōlagaṅgoṭṭireyire—

beḷagugaḷellamonduruḷiyāgi nabhasthaḷadindamī mahī
taḷakiḻitarpudendu manujākr̥tiyendu munīndranendu ka
ṇgoḷise munīndraroḷ kamaḷasambhavanandananendu nōṭakar
taḷaveḷagāge sārevare nīrada mārgadinandu nāradaṁ // ViVi.6 [campakamāle]

baḷasi tannoḍanoyyanoyyane barpa dēvaradondu gā
vuḷiyaninnirimendu tannane niḷki nōḻpare kaṇge ka
ṇboḷepu tannayameyya beḻpinoḷaḻdu nindoḍe vāḷemīn
poḷeye dhātrige varpa gaṅgevoloppidaṁ munipuṅgavaṁ // ViVi.7 [taraḷaṁ]

antu barpāgaḷ—


[p. 150]
sarigeyoḷ samedakṣamālike ponna muñji toḷappa ka
ppurada bhasma raja[stripuṇḍra]kamoppe piṅga jaṭāḷi tā
vareya sūtradoḷāda jannaviraṁ dukūlada kōvaṇaṁ
karamoḍambaḍe nōṭakarkaḷanā tapasvi maruḷcidaṁ // ViVi.8 [taraḷaṁ]

baṭṭagoḍe candrakāntiya
naṭṭumbarigoḷe podaḷda kr̥ṣṇājinamoṁ
diṭṭaḷameseye beḍaṅgaṁ
puṭṭise gāḍigaḷoḷeseva vīṇā kvaṇitaṁ // ViVi.9 [kandaṁ]

beraloḷ bīṇeya tantiga
ḷorasida keṅgalegaḷakṣamāleyoḷesedaṁ
tire poseyemuttupavaḷaṁ
berasidavōlāytu cenna tapasiya keyyoḷ // ViVi.10 [kandaṁ]

antu sākṣāt brahmaṁ barpante bandu—

aḍiyiṭṭaneḷeyoḷivaneṁ
beḍeyoḷ parijana samētamidireḻdarasaṁ
poḍavaḍe tapasvi keyyaṁ
piḍidetti palarme parasidaṁ parakegaḷaṁ // ViVi.11 [kandaṁ]

antu dharmaputranabjajaputranaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bandu maṇi kanaka
racana vicitra vētrāsanadoḷirisi mahārghya guṇamaṇi vibhūṣaṇaṅge kanaka
pātradoḷarghyametti kanaka kaḷaśa sambhr̥ta śucijalaṅgaḷindamā munīśvarana
pādapadmamaṁ karci tatpāda pavitrōdakaṅgaḷiṁ mahā r̥ṣiya taḷida kanaka kamaṁ
ḍaluvinatīrthōdakaṅgaḷindayvuruṁ pavitrīkr̥tamastakarāgirdu yudhiṣṭhiraṁ nārada
mahā muniya mogavaṁ nōḍi—


[p. 151]
paḍedaṁ brahmaṁ jagamaṁ
paḍeyal tānārtanilla pempaṁ nimmaṁ
paḍedalte paḍedanenisida
kaḍu pempina poṟege nīvu modaligarādir // ViVi.12 [kandaṁ]

bādēnā madīya karma pha
ḷōdita santāparūpa pāpakaḷāpa
cchēdanakaramāytu bhava
tpāda prakṣāḷanōdakaṁ munināthā // ViVi.13 [kandaṁ]

besanenagāvudō besasiṁ
besanaṁ piridakke geyye sārdirdenadaṁ
besasiṁnimmaya baravaṁ
posatāgire bandirīgaḷelliṁ bandir // ViVi.14 [kandaṁ]

embudumā munīndranindralōkadiṁ bandemendoḍalliya
paḍemātāvudu—

divijēndraṁ sukhamirdanē ditisutavyābādhegaḷ dēvargi
llavalāṣōḍaśa rājarirpa teṟanēnemmanvayakṣmāparā
va viḷāsaṅgaḷoḷirparēdoretu tānemmayyanaiśvaryamiṁ
tivanellaṁ tiḷivantuṭāgi besasiṁ paṅkēja garbhātmajā // ViVi.15 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embudumā munīśvaraniḷā[dha]rēśvaraṁ besagoṇḍandadoḷe dēvalōkada
paḍemātellamaṁ pēḻdu pāṇḍurājana mātanintendaṁ—

nīḍiradindranōlagake pōpudumāgaḷumante pōgiyuṁ
ṣōḍaśa rājariṁ kaḍeyoḷirpudu jīya pasādamembuduṁ
nōḍida dr̥ṣṭigaḷkisugidirpudumādame mānabhaṅgamaṁ
māḍe manaḥkṣatakkaḷavigāṇevu nōḍire pāṇḍurājanā // ViVi.16 [utpalamālike]


[p. 152]
para cakraṅgaḷanottikoṇḍadaṭaraṁ kondikki dāyādare
llarumaḷkuttire sanda sāhasada nimmīyayvaruṁ makkaḷā
gireyuṁ niccalumindranōlagadoḷantā pāṇḍurājaṅge ni
rneramappondapamānadindaminitondūnatvamappantuṭē // ViVi.17 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āmumadaṁ nōḍalāṟadeyuṁ pāṇḍurājanennirdiravanenna makkaḷgaṟipi
rājasūyamemba yāgamaṁ bēḷvante māḍi bannimeneyumidanaṟipalende bandemā
makhada mahātmyamaṁ pēḻvoḍe munnaṁ kr̥tayugadoḷ hariścandranemba cakravarti
śatakratuvaṁ nirvartisi caturarṇava parīta mahītaḷamellamaṁ dharāmararkaḷge dakṣiṇe
goṭṭanappudaṟindamadaṟa phaladoḷīgaḷātanalligindraṁ niccamondu poḻtu pōgi
pūjisi barpaṁ nimmayyaṅge nīmumanitu mahimeyaṁ māḻpirappoḍe—

birudaranotti bīraranaḍaṅgisi koṅkigaraṁ kaḻalci ce
nnaranaḍigotti maṇḍaḷikaraṁ besakeysi kaṟumbaraṁ nirā
karisi samastavāridhi parīta mahītaḷadarthamellamaṁ
tarisi negaḻteyaṁ niṟisalārpoḍe māḍire rājasūyamaṁ // ViVi.18 [campakamāle]

endu rājasūyāntaṁ kaḷahamembudaṁ bagedu tānuṁ kalaha
priyanappudaṟindamanitane nuḍidu māṇda munīndranaṁ narēndranintendaṁ—

beḷaguvudindralōkadoḷagayyana mātenalemma sāhasaṁ
beḷaguvudī dharāvaḷayadoḷ taṇivar‌ dvijamukhyarappuda
ggaḷike podaḷdu parvuvudu kīrti purākr̥ta puṇyadinde saṁ
gaḷisuvudendoḍī makhadoḷēn todaḷuṇṭe munīndra nāyakā // ViVi.19 [campakamāle]

embudumā mātaṁ nile nuḍidudarke mecci ninagadēviridu—

parapina nīḷada kaḍeyaṁ
maruḷaṁtave nōḍalāṟadambara taḷamaṁ
karidembantire ninnaṁ
naranembude ninna sāhasakkadu piridē // ViVi.20 [kandaṁ]


[p. 153]
endu nuḍidu nāḍeyuṁ poḻtirdumin pōpemenda munināthanaṁ
naranāthaṁ bijayaṅgaiyyimene nāradanirade gaganataḷakkogedu mugila poreyoḷaḍaṁ
gidanitta dharmarājaṁ nijānujaroḍane rājasūya prapañcamanāḷōcisi
puruṣōttamananī padadoḷ barisuvudu namaguttama pakṣamendu—

dvāravatī purakke cararaṁ taḍavillade bēgamaṭṭi paṁ
kēruhanābhanaṁ barisi majjana bhōjana bhūṣaṇādi sa
tkāradoḷaḻkaṟaṁ neṟeye māḍi murāntaka pāṇḍu bhūbhujaṁ
kāraṇamāge nāradana pēḻda negaḻteya rājasūyamaṁ // ViVi.21 [utpalamālike]

bēḷale bagevoḍe hariyoḍa
nāḷōcipamendu baḻinaṭṭidenemmaṁ
pāḷisuvai[nīn]nimmoḍa
nāḷōcisademage negaḻalēṁ neravuṇṭē // ViVi.22 [kandaṁ]

embudumadellamaṁ neṟeye kēḷdu mundaṇa kajjada biṇpuma
naṟidambhōruhanābhaṁ śumbhadambhōdhara dhvaniyinintendaṁ—

endu bigurtu dhīrarane kondapirentu samasta vārdhi pa
ryanta dharitriyaṁ vaśake tandapirentu dhanaṅgaḷaṁ prayō
gāntaradiṁ teraḷcidapirāgadidādoḍamentu rājasū
yāntamidentu bēḷdapirapāya śataṁ bare rājasūyamaṁ // ViVi.23 [utpalamālike]

gāḷu goravaṁ taguḷci pa
ḷāḷamanēnondanappoḍaṁ gaḻapidoḍā
bēḷu nuḍigēḷdu kemmane
bēḷal nimagantu rājasūyaṁ moggē // ViVi.24 [kandaṁ]

munnaṁ kr̥tayugadoḷ sōmanavaruṇana rājasūyada kaḍeyoḷ
dēvāsura yuddhaṁ negaḻe hiraṇya kāḷanēmigaḷ modalāgi negaḻteya daityarellamenna
cakraghātadoḷaḻgimaḻgidantādaradondu dharāvani[te]ya bhārāvatāradoḷenitānuṁ
[p. 154]
ghasaṇi pōdudadu kāraṇadiṁ rājasūyada mātaṁ kēḷdalliye maṟevudu
nuḍiyalvēḍene maṟumātuguḍalaṟiyade dharmaputraṁ maunaṅgoṇḍusiradire
parākramadhavaḷanintendaṁ—

enitu gaḍaṁ payōnidhiparīta mahītaḷamembudāmpa bī
ranapesarāvudī nuḍiyanī padadoḷ peṟagikke nāradaṁ
manadoḷe pēsuguṁ surapanuṁ naguguṁ kaḍuvinnanakkuma
yyana mukhamentupēkṣisuvudī makhamaṁ sarasīruhōdarā // ViVi.25 [campakamāle]

endoḍe bhīmasēnanintendaṁ—

pannatara naḍuvanuḍiya
lkenna bhujārgaḷame sālgumose mēṇ muni mē
ṇenna nuḍiṭāṭhaḍāḍhaṇa
mennaṁ besasuvudu rājasūyaṁ bēḷal // ViVi.26 [kandaṁ]

endu gajaṟi garjisuvudumamaḷarumī bēḷveya mātantemaḷe
nuḍidoḍemma gaṇḍavātumaḷumbaṁ bhr̥tamakkumendumey meyge
besasembuduṁ rājasūyamaṁ bēḷdalladirirappoḍe gaṅgānadiya baḍagaṇa taḍiya
maghamaghisuva vāraṇāsi puramanāḷva br̥hadbaḷaṁputrōtpattinimittamappondu
divya piṇḍamaṁ tannirvararasiyarge peccu koṭṭoḍe puṭṭideraḍu
pōḻumanivēvuvendu bisuḍe jareyemba rakkasi kaṇḍu tinalenderaḍu pōḻumanondu
keyyoḷe piḍidoḍondondaṟoḷ sandisi mānasa rūpugoṇḍoḍe cōdyambaṭṭu
jarāsandhanendu pesaraniṭṭu br̥hadbaḷaṅge koṭṭoḍe jarāsandhanuṁ sālvalanumemba
daityanumondāgi mūvatteraḍakṣōhiṇībalaṁ berasu madhurāpurakke vandennaṁ
muttikoṇḍoḍupāya baladoḷe sālvalanaṁ kondu jarāsandhaṅgaḷki madhurāpuramaṁ
bisuṭṭu pōgi dvārāvatiyaṁ samudrame nīrgādigeyāgi māḍideninnuṁ yādavara
seṟegaḷellātanallirdarātanuṁ bhīmana keyyoḷallade sāyanembudādēśamadaṟi
nemmicceyuṁsamasta balamberasu bhīmārjunaraṁ pēḻvudendu
[p. 155]
dharmaputrananoḍambaḍisi nuḍidu madhurāpuramaneydi br̥hadbaḷa tanūjanallige
dharmayuddhamaṁ bēḍiyaṭṭidoḍe—

kalimārkoḷḷade koṭṭu meyyoḷe siḍil tāpantevōl tāge me
ygali bhīmaṁ peṟapiṅgadāntu palavuṁ bandhaṅgaḷiṁ taḷtu ta
tkulaśailaṁ kulaśailadoḷ kaluṣadiṁ pōrvantevōl pōrdu ne
ydila kāvaṁ tudigeyde sīḷva teṟadiṁ sīḷdaṁ jarāsandhanaṁ // ViVi.27 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu dr̥ḍha kaṭhina hr̥daya bandhanaṁ jarāsandhanaṁ kondumātana magaṁ
kṣēmadhūrtiyaṁ rājyadoḷ niṟisi jarāsandhanēṟuva rathamaṁ tarisi samasta
vastugaḷaṁ koṇḍu garutmanaṁ nenedu barisi rathamaṁ cōdisalvēḻdu yādavara
seṟegaḷumaṁ mundiṭṭu nārāyaṇaṁ bhīmārjunarverasu sukhaprayāṇaṅgaḷiṁ
dindraprasthakke vandu dharmaputranaṁ kaṇḍu—

jarāsandhaṁmunnaṁmaḍidoḍiḷe niṣkaṇṭakamada
rkiralvēḍin nālkuṁ desege besasiṁ nimmanujaraṁ
bharaṅgeyvāgaḷ nīṁ pesarvesaroḷā nālvarumanā
daraṁ[goṇḍā]nālkuṁ desege[besasiṁ]beḷkuṟuvinaṁ // ViVi.28 [śikhariṇi]

antu bhīmasēnananindrana mēlevēḻvante pūrva digbhāgakke vēḻdu nakuḷanaṁ
yamananadirpalvēḻvante dakṣiṇadiśābhāgakke besasi sahadēvanaṁ varuṇananadirpal
niyamisuvante paścima digbhāgakke vēḻdu vikramārjunanaṁ kubēraniṁ kappaṅgoḷal
samarpisuvante uttarōttara māgaluttaradiśābhāgakke vēḻdāgaḷ—

ari narapāla mauḷimaṇiyoḷ nelegoṇḍudu śaṅkha cakra cā
mara haḷa cihna cihnita padākr̥ti bīsuva cāmarāḷi suṁ
dariyara keygaḷiṁ barduki biḻduvu beḷgoḍe nōḍe nōḍe niṁ
duriduvu sālabhañjikegaḷaḻtuvu vairi narēndra gēhadoḷ // ViVi.29 [campakamāle]

antu vijayaṁ tanna digvijayadoḷāda vijaya cihnaṅgaḷ
munname negaḻe vijaya[da]guḍiviḍisiarinr̥paraṁ chēdisi pāñcāḷaraṁ
[p. 156]
cāḷisi gāndharvaraṁ viratharmāḍi kauḷādhīśaraṁ sādhisi kimpuruṣaraṁ kāpuruṣarmāḍi
bāhlikarana[nanī]karenisimāḷavigaraṁ keḻagivigeyyalīyadāṭandu nija nāmāṅkita
sāyakaṅgaḷindeccu naccaṁ kiḍisi—

uṟadirpantemagāva garvamiṟiyalvēḍemma nemuḷḷudaṁ
neṟekoṇḍemmaya bāḻveyoḷ niṟisuvaṁ nīnendu tandittu ke
yseṟeyaṁ koṭṭaḷavaṭṭasāra dhanamaṁ mūviṭṭigaṁ pūṇdu kā
lgeṟagittantarigaṅge berci bhayadiṁ grāmaṁ kuḷaṁ rājakaṁ // ViVi.30 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

mattamalli kelaraṁ maitrāsana vr̥ttiyoḷaṁ niṟisi kelaranuddhatāpratima
hitarmāḍi kelaranuccāṭisi sarva haraṇaṅgeydu kasavaramellamanindraprasthakke kaḻipi
kāśmīra himavanta hēmakūṭa kaiḷāsa pāriyātra śvētaśr̥ṅga gandhamādana giri
nikaṭa vartigaḷappa parvata rājaranapagata tējarmāḍi kasavaramaṁ keygemāḍi
mēruparvatada teṅkaṇa taḻpaloḷ dvādaśa yōjana pramāṇamappa jambūvr̥kṣada
keladoḷaḍasi rasada toṟe parivante kanaka giriyanalendu pariva jambūnadamemba
toṟeyoḷ puṭṭida jāmbūnadamemba ponna pāsaṟegaḷaṁ kaṇḍu—

gāṇḍīvada koppugaḷoḷ
khaṇḍisi tattaṭada kanaka rēṇuvanavanā
khaṇḍala tanayanasuṅgoḷe
khaṇḍisidaṁ niśita paraśu śara samitigaḷiṁ // ViVi.31 [kandaṁ]

antu kanaka rēṇugaḷ puṭṭida pāsaṟegaḷumaṁ kanakada piriya
selegaḷumanoṭṭi beṭṭāgi puñjisi—

barisi ghaṭōtkacaṁ berasu dānava sēneyanīgaḷī balaṁ
berasivanintu pottu naḍe namma purakkene tadgirīndra kaṁ
dara kanakācaḷaṅgaḷenituṇṭanitaṁ tave hēma rēṇuga
ḷverasu kaḍaṅgi pottu naḍedattu ghaṭōtkaca raudrasādhanaṁ // ViVi.32 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ parākramadhavaḷaṁ tanna parākramamaṁ meṟeyalendu kaiḷāsada mēgaṇge
vandu kubēraniṁ kappaṅgoṇḍu ponnaṁ jakkarekkeyiṁ pottu bare taḍeyadindraprasthakke
[p. 157]
bandanitta bhīmanuṁ mūḍaṇa diśābhāgamaṁ bāykēḷisi dēvēndrana
vajramumindrāṇiya kaigannaḍiyumuḻiye samasta vastugaḷaṁ tandaṁ sahadēvanuṁ
paḍuvaṇa deseya maṇḍaḷikaranadirpiyumudirpiyuṁ koṇḍu varuṇana makaramuṁ
varuṇāniya koraloḷaydeminugumuḻiyeyuḻida vastugaḷellamaṁ tandu
mundiṭṭaṁ nakuḷanuṁ teṅkaṇa deseya maleparaṁ maṇḍaḷikarumanasiyarāge
kavardukoṇḍu laṅkeya mēge naḍedu vibhīṣaṇaṁ tanage bāykēḷadirdoḍe
vikramārjunaṅge pēḻdaṭṭidoḍe—

toṇḍinoḷurkikeṭṭa daśakaṇṭhananakkaṭa koṇḍapermaruḷ
koṇḍude tannumaṁ bisuḍu nīṁ balagarvamanā samudramē
baṇḍamo pāydoḍendu nija sāyakadoḷ baredeccu kappamaṁ
koṇḍanavuṅki laṅkeya vibhīṣaṇanaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.33 [utpalamālike]

antu nālkuṁ samudraṅgaḷa nīruḻiye ratunaṅgaḷumaṁ diśā gajaṅgaḷuḻiye
gajaṅgaḷumaṁ ādityana kuduregaḷuḻiye kuduregaḷumaṁ dēvēndrana surabhiyu
mīśvarana nandiyumuḻiye gōvrajaṅgaḷumanindraprasthakke teraḷci baḻiyaṁ
nārāyaṇana matadoḷ hastināpuradoḷirda dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidura gāṅgēya
drōṇāśvatthāma kr̥pa bāhlīka sōmadatta bhagadatta bhūriśravaḥ karṇa śalya śakuni
saindhava duryōdhana duśyāsanādigaḷgellaṁ baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi śiśupālādigaḷa
ppanēkādhīśvararellarumaṁ barisi vyāsar modalāge brahmar̥ṣiyarellarumaṁ
parasi tuḻila parakeya samāna pratipattiyiṁ kiṟiviriyaraṟidu poḍevaṭṭu
parasiyappikoṇḍu nuḍiduṁ nōḍiyuṁ nakkuṁ keyyaṁ piḍiduṁ ballidire endu
priyadoḷaṁ birdinoḷaṁ santasambaḍasi śubha dina vāra nakṣatra yōga karaṇa
muhūrtadoḷindraprasthakke uttara digbhāgadoḷ sahasra yōjana pramāṇadoḷ
yāgamaṇṭapamaṁ samedu mayana koṭṭa sabhāmaṇṭapadoḷ brahma
r̥ṣiyarumanarasumakkaḷumaneḍeyaṟidirisi yajña dravyaṅgaḷellamaṁ nerapi
mahāvibhavadoḷ śamī pārśvataḷadakṣiṇāśāleyoḷ hiraṇyadānavaṁ
māḍi vēdinihitaṁgaḷappāhavanīya dakṣiṇa gārhapatyaṅgaḷemba mūṟuṁ
koṇḍaṅgaḷoḷuttara vēdiyoḷagni sandhānaṁ geydu vyāsa kaśyapa viśvāmitra
[p. 158]
bhāradvājabrahmādhvaryvāgnīdhra maitrāvaruṇāgni paricārakōdgātr̥ nētr̥
hōtr̥ jamadagnyādigaḷappa ṣōḍaśartvijarkaḷiṁbēḷalvēḻdu dharmaputraṁ sapatni
yajamānanāgirdāgaḷ—

cārutara yajña vidyā
pāragara ravaṅgaḷiṁ svadhākāra vaṣa
ṭkāra svāhākārōṁ
kāra dhvani negaḻe negaḻdudāhuti dhūmaṁ // ViVi.34 [kandaṁ]

baḷase mugilgaḷ kanakā
caḷamaṁ baḷasuvavolikkidāhutigaḷa goṁ
daḷadinoḍanogeda pogegaḷ
baḷasiduveḍeviḍade kanakayūpamanāgaḷ // ViVi.35 [kandaṁ]

oḍane diganta dantigaḷa kōḍa modalgaḷoḷeyde pokku si
ppaḍisida māḻkeyāduvu karaṅgaḷaḍaṅgi kilumbugoṇḍa ka
nnaḍigeṇeyāytu bhānuvaḷayaṁ divijāpage nōḍe kūḍe ka
rpaḍardeṇeyādudā yamunegaggada yāgada dhūmadēḻgeyoḷ // ViVi.36 [campakamāle]

gaṇanātītājyāhuti
gaṇadindaṁ taṇiye jātavēdanumābrā
hmaṇa samiti bēḷe dēvar‌
taṇiyuṇḍar neredu divyahavyāmr̥tamaṁ // ViVi.37 [kandaṁ]

tridaśēndraṅge yudhiṣṭhirādhvaradamāsāmarthyamaṁsūḻu sū
ḻade pēḻal parivante poṇme palavuṁ dhūmaṅgaḷā hōma dhū
mada gandhaṁ nasu muṭṭe divya makhamaṁ keykoṇḍu saggakke pā
ṟiduvā pāriva jakkavakkigaḷadēṁ pempō mahāyajñadā // ViVi.38 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 159]
antu purōḍāśa pavitrōdaranuṁ sōmapānakaṣāyitōdaranumāgi
mūvatteraḍu divasadoḷ kratuvaṁ nirvartisi mahādānaṅgeydu dakṣiṇā
kāladoḷ—

oṭṭida ponna beṭṭugaḷanīveḍegēvudo tūkamenna ke
ygaṭṭaḷe koḷḷimendu kuḍe ṣōḍaśa r̥tvijargittudarke bā
yviṭṭire vipra kōṭi maḍagalkeḍeyillade ponna rāśiyaṁ
baṭṭane bandu kāye yamanandananēn todaḷilladittanō // ViVi.39 [utpalamālike]

dānāmbhaḥ pīna gaṇḍasthaḷa kari nikaraṁ bāḻteyō meccuvēḻā
jānēyāśvōtkaraṁ bāḻteyo maṇinicayaṁ bāḻteyō pēḻimendā
dīnānātharge vr̥ddha dvija muni nikarakkandeḍar pōpinaṁ kaḥ
kēnārthī kō daridraḥ enutumanitumaṁ dharmajaṁ sūḻe goṭṭaṁ // ViVi.40 [sragdhare]

antu nija dhavaḷacchatra cāmara siṁhāsanādi rājacihnaṅgaḷuḻiye
sarvasvamellamaṁ dakṣiṇegoṭṭu vyāsa gāṅgēya vidura bāhlīka sōmadatta
bhagadatta dhr̥tarāṣṭra drōṇāśvatthāma kr̥pa kulavr̥ddharumaṁ duryōdhana duśyāsana
karṇa śalya śakunigaḷumanavaravara dāna sanmānādigaḷoḷaṁ santasambaḍisi dharmaputraṁ
pēḻimī sabheyoḷagrapūjegār takkarene gāṅgēyanintendaṁ—

baliyaṁ kaṭṭidanāvanī dharaṇiyaṁ vikrāntadinda rasā
taladindettidanāvanandu narasiṁhākāradiṁ daityanaṁ
caladiṁ sīḷdavanāvanabdhi mathana prārambhadoḷ mandarā
calamaṁ tandavanāvanātane valaṁ takkaṁ peṟar takkarē // ViVi.41 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu tanna manadoḷaccottidante nuḍida gāṅgēyana mātaṁ manadegoṇḍu
yamanandananānandamberasante geyvenendu puruṣōttamaṅgarghyamettidāgaḷ—


[p. 160]
muḷidu śiśupālanā sabhe
yoḷage mahāpraḷaya jaḷadhinādadiniradu
ccaḷisi nuḍidante kaḷe kaḷe
harigettidanarghyadarghyamaṁ dharmasutā // ViVi.42 [kandaṁ]

tīvida nareyuṁ ḍoḷḷuṁ
dēvavratanenisi negaḻda yaśamuṁberasi
nnīvudu harigarghyamaneṁ
dāvanānumī bhīṣmarantu nuḍidarumoḷarē // ViVi.43 [kandaṁ]

kuru vr̥ddhaṁ kula vr̥ddhaṁ
saritsutaṁ takkanendu nambida sabheyoḷ
doregiḍisi nuḍidoḍēnola
varamennade nīnumadane koṇḍesaguvudē // ViVi.44 [kandaṁ]

manadolavaramuḷḷoḍe kuḍu
maneyoḷ harigagrapūjeyaṁ yajñadoḷī
manujādhīśvara sabheyoḷ
neneyalumāgadu durātmanaṁ besagoḷvā // ViVi.45 [kandaṁ]

aḷavaṟiyadeggu baḷavaḷa
baḷevinegaṁ pacca pasiya tuṟukāṟaṅga
ggaḷikeyane māḍi nīnuṁ
paḷiyaṁ kaṭṭideyo bhūparinibara koraloḷ // ViVi.46 [kandaṁ]

dēvaranaḍigeṟagisi saka
bhāvanitaḷadadaṭaraṁ paḍalvaḍisida śau
ryāvaṣṭambhadoḷānire
gōvaḷigaṅgagrapūjeyaṁ nīn kuḍuvā // ViVi.47 [kandaṁ]

samakaṭṭaṟiyade hariga
rghyametti nindirda yajñamadu modaloḷ tā
namardumamardiradetaṇiyuṁ |
ḍamardaṁ gōmūtradinde bāyvūsidavōl // ViVi.48 [kandaṁ]


[p. 161]
kuḍavēḻvana kuḍuvana kuḍe
paḍevana pempēṁ negaḻtevaḍegumo pēḻvaṁ
kuḍavēḻgema kuḍuvaṇṇaṁ
kuḍugema kuḍe koḷva kaliyanaṟiyalkakkuṁ // ViVi.49 [kandaṁ]

endanitaḷ māṇade gīrvāṇāriyasurāriyanintendaṁ—

doreyakkume ninage yudhi
ṣṭhiranarghyamanette śaṅkhadoḷ pāleṟedaṁ
tire malinamilladoḷgula
darasugaḷire nīnumagrapūjeyanāmpā // ViVi.50 [kandaṁ]

manadolavaradindī yama
tanayana kuḍuvagrapūje matsannidhiyoḷ
ninagaśaniya miḻtuva naṁ
jina doreyendoṇara nandagōpāla sutā // ViVi.51 [kandaṁ]

mane ninage nandagōpā
lana mane tuṟugārti ninage maneveṇḍati pa
ccane pasiya gōvanai kara
manayade ninnaḷavigaḷavanaṟiyade negaḻde // ViVi.52 [kandaṁ]

muranaḍasi piḍidu kaṭṭida
paribhavamaṁ maṟedeninna peḍageyga[ṭṭa]ṁ
śaradiṁ biḍisidanallane
saritsutaṁ bannavinnavembuvumoḷavē // ViVi.53 [kandaṁ]

danujāntakanembī ni
nna naccuvōdaṅkamelavo munnennannaṁ
danujaṁpuṭṭade sandudu
ninagī pesaranna mundeyuṁ sandapudē // ViVi.54 [kandaṁ]


[p. 162]
ānirda sabheyoḷarghyama
nānalkāṭisida ninna bisunettaraniṁ
tī neravi nōḍe kuḍiyado
ḍēnō śiśupālanemba pesaresedapudē // ViVi.55 [kandaṁ]

maṟeda mucukundanemba
maṟevokkudanandu nīn jarāsandhaṅgaṁ
biṟutōḍidudaṁ bhūtaḷa
maṟiyade neneyelavo gōvugādudu pusiyē // ViVi.56 [kandaṁ]

mīnāve pandiyendeni
tānuṁ teṟanāgi ḍomba viddeyanāḍal
nīnaṟiveyuṟadidircido
ḍānaṟiveṁ ninnanilli desevaligeyyal // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

aṟiyadidaṁ māḍidene
nnaṟiyamikege sairisendu nīn sabheyoḷ kā
lgeṟageṟagu kollenenderde
teṟevinegaṁ hariya neṟananasuraṁ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.58 [kandaṁ]

antu nuḍidu kāypinoḷ piḍugi naḍanaḍa naḍugi—

poḷeduḷkuva kuḍu dāḍeya
poḷapu nosalgaḍardu poḍarva purvesevinama
vvaḷisuva muḷisina daḷḷuri
gaḷanuguḻvavoluguḻdanasuranuriva paḻigaḷaṁ // ViVi.59 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ sabhāsadarellamevemiḍukade pandeyaṁ pāvaḍardavolusiradire
nārāyaṇaṁ śiśupālananintendaṁ—

ninnaya tāy sātvatiyuṁ
ninnaṁ tandenna toḍeyamēliḻipuvuduṁ
ninna lalāṭada kaṇṇadu
munname kiḍe ninna mr̥tyuvennaya keyyoḷ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]


[p. 163]
neṟedudanaṟidī kiṟiyava
naṟiyade keḍe nuḍidanappoḍaṁ nūṟuvaraṁ
neṟe salisuvudendudanāṁ
maṟevene bay bayye salisuveṁ nūṟuvaraṁ // ViVi.61 [kandaṁ]

muniyalenagāga gāṅgē
yanirdanirdaṁ ghaṭōdbhavaṁ negaḻda pr̥thā
tanayarumirda‌r duryō
dhananirdaṁ kēḷe pēḻvarāballavaruṁ // ViVi.62 [kandaṁ]

eneyene bāygaṁ bandani
tanitumanamarāri bayye sairisi nūṟeṁ
banituvaraṁ mannisi nasu
kinisade mige kinisi ditijakuḷa davadahanaṁ // ViVi.63 [kandaṁ]

muḷidu tanagarghyamettida
taḷigeyoḷiḍetiṟida teṟade tale paṟidāgaḷ
kaḷakaḷisi nagutumirdudu
taḷigeya mēlasuranadaṭidēnaccariyō // ViVi.64 [kandaṁ]

antu javanarghyamettidantirda śiśupālana śirōmbujamaṁ kaṇḍaḻaldātana
naṇṭarappaśvagrīva vidyunmāli nīlādigaḷappaprabhugaḷenibarānuṁ murāntakanaṁ
bandu tāgidoḍe—

tiripikara cakramaṁ danu
jara talegaḷanasuravairi muḷidiḍe paṟidaṁ
barataḷamaneydi mēghada
porevoreyoḷ toḍardu nelakebīḻavetalegaḷ // ViVi.65 [kandaṁ]

anitondu mahā praghaṭṭadoḷagrapūjeyaṁ nārāyaṇaṅge koṭṭavabhr̥thasnānadoḷ piridumosageyaṁ māḍi yāgavidhiyaṁ nirvartisi nereda
rājakulamellamaṁ pūjisi visarjisidāgaḷ murāntakanantakanandanananintendaṁ—


[p. 164]
hima sētu pratibaddha bhūvaḷayamaṁ niṣkaṇṭakaṁ māḍi vi
kramamaṁ tōṟi nijānujar nerapidondaiśvaryadiṁ rāja sū
yamanindaggaḷadaggaḷikkeya makhaṁ tānembinaṁ ninna kī
rti mukhaṁkīrti[mukhambolēne]sedudō digdanti dantaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.66 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu nuḍida mandaradharanaṁ ninnanugrahadoḷadēviridenduvastu
vāhanaṅgaḷanittu dvārāvatige kaḷipi sukhasaṅkathā vinōdaṅgaḷoḷ rājyalakṣmi
yananubhavisuttirpanne gamattaṁ—

mēgillada ballāḷtana
dāgaramene negaḻda tatpr̥thānandanaru
dyōgada cāgada yāgada
bhōgadamaimege suyōdhanaṁ beṟagādaṁ // ViVi.67 [kandaṁ]

āgi duśyāsana karṇa śakuni saindhavaremba duṣṭacatuṣṭayadoḷ
mantaṇamirdu dāyigarappoḍe karaṁ percidaravara perciṅgēgeyvaṁbasanaṅgaḷaṁ
samakaṭṭuvamappoḍe saptavyasanaṅgaḷayvarumanonduṁ gelvuvallavu rāṣṭra vyasanamaṁ
baḷavyasanamaṁ pārvamappoḍavu munnamilla paramaṇḍaḷa vyasanamanārayva
mappoḍittuṁ tettuṁ bāḻva maṇḍalamallade kīṟiyuṁ mīṟiyuṁ negaḻva
maṇḍalamilla puruṣamaṁ samakaṭṭuvamappoḍe pokkiṟiyalaṇmuvarilla rasa
dānādigaḷoḷ chidrisuvamappoḍavarāptavantaruṁ buddhivantarumāgi negaḻdarinnāva
māḻkeyoḷ pageyaṁ keyge māḍuvaṁ pēḻimene śakuniyintendaṁ—

besasida ninna mātinitumantuṭe gellavu pāṇḍu putraraṁ
basanadoḍambaḍaṁ maṟedumā yamanandananaltenettadoḷ
basaniganātanaṁ barisi nettamanāḍisi geldukoḷvamī
vasumatiyaṁ manambasade nīn baḻiyaṭṭu phaṇīndrakētanā // ViVi.68 [campakamāle]


[p. 165]
endu nāḻavāsagegaḷaṁ munname samakaṭṭi tāmumāmuṁ kelavu devasaṁ
gōṣṭhiyoḷirpaṁ barkendu baḻiyanaṭṭidoḍavara manada pulvageyaṁ
pollameyumanaṟiyade samasta baḷōdyuktanāgi śakunaṅgaḷa kramamaṁ bageyade
niyatiḥ kēna laṅghyatē emba nuḍiyaṁ nannimāḍi madagajēndra puramaneyde bare
dhr̥tarāṣṭrādi kulavr̥ddharoḍane duryōdhananidirvōgi dharmaputraṅge poḍavaṭṭu
bhīmanaṁ samāna pratipattiyoḷ kaṇḍu tange poḍavaṭṭa mattina mūvarumaṁ
tegedu taḻkaisi parasi tanna tammandirellarumanayvargaṁ poḍavaḍisi poḻa
loḷagaṇgevandu rājamandiramaṁ pokku—

nōḍi pr̥thā tanūjara sabhāgr̥hadandamanantuṭappudaṁ
māḍipenendu māḍisi sabhālayamaṁ nijarājalīleyoḷ
kūḍi yudhiṣṭhira prabhuge tāne suyōdhananuydu tōṟidaṁ
nōḍiresiṁhamāḍuvara bālamanāḍidaremba māḻkeyiṁ // ViVi.69 [utpalamālike]

antu suyōdhanaṁ tanna vibhavamumaṁ viḷāsamumaṁ pāṇḍavarge meṟedu
kandukakrīḍādi nānā vidha vinōdaṅgaḷiṁ kelavu divasamanirdondu divasaṁ tanage
sāvaṁ samakaṭṭuvante piṅgākṣanakṣakrīḍeyaṁ śakuniyoḷ samakaṭṭi pūḍalvēḻdu
pusiyane peṟaraṁ munnamāḍalvēḻdu tānuṁ dharmaputranuṁ keladoḷirdu nōḍuttire
śakuniyintendaṁ—

nōḍuvudaṟoḷēnaḻtiyo
ḷāḍuttiralāga tammutirvarumene nā
māḍuvamebannimembudu
māḍuva bage bandu nettamaṁ dharmasutaṁ // ViVi.70 [kandaṁ]

karedoḍe jūdiṁgaṁ dhura
bhara[kākhēṭa]kkebhūbhujaṅgāgadu me
ygarediralemba purātana
guruvacanaṁ tanage niṭṭepaṭṭudaṟindaṁ // ViVi.71 [kandaṁ]

antu pūḍikoṇḍu nāḻavāsageyanikkalvēḻvuduṁ śakuni munne tanna māḍida
nāḻavāsagegaḷanarasāḷante kaṇṇaṟidu meṭṭi maṭṭamaṟidikkuvāgaloḍḍamaṁ pēḻimene
[p. 166]
poḻtupōgiṅgamaḻtigamāḍuva tammutirvaruṁ palagege sāyira gadyāṇada ponnē
sālgumaggaḷaṁ bēḍendu duryōdhananokkalaṁ puḍiyoḷ poraḷcuvante
pāsaṅgeyaṁ poraḷci munnaṁ nettamanaṟiyadanantavara dāyamanāḍe
maḍimaḍiguṟuvudu[mo]ndu patteṇṭu palageyaṁmeḷpaḍisalendu sōltu
sōladoḷēvayisiyinnoḍḍaṅkoḷḷimendu—

palagege pattu sāyirame gadyaṇamendiradoḍḍi tāmera
ḻvalageyanāḍi sōltoḍe suyōdhananēvade dharmaputranaṁ
kuladhana saṅkulaṅgaḷane tandiḍeyiṭṭavanāḍi sōltanā
kula mati munde bhāratadoḷoḍḍuvudaṁ kaḍu nanni māḻpavōl // ViVi.72 [campakamāle]

antu kāḷiṅgāṅga vana sambhavaṅgaḷappa madāndha gandha sindhuraṅgaḷumanā
jānēya kāmbhōja bhūmijaṅgaḷappa jātyaśvaṅgaḷumanoḍḍidāgaḷ duryōdhanaṁ
bandikāṟanante seṟegeyduṁ vraṇavaidyanante koḍasāriyaṁ piḍiduṁ sūḷeyante
kaḻivuḻivanaṟiduṁ rasavādiyante ....... kaṭṭiyuṁ perjōḍeyante nuṇṇitaṁ
vēḻduvaṇugāḷante dāyambaḍedu[ṁ]mēḷadaṅkadante suḻiyaḻidu[ṁ]ḍombara
kōḍagadantāḍi geldāgaḷ tammaṇṇana sōlamaṁ kaṇḍāgaḷ bhīmasēnanintendaṁ—

bhayamaṟiyada kaliyuṁ cā
giyumenisade nāḍe lōbhiyuṁ pandeyumā
giye bāḻvaṅgallade sū
ḷeya kaṇ pāsageya kaṇṇumēnuṟugugumē // ViVi.73 [kandaṁ]

endu kaype saraṁ berasu nuḍida bhīmasēnana nuḍigaḷ kiḍigaḷante tanna
manamanonaliseyumerdeyaṁ kanaliseyumēnumennade muntaṇa kajjamane
bagedusiradirda duryōdhananallige gāṅgēyanuṁ viduranuṁ bandu—


[p. 167]
sālade jūdu nimmoḷagidēṁ gaḷa māṇisimendoḍanya bhū
pāla kirīṭa tāṭita padaṁ yamanandananajja nāḍeyuṁ
sōladoḷādamēvayisideṁ nuḍiginneḍeyilla pōgimā
tmālayakendoḍēnumēnalaṇmade bārisalaṇmadirvaruṁ // ViVi.74 [utpalamālike]

dhr̥tarāṣṭranallige pōgi—

ninage magaṁ purākr̥tada karmame puṭṭuvavōle puṭṭi ni
mminibarumaṁ rasātaḷadoḷaḻdidapaṁ page polla pāṇḍu naṁ
danaroḷahīndrakētanana jūdina gellamadentuṭenna naṁ
jina saviyantuṭendoḍinisantadoḷantakanalligaṭṭuguṁ // ViVi.75 [campakamāle]

puruḍisikoṇḍīgaḷ nī
narasina garvadoḷe bīgi beseyade maganaṁ
karedoppisavēḻa yudhi
ṣṭhiraṅge mun gelda vastuvāhana cayamaṁ // ViVi.76 [kandaṁ]

endu mattamintendar‌—

kadana prārambha śauṇḍaṁ ripu nr̥paba[la dā]vānalaṁvairi bhūbhr̥
nmadavanmātaṅgakumbhasthaḷa daḷa na[kha]rōgrāsi pañcāsya dhairyaṁ

ydidiroḷ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ hariganire bigurtāmpanantāva gaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.77 [mahāsragdhare]

kādudusaraṇgevandara

endenitānu teṟadoḷe sāṟiyuṁ kīṟiyuṁ nuḍidoḍe dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ

vyāḷa gajaṅgaḷanaggada
sūḷeyarokkalananarghya vastugaḷaniḷā
pāḷaṁ sōltoḍe jūdina
kēḷiyanā kēḷi[ya]nitaṟoḷ māṇisidar // ViVi.3 [kandaṁ]

māṇisidoḍe māṇade rapaṇamaṁ tōṟiyumotteyanuggaḍisiyumāḍi
mane peṟatēnumupāyamillademmāḷva nelanotteyendoḍe bagedu nōḍi geldiṁ
baḻiyaṁ mudugaṇgaḷ maguḻe kuḍisuvaremba bageyoḷaṁ vikramārjunanuṁ
bhīmanu yamaḷarumeḻedukoḷvaremba saṅkeyoḷamantaltu ninna nanniyoḷaṁ
varṣāvadhiyoḷallade nelananotteviḍiyenendoḍe dharmaputraṁ panneraḍu varuṣambaraṁ
nāḍaṁ pugadaraṇyadoḷirpantumajñātavāsamendondu varuṣadoḷārānu
[p. 169]
maṟidarappoḍe mattaṁ dvādaśābdambaraṁ nāḍa deseyaṁ nōḍadantāgeyonde
palageyoḷe gellasōlamappantu nanni nuḍidu nelananotteyiṭṭāḍi—

ā palageyumaṁ sōltu ma
hipati caladiṁ baḻikke sōltaṁ gaḍamā
draupadiyumanēnāgado
pāpada phaḷameydevanda devasadoḷārgaṁ // ViVi.4 [kandaṁ]

antu duryōdhananajātaśatruvina sarvasvamellamaṁ geldu gelda kasavaramellaṁ
bandudu pāñcāḷarāja tanūjeyorvaḷ bandaḷillākeyaṁ tannimendu yudhiṣṭhiraṁ
koṭṭa nanniya baladoḷ tanage layamilladudanaṟidu mēgillada goḍḍāṭamāḍal
bagedu karṇana leṅkaṁ prātikāmiyembanumaṁ tanna tammaṁ duśyāsananumaṁ
pēḻdoḍavandirāgaḷe bīḍiṅge varidu rajasvaleyāgirdeṁ muṭṭalāgadeneyumottaṁ
badindoḷagaṁ pokku pāñcāḷiyaṁ kaṇgiḍe jaḍidu muḍiyaṁ piḍidu tanmadhyadiṁ
suyōdhanana sabhāmadhyakke tandu—

manadoḷ nondamarāpagāsuta kr̥pa drōṇādigaḷ bēḍavē
ḍeneyuṁ māṇade toḻte toḻtuvesakey pō pōgu nīnendu ba
ydenitānuṁ tēṟadiṁdamuṭṭuduvaraṁkeydandu duśyāsanaṁ
tanagaṁ mellane mr̥tyu sāre tegedaṁ dhammillamaṁ kr̥ṣṇeyā // ViVi.5 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu kr̥ṣṇeya kr̥ṣṇa kabarī bhāramaṁ mēgillade piḍidu tegedu kr̥ṣṇōraganaṁ
piḍida beḷḷāḷantummane bemaruttumirda duśyāsananumaṁ kaṇketti kiṟunage naguva
kūradaramogamumaṁ tammaṇṇana binnanāda mogamumaṁ kaṇḍu kaṇgaḷiṁ nettar
tuḷuṅke—

kōpada percinoḷ naḍuguvūruyugaṁ kaḍupindaralva nā
sāpuṭamekkeyiṁ poḍarva purvu podaḷda layāntakatriśū
lōpama bhīṣaṇa bhrukuṭi munname raudra gadāyudhambaraṁ
pōpa bhujārgaḷaṁ ripugaḷa grahamādudu bhīmasēnanā // ViVi.6 [utpalamālike]


[p. 170]
nelanaṁ nuṅguva mēruvaṁ piḍidu kīḻvāśāgajēndraṅgaḷaṁ
caladiṁ kaṭṭuva sapta saptiyaniḷābhāgakke tarpondu tō
ḷvalamuṁ garvamumuṇmi poṇme manadoḷ kōpāgni keygaṇmika
ṇmalaroḷ bandirenōḍidaṁ kaluṣadiṁ gāṇḍīvi gāṇḍīvamaṁ // ViVi.7 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

prakupita mr̥gapati śiśu sa
nnikāśarati vikaṭa bhīṣaṇa bhrū bhaṅgar
nakulasahadēvarirvaru
makāla kālāgni rūpamaṁ keykoṇḍar // ViVi.8 [kandaṁ]

antu viḷaya kāla jaḷanidhigaḷante mēredappal bageda tanna nālvar
tammandira munida mogamaṁ kaṇḍu tanna nuḍida nanniya kēḍaṁ bagedarendu kaṭākṣa
vikṣēpadiṁ bārise—

anitondurkinoḷurki kaurava khaḷar pāñcāḷarājātmajā
nana padmaglapanaika kāraṇaparer tāmāgeyuṁ mattama
ṇṇana kaṇsannege mīṟalaṇmadesamantirdar pr̥thāputraraṁ
tinitondādoḍamēṁ mahāpuruṣarājñālaṅghanaṁ geyvarē // ViVi.9 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ draupadi tanna kēśapāśamaṁ duśyāsanaṁ piḍidu tegedanemba siggaggaḷaṁ
perce sabheyoḷintendaḷ—

muḍiyaṁ piḍideḻedavanaṁ
maḍiyisi mattavana karuḷa piṇilindennaṁ
muḍiyisuvinegaṁmuḍiyaṁ
muḍiyeṁ gaḍa kēḷimīgaḷān[nuḍi]nuḍideṁ // ViVi.10 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ bhīmasēnanā mātaṁ kēḷdu sairisalāṟade—


[p. 171]
āṟada kōpa pāvakaninaṇṇana nanniyanilli mīṟuveṁ
mīṟenenuttumirpa padadalliye nōḍa maruḷgedhūpamaṁ
tōṟida māḻkeyiṁ drupadarājasutā vacanaṅgaḷalli me
ydōṟe marutsutaṁ nuḍidanā sabheyoḷ navamēghanādadiṁ // ViVi.11 [utpalamālike]

muḷisindaṁ nuḍidondu ninna nuḍisalgārāgadembar mahā
praḷayōlkōpama madgadā hatiyinatyugrājiyoḷ munnamī
khaḷa duśyāsananaṁ poraḷci basiṟaṁ pōḻdikki bambalgaru
ḷgaḷinānalte viḷāsadiṁ muḍiyipeṁ paṅkējapatrēkṣaṇē // ViVi.12 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

kuḍiveṁ duśyāsanōrasthaḷamanagale pōḻdārdu kennettaraṁ po
kkuḍiveṁ piṅgākṣanūrudvayamanurugadā ghātadiṁ nuccu nūṟā
goḍeveṁ tadratna raśmi prakaṭa makuṭamaṁ nambu nambenna kaṇṇiṁ
kiḍiyuṁ keṇḍaṅgaḷuṁ sūsidapuvahitaraṁ nōḍi paṅkējavaktrē // ViVi.13 [mahāsragdhare]

muḷisaṁ māḍiyumēvamaṁ paḍeduminnī pandegaḷ prāṇadiṁ
doḷarinnuṁ tale mattamaṭṭegaḷa mēlirdappuvendante dal
muḷisillaṇṇana nanniyembudane pēḻēvēḻdumī kaurava
rkaḷanuntinnegamurci mukkade saḍildī bhīmanēṁ māṇgumē // ViVi.14 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu pāñcāḷarājatanūjeya manamanāṟe nuḍidu mattamintendaṁ—

surasindhu priya putra kēḷ kaḷaśajā nīṁ kēḷ kr̥pā kēḷa maṁ
daradindambudhiyaṁ kalaṅkidasura pradhvaṁsivōl bāhu maṁ
daradiṁ vairi balābdhi ghūrṇise bigurtī kauravar kūḍe nū
rvarumaṁ kolvenidenna pūṇke nuḍideṁ nimmī sabhāmadhyadoḷ // ViVi.15 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 172]
endu viḷaya kāḷa jaḷadhara ninādadiṁgiritāṭisidantānuṁ nelaṁ
moḻagidantānuṁ gajaṟi garjisi nuḍidu mahāpratijñārūḍhanāda bhīmasēnana
nuḍiyaṁ kēḷdu kauravar kaḍala naḍuvaṇa parvatadantaḷḷāḍe kuruvr̥ddhanuṁ
buddhivr̥ddhanumappa gāṅgēyaṁ dhr̥tarāṣṭraṅgintendaṁ—

bharata yayāti kutsa purukutsa purūravarindaminnegaṁ
pariviḍiyinde banda śaśivaṁśamadīgaḷivandirinde ni
ttarisuvudakkumende bagedirdoḍe kīloḷe kiccu puṭṭi bhō
rgareduridante ninna maganinduridattidanāro bāripar // ViVi.16 [campakamāle]

endaḻaldu dhr̥tarāṣṭranoḷ nuḍiye kumbhasambhavāśvatthāma kr̥pa vidurādi
gaḷ nīmenitu nuḍidoḍamāneya kōḍu bāgadembante duryōdhananudvr̥tta
teyumaṁ bhīmasēnana mahāpratijñeyumanārgaṁ bārisalbāradu keygaḻida
manevāḻte buddhivēḻaleḍeyilla tāmuṁ tāmumaṟivar bannimendu nija
nivāsaṅgaḷge pōdarāgaḷ bhīmasēnaṁ dharmaputraṅgendanuppikkidoḍe tuppada
meḷpaḍitembante namma kemmanirpiravidē kāraṇaṁ banniṁ pōpamendaramaneyaṁ
poṟamaṭṭu bare dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ duryōdhananēgeydumoḍambaḍisalāṟadireyuṁ
draupadi parastrīyaṁ namma maneyoḷirisuvuducitamallendu kaḻipidoḍe
pāñcāḷarāja tanūjeverasu binna binnane poḻalaṁ poṟamaḍe purajanaṅgaḷellaṁ
neredavara pōgiṅge sairisalāṟade tammoḷintendar—

ēdoreyaṁ yamanandana
nēdoreyaṁ bhīmasēnanēdoreyaṁ kaṁ
jōdarana maidunaṁ tā
mēdoreyaramaḷgaḷavargamī yiravāytē // ViVi.17 [kandaṁ]

jūdāḍi sōltu nannige
mēdiniyaṁ koṭṭu pāṇḍunandanarīgaḷ
pōdoḍamēn tiṇukāgade
pōdapudē namma nr̥patigavu tavudaleyoḷ // ViVi.18 [kandaṁ]


[p. 173]
jūdina gelladoḷādī
mēdiniyaṁ kaṇḍu kajjamaṁ kāṇade du
jjōdananadēnadēṁ maru
ḷādano baḍigaṁḍanillapālane kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.19 [kandaṁ]

enitānumandadiṁ jū
danikkeyuṁ drupadasuteyaneḻeduyyeyumiṁ
tinitondādudu duśyā
sananindaṁ śakuniyemba beḷpoṟasindaṁ // ViVi.20 [kandaṁ]

endirdarirdalliye tantamma kaṇḍudane nuḍiyeyuṁ kelaravara
pōgiṅgaḻaldu kaṇṇa nīranikkeyuṁ kelar parasi sēseyanikkeyuṁ poḻalaṁ poṟamaṭṭu
purada bāhigeyaneyduvāgaḷ gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pavidurādigaḷ kontiveraseyde
vandu kiṟidantaramaṁ kaḷiputtuṁ bare dharmaputranemage takka buddhiyaṁ pēḻdu
maguḻimendoḍanibaruṁ manaṁbandhisida mōhadiṁ gaḻagaḻane kaṇṇa nīrgaḷaṁ
suridu—

puguvudaraṇyamirpiravu panneraḍabdamadalladallikō
ḻmigada vanēcarādhipara dāyigarattaṇinappapāya kō
ṭige pavaṇilla kalpigeḍeyāvudo pāḻiya baṭṭedappi muṁ
negaḻdeḍeyilla pōgu jayamakke śubhaṁ nimagakke maṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.21 [campakamāle]

endoḍallirdu nimma manakke kokkarikkeyāgiyuṁ pāḻige geṇṭāgiyuṁ
negaḻvamallendu poḍavaṭṭu kontiyaṁ vidurana maneyoḷiralvēḻdu
subhadreyanabhimanyuverasu nārāyaṇanallige dvārāvatige kaḷipi nija parijanamberasu
gaṅgeyaṁ pāydadaṟa paḍuvaṇa deseya kāmyakavanada baṭṭeyaṁ taguḷdu pōge
vōge—

dese pasurēṟi pacceyoḷe mucci musuṅkida māḻkeyādudā
gasamaḷinīḷa nīḷa gaḷakaṇṭha tamāḷa vinīḷa nīrada

[p. 174]
prasara vibhāsiyādudu samīranudāra kadamba kētakī
prasara rajasvara prakaṭapāṁsuḷamādudu mēghakāladoḷ // ViVi.22 [campakamāle]

kariya mugilgaḷiṁ gaganamaṇḍaḷamoppire sōgeyiṁ vanāṁ
taramesedoppe tōrpa moḷevulgaḷinī dharaṇī vibhāgamo
ppire posa vēṭakāṟarerdegaḷ posa kārapoḍarpugaṇḍadēṁ
karituvadēṁ kalaṅkiduvadēṁ kuḻigoṇḍuvadēṁ kanalduvō // ViVi.23 [campakamāle]

adalladeyuṁ—

bhava lālāṭavilōcanāgni śikheyiṁ bendaḷki mattaṁ manō
bhavaneḻcattoḍe kāma kānte baḻiyaṁ tannicceyiṁ mecci ba
ṇṇavuraṁ tīvida māḻkeyāytu naviliṁkundaṅgaḷindindragō
paviḷāsaṅgaḷinālikalla paraliṁ kāroḷ mahīmaṇḍalaṁ // ViVi.24 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

poḷevamarēndragōpada pasurteḷavulgaḷa taḷta kārmugi
lgaḷa kiṟugoṅku goṅkida ponalgaḷa kempu pasurpu karpu be
ḷpoḷakoḷe śakra kārmuka viḷāsamanēnerdegoṇḍu bēṭada
ttaḷagamanuṇṭumāḍidudo kāmana kārmukadante kārmukaṁ // ViVi.25 [campakamāle]

antu tamagidiraṁ barpante banda payōdhara kāladoḷeraḍu taḍiyumaṁ
poydu pariva toṟegaḷumaṁ tovaltu sogayisuvaḍavigaḷumaṁ pasiyanētramaṁ
paccavaḍisidante pasurpuvaḍeda neladoḷpadmarāgada paralgaḷaṁ baligedaṟidante
upāśrayambaḍedaḷaṅkarisuvindragōpaṅgaḷumaṁ kisugāḍa nelaṅgaḷeḷadaḷira baṇṇamaṁ
keykoṇḍu virahigaḷa manamanolisuvante jala jalane parivajarivonalgaḷumaṁ
kaṇḍu tamma kaṇgaṁ manakaṁ sogayise payaṇaṁ bandu kāmyaka vanamaṁ
pugutandaradentendoḍe—


[p. 175]
desegettaṁ gajaṟuttumirpa puliyiṁ nīḷābhramaṁ dantige
ttu siḍildāgasakeyde pāyva palavuṁ siṅgaṅgaḷindettagu
rvisi pāyvarvigaḷiṁ madāndhavanagandhēbhaṅgaḷiṁ kaṇgagu
rviseyuṁ cittadoḷandu kāmyakavanaṁ māḍittati prītiyaṁ // ViVi.26 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu saumyabhayaṅkarākāramappa kāmyakavanamaṁ pugutandalli
tadvanādhipatiyappa daityaṁ kimmīranavaraṁ pugalīyadaḍḍamāgire—

masiyaṁ puñjisidantuṭappa tanu nīḷāmbhōdharaṁ dāḍegaḷ
posa miñcugra vilōcanaṁ divija gōpaṁ kāro mēṇ kāḷa ra
kkasanō pēḻene bandu tāge gadeyaṁ koṇḍeyde bhīmaṁ siḍi
ldu siḍil poydavolāge poydaniḷeyoḷ kimmīranaṁ vīranaṁ // ViVi.27 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu kimmīranaṁ kondu kāmyakavanamaṁ pokku tadvana tapōdhanara
gōṣṭhiyoḷamāṭavikaraṭṭaṭṭiyoḷaṁ tamagindraprasthada rājyaśrīyaṁ masuḷise—

piriya maraṅgaḷe māḍamāge poḷeveḷadaḷirgaḷe sejjeyāge
piriya maḍugaḷe majjanamāge posa nāre dēvāṅga vastramāge
pareda taṟageleya pariyaṇamāge paṇpalamettida bōnamāge
siriya mahimeyaṁ meṟeyalēnārtudo banadoḷirpiravā pāṇḍavarā // ViVi.28 [piriyakkaraṁ]

pāsaṟe siṁhapīṭhamaḷinī ruti maṅgaḷa gīti bhūtaḷaṁ
pāsu mr̥gavrajaṁ parijanaṁ podaṟōlagasāle mokkaḷaṁ
bīsuva gāḷi cāmarada gāḷiyenal dorevettadēṁ sukhā
vāsa nimittavāyto vanavāsanivāsame pāṇḍuputrarā // ViVi.29 [utpalamālike]

antu kāmyakavanadoḷaydu varuṣamirdāṟaneya varuṣadoḷadaṟa
keladoḷondi sandisi gaganataḷamaṁ taṟumbuvantirda śikhariśikharaṅgaḷindaṁ desegaḷaṁ
taḍavarisi koḷvante baḷvaḷa baḷedu sogayisuva permaraṅgaḷindaṁ vanalakṣmiya
[p. 176]
gōmaṇḍaladantirda kaḍavina kāḍermeya piṇḍugaḷindaṁ desegaḷgeberci
mūṅkiṟiva vanamahiṣigaḷiṁ madahastiyante maravāyva puligaḷinati bhayaṅkarākāra
mappa dvaitavanakke bandu tadvanōpa kaṇṭhavartigaḷappa tāpasāśramaṅgaḷoḷ
viśramisal bagedu—

pugalillī banamārgamimbu nelasal nāruṇṭuḍal melle kōṁ
bugaḷoḷ paṇbalamuṇṭumīye kuḍiyalnīruṇṭu padmākarā
ḷigaḷoḷ taṇpugaḷuṇṭu hēmalatikā kuñjaṅgaḷoḷnamma na
nnige bannaṁ baralīyadī banadoḷirdēṁ kālamaṁ pārevē // ViVi.30 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

enda tammoḷayvarumēka kāryāḷōcanapararāgi daitavanadoḷadvaita
sāhasarirpannegamondu divasaṁ duryōdhanana maydunaṁ sindhudēśādhīśvaraṁ
saindhavanavaraṁ chidrisalendu meygaredu bandu—

mr̥gayā krīḍege pāṇḍurāja tanayar‌ pōpannegaṁ bandu to
ṭṭage pāñcāḷiyanetti tanna rathadoḷ tandiṭṭukoṇḍuydana
nnegamantā paḍemātugēḷdatibaḷar bhīmārjunar kāypu ke
ymige bennaṁ paridetta pōpeyelavō pō pōgalendeydidar // ViVi.31 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

anteydi tadgadāghātadoḷaṁ bāṇapātadoḷamavana rathamaṁ śata cūrṇaṁ
māḍi jayadrathanaṁ kōḍugagaṭṭugaṭṭi bennaṁ billa koppinoḷiṟidu naḍeyendu
naḍeyisi pāñcāḷiyaṁ līleyindoḍagoṇḍu bīḍiṅge vandu dharmaputraṅge
tōṟidoḍe—

lākṣāgr̥hamaṁ pugisalu
makṣakrīḍeyoḷe dharaṇiyaṁkoḷaluṁpiṁ
gākṣaṅge vēḻdu sairisa
dākṣēpadinemmanilli chidrisa bandai // ViVi.32 [kandaṁ]


[p. 177]
endu ninna[ṁ]paribhavakke tandu ninna yaśamaṁ kiḍisidevin kondoḍēvaṁ
dapudendu duryōdhananallige pōgendu kaṭṭida kaṭṭugaḷaṁ biṭṭu kaḷedoḍe
jayadrathaṁ siggāgi kailāsadoḷīśvaraṅge tapaṅgeydu meccisi pāṇḍavaranondu
devasadanuvaradoḷ gelvenakkendu barambaḍedu pōdanitta duryōdhanaṁ samasta
sādhana sahitanāgi kāḍoḷ bēḍarante toḻalva dāyigara kandi kundida mogaṅgaḷaṁ
nōḍuvudumennanavariṁ nōḍisuvudumīyeraḍe saṁsāra phalamendu nāgapuradiṁ
poṟamaṭṭu duśyāsanādigaḷappa nūrvar tammandiruṁ bhānumatiyuṁ candramati
yumemba bēṭadarasiyaruṁ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvar makkaḷuṁ gāṅgēya
drōṇa kr̥pa vidura prabhr̥tigaḷumaśvatthāma karṇa śalya śakuni saindhava pramukha
nāyakaruṁ berasu bēṇṭeya nevadiṁ bandu dvaitavanada kelada nandana vanadoḷ
pāṇḍavarge samīpamāge bīḍaṁ biṭṭu pāḍisuttaṁ pogaḻisuttumirdanannegaṁ
pageyiṟiyabandara mūganaridarembantanibaruṁ bāyaṁ biṭṭu nōḍe nōḍe
pūrvajanmada page citrāṅgadanemba gandharvanaṟuvattukōṭi gāndharvabalaṁ berasu
bandu duryōdhana duśyāsanarirvarumaṁ kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi—

miḍukade bhīṣma nōḍutiru kumbhaja surkiru karṇa mikku mā
rnuḍiyade mūguvaṭṭiru guru priyanandana kūgaḍaṅgadi
rdoḍe bardukāvudir poḍardoḍīgaḍe kondapenendu kūḍe ka
ṇgiḍe jaḍiduydanā khacaranirvarumaṁ paramāṇumārgadiṁ // ViVi.33 [campakamāle]

antuyvuduṁ negaḻteya bīrarellaṁ baḍavara pitararante miḷmiḷa nōḍuttire

endu gadādaṇḍamaṁ bhujādaṇḍadoḷaḷavaḍisikoṇḍu pagevarirda

antu nabhōvibhāgadiṁ dharāvibhāgakkiḻitanda kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyananaṁ

rvandu dharātaḷa niṣṭha lalāṭa paṭṭaṁ sāṣṭāṅgaveṟagi poḍavaṭṭu tadīyāśīrvāda

gaḷaṁ padmapatra puṭaṅgaḷiṁ tandu padapadmaṅgaḷaṁ karci tatpāda pavitrōdakaṁ

adu kāraṇadindavaraṁ gelvāgaḷ vikramārjunanallade gellanadaṟindātaṅge

aḷi biridirda jādiyoḷe palmoreyuttire haṁse pūta pū

puḷiyoḷ karcida bāḷa baṇṇamane pōlvākāśamākāśamaṁ
ḍaḷamaṁ parvida beḷmugil mugila beḷpoḷpokku taḷpoyye ba

ṇgoḷisittormeye bandudandu śaradaṁ lōkakke kaṇ barpinaṁ // ViVi.71 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ vijayaṁ tanna vijayaśrīya baraviṅgidirvandantebanda
śaratkālaśrīyanutkaṇṭhita hr̥dayanāgi mecci nōḍuttuṁ barpannegaṁmundeśārada

vidaḷatkunda śaśāṅka śaṅkha dhavaḷaṁ gandhēbha dānāmbu pū
rṇa darī sundarakandaraṁ mr̥gapati pradhvāna garjadguhaṁ
madirōnmatta niḷimpa kimpuruṣa kāntārabdha saṅgītamo
ppidudaltē sura siddha dampati ratiśrī ramyahaimācaḷaṁ // ViVi.72 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

laḷitōtsava dhvajāṁśuka
viḷasanamaṁ munde ninage tōrpantire ka
ṇgoḷisirdudu nōḍa himā
caḷa śikharada mēle pāyva gaṅgāsrōtraṁ // ViVi.73 [kandaṁ]

endu guhyakaṁ himavanmahīdharamaṁ tōṟuttuṁ bandu kailāsa parvatamaṁ
kaṇḍu—


[p. 187]
idu kailāsaṁ bhavānīdhavana nele manōjātanaṁ būdimāḍi
ttidaṟoḷ dakṣādhvara dhvaṁsakana nosala kaṇṇāta[noḷ]tanna dōrga

ttidoḍittaṁmecci laṅkādhipatige baravaṁ rāgadiṁ nīḷakaṇṭhaṁ // ViVi.74 [mahāsragdhare]

toṟe toṟeyemba mātanananitilladoḍāṁ toṟevendalendoḍā
toṟeyoḷe pōytu sūruḷene sūruḷavēvuvo nambenembuduṁ
kaṟegoralātanātma viṭa tattvamanuṇṭoḍetāgi māḍi bāṁ
doṟeyane pottu gaurige ka[va]ldoṟegeysidanī pradēśadoḷ // ViVi.75 [campakamāle]

endu guhyakaṁ kailāsa śailadelleḍegaḷumaṁ vikramārjunaṅge tōṟuttuṁ
bandu—

sāḷa tamāḷa kānana bharōddhata sindhura kaṇṭha garjanā
bhīḷamanambarēcara vadhū karapallava sañcaḷallatāṁ
dōḷamanāśritādri nada kūḷamanatyadharīkr̥tā nyaku
tkīḷamanindukāntasusalīḷamaneydidanindrakīḷamaṁ // ViVi.76 [utpalamālike]

kamaḷāntargata gandha bandhu nayadiṁ bandappikoḷvante gā
ḷi manaṅgoṇḍire tīḍe bhr̥ṅgarutigaḷ māṅgalya gēyaṅgaḷaṁ
damanandīyē maḍaltu pūta lategaḷ keygeydupūnīḍalka
rghyamanīvantevolādudadri harigaṅgiṣṭārtha saṁsiddhiyaṁ // ViVi.77 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ guhyakanindra sutananindrakīla nagēndrada candrakāntaśilātala
doḷiḻipi bīḷkoṇḍu pōdanitta vikramārjunaṁ parantapaṁ tapōniyama
niyamitanāgi—


[p. 188]
bhasitaṁ karpūra kāḷāgaru bahuḷa rajaṁ valkalaṁ kalpavr̥kṣa
prasavaṁ yajñōpavītaṁ kanaka kamaḷanāḷōtkaraṁ niccaniccaṁ

dhisitudyadbhakti bhārānata vanavanitāvr̥ndamānandadindaṁ // ViVi.78 [mahāsragdhare]

adirada cittamaḷkada manaṁ bagegoḷḷada mōhametti ka
