odavida ninnadondu daye mēṇ piridō negaḻdenna gaṇḍumā
dadaṭumaḷurkeyuṁ pirido sandeyamādapudintidilli tū
gidoḍaṟiyalke bāradadu kāraṇadiṁ ripu bhūpa danti daṁ
tada toleyoḷ parākramadinennane bhūpati tūgi tōṟenē // ViVi.40 [campakamāle]

endu tanna seraguṁ beragumillada kalitanamanaṟiye nuḍidaṁ matta
mondeḍeyoḷorva vīrabhaṭanudāra vīrarasa rasikanāgi—

kudureyanēṟidamberasu sauḷene vōgirepoydumeyde ka
ṭṭidiroḷe nūṅkidānegaḷa kōḍugaḷaṁbaḷevōge poydumāṁ
tadaṭaranondevoydumeraḍuṁ balamennane nōḍe takkine
nnadaṭamanenna vīramumanājiyoḷennarasaṅge tōṟuveṁ // ViVi.41 [campakamāle]

endatirabhasa raṇavyasanamanātmīyaśāsanāyattaṁ māḍidaṁ mattorvana
tyugra maṇḍaḷāgramananugeydu vīragraha grastanāgi—

siḍiloḷe taḷtu pōrva siḍilantire bāḷoḷe bāḷ‌ paḷañci mā
rkiḍiviḍe nōḍalañji desedēvategaḷ peṟapiṅge tōḷa tīn
kiḍenalidonderaḻkudureyaṭṭeyumonderaḍāneyaṭṭeyuṁ
toḍardoḍanāḍetaḷtiṟiyadirdoḍe jōḷamanentu nīguveṁ // ViVi.42 [campakamāle]

endu nijabhuja vijayamanappukeydu nuḍidaṁ mattōrvanalliye—

suralōkaṁ dorekoḷvudondu parama śrī lakṣmiyuṁ barpudā
daradiṁ dēvanikāyadoḷ nerevudondutsāhamuṁ tanna me

[p. 258]
ysiri bhāgyaṁ neramappudonde raṇadoḷ geldājiyaṁtaḷtusaṁ
garadoḷ jōḷada pāḻiyaṁ nerapidaṁ gaṇḍaṁ peṟaṁ gaṇḍanē // ViVi.43 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

[endu nuḍidaṁ]—

tave māṟānta balaṁ kaṟuttiṟidu tannāḷdaṁ karaṁ mecce ge
ldavanaṁ śrīvadhu pattuguṁ maḍidanaṁ dēvāṅganānīkamu
tsavadinduygumadentumimbusubhaṭaṅgintappudaṁ kaṇḍumaṁ
juvanēkañjuvanendu perci nuḍidaṁ mattorvanāsthānadoḷ // ViVi.44 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu nuḍideraḍuṁ balaṅgaḷuṁ tantamma vīramaṁ cāgamaṁ meṟedu
tamma keydugaḷanarcisi darbhaśayanaṁ māḍi pallaṁ sulidu śastrasaṅgraharāgi
palaruṁ vīrabhaṭar tammaṁ tāme paricchēdisirdaratta mattamorvaṁ tanna
nallaḷoḷintendanī poḻte poḻtu nāḷe dēvalōkada kanyakeyarōlagadoḷirpe
nendu nuḍiye nīnendantu pōgal‌ tīradu nāḷe maguḻdu bandennoḷ
nereveyendu pēḻe ninagaṟivuṇṭe endu kēḷiyennōlevāgya muṇṭendaḷ
mattamondeḍeyoḷorvaḷ darbhaśayanasthanāda nija prāṇēśvarana
paricchēdamanaṟidu tanna sāvaṁ paricchēdisi—

tāṁ gaḍa nāḷe pōgi divijāṅganeyoḷ toḍardirpanilli mā
ṇdāṁ gaḍamirpenantanitubeḷḷene munname pōgi nalmege
llaṅgoḷe dēvalōkadoḷadhīśananānidirgoḷvenōvo sa
ggaṅgaḷoḷirpa dēvaḍiti toḻtiroḷaḻtiyanāgalīvenē // ViVi.45 [utpalamālike]

endu kaidavamillada nalmeyiṁ nālageya tudige tandu nuḍidaḷ
mattorvaḷ tannāṇmana dōrvaladagurvaṁ nacci—

jaḷadhiyoḷāda muttugaḷavēṁ posatāduve ninna tōḷa bā
ḷoḷe bala garvadiṁ tegedudagra virōdhi madēbhamastaka
sthaḷa jaḷarāśiyoḷ baḷeda nirmaḷa nirvraṇa vr̥ttamauktikā
vaḷiyane tarpudendu nuḍidaḻkaṟoḷāṟisidaḷ nijēśanaṁ // ViVi.46 [campakamāle]


[p. 259]
antubhaya balaṅgaḷoḷaṁ vīrajanajanitāḷāpaṅgaḷ negaḻe vikramārjuna
nanantanuṁ tānuṁ jalakkanire pallaṁ sulidagaṇya puṇya tīrthōdakaṅgaḷaṁ mindu
maṅgaḷavasadanaṅgoṇḍu sāmānya yajñaṅgeydu palavuṁ teṟada paṟegaḷeseye
nāndī mukhamaṁ nirvartisi śubha lakṣaṇa lakṣitanuṁ sannāha karmanirmitanuṁ
hastāyudha kuśaḷanuṁ bhadramananumappa vijaya gajamu manakṣayarathāśva kētana
śarāsana śaradhi vicitra tanutra vividhāstra śastraṅgaḷumaṁ gandha dhūpa
dīpādigaḷindarcisi poḍevaṭṭāgaḷ—

beḷaguva soḍargaḷa beḷaguma
niḷisi taḻattaḻisi poḷeye tammaya beḷaga
ggaḷisi taḻataḻisi vidyu
dviḷasitamenisiduvu narana divyāstraṅgaḷ // ViVi.47 [kandaṁ]

soḍarguḍiya kempinoḷ keṁ
piḍidire ripu nr̥pati balada śōṇita jaḷamaṁ
kuḍiyadeyuṁ dal munname
kuḍidantesedirduvariganastracayaṅgaḷ // ViVi.48 [kandaṁ]

antāyiruḷaṁ vijayaṁ vijayōdyōgadoḷ kaḷeye beḷagappa
jāvadoḷ bīḍuvīḍugaḷgellaṁ toḻaldēkirpirēḻiṁ paṇṇimene—

taṇḍade kīṟi sāṟuva palar paḍevaḷḷara mātugaḷ manaṁ
goṇḍiresannaṇanduḍuva paṇṇuva bāḻteyavandiraṁ maru
ḷgoṇḍavolūḷva baggisuva bēgadoḷā kaṭakaṅgaḷeyde ke
ykoṇḍuvu mandara kṣubhita dugdhapayōdhi gabhīranādamaṁ // ViVi.49 [utpalamālike]

kr̥ta vividhāstra vīrabhaṭa kōṭi bhayaṅkaramāgebīsuvā
vutiya kaḷaṅka paṅkadoḷe percida kaḻtale tīvra śastra saṁ
hatigaḷa dīptiyiṁ bisugeyāgi karaṁ pogarvaṭṭagurvuma
dbhutamumanīye paṇṇiduvu pāṇḍava kaurava raudra sādhanaṁ // ViVi.50 [campakamāle]

anteraḍuṁ paḍegaḷuṁ paṇṇapaṇṇane paṇṇi kāḷegakke naḍeyaloḍarisi
dāgaḷ—


[p. 260]
lōkaika cakṣu nava kama
lākara bāndhavananēka ditisuta samarā
nīka bhayaṅkaraneraḍuma
nīkaṅgaḷanaḍare nōḍuvantudayisidaṁ // ViVi.51 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷēṟisidabisugegaḷumikkida lōhavakkaregaḷumurcida
mogavaḍaṅgaḷuṁ kaṭṭida paḻayigegaḷumoṭṭida mūvatteraḍāyudhaṅgaḷuṁ
beraseṟaṅkeverasida kulagirigaḷe taḷarvante taḷarva madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷumaṁ
cakra cītkr̥ta nādadoḷ dikcakramumaṁcakraghātadoḷ dharācakra manākramisi
niśāta hēti garbhaṅgaḷumanēka prakāra kētana vājirājigaḷumāgidommaḷisinaḍeva rathaṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇṇuṁ khuramaṁ tōṟe pakkareyikki poḷeva ponna
paryāṇaṅgaḷumeseye ghōḷāylar‌ poḷeyise bisilguduregaḷ poḷevante
poḷeva kaḍuguduregaḷumaṁ miḍumiḍukanemiḍukuvasiḍilēḻgeyumaṁ
kōḷmasagida puliya piṇḍugaḷumananukarisi naḍevaṇiya sandaṇiyumaṁ kāḻtuṟu
masagidante masagida durdhara dhanurdhara balamumaṁ śvēta bhīṣmara pēḻdōje
yoḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷa paḍevaḷarkaḷ kurukṣētradoḷ citrisidantoḍḍi nindāgaḷ—

jalaśayanōdarāntaradinī trijagaṁ poṟamaṭṭudīgaḷeṁ
buli sale tamma tamma śibiraṅgaḷinugra caturbalaṅgaḷaṁ
palavumanonde māḍi desegaḷ masuḷalnaḍetandarājigi
rvaladalarātināyakarumorbaranorbare gelva takkinoḷ // ViVi.52 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ kaurava balada sēnānāyakaṁ gāṅgēyanaḍḍamāge tannoḍḍida
makaravyūhada moneyoḷ suttiṟidettida ponna toḷapa paḻayigegaḷuṁmeṟevabeḷḷiya rathamumā rathadoḷoḍambaḍe pūḍida kuduregaḷuṁ jōlda purvanetti
kaṭṭida lalāṭa paṭṭadoḷiṭṭaḷamoppuva bīravaṭṭamumasadaḷameseye divyakavacamaṁ
toṭṭu paraśurāmaṁ bāḻgendu pracaṇḍa kōdaṇḍamaṁ koṇḍu pāṇḍava balamaṁ
mārkoṇḍu nindāgaḷ śvētanumā vyūhakke prativyūhavāgi sūcīvyūhama
noḍḍi kanakakavacālaṅkr̥ta śarīranumārūḍha samara rasanumupārūḍha
[p. 261]
kanakarathanumāgi kailāsavāsige poḍevaṭṭu billaṅkoṇḍu gaṅgāsutaṅgadiradidirci
nindāgaḷ—

śvētana gaṅgājātana
mātane pārderaḍumoḍḍaṇaṁ kādalkeṁ
dī teṟadinoḍḍi ninduvu
bhūtaḷamaḷḷāḍe kesaṟa kaḍitada teṟadiṁ // ViVi.53 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ dharmaputraṁ puruṣōttamana mogamaṁ nōḍi kaurava
baladoḍḍaṇada nāyakarivarārendu besagoḷe makara mastakabhūmiyoḷ
yuddhasannaddhanāgi—

kembaṇṇada kuduregaḷoḷo
ḍambaḍe nija rajata rathamagurvurvareyaṁ
timbe kaḷaśadhvajaṁ miḷi
rdambaramaṁ baḷase nindanātaṁ drōṇaṁ // ViVi.54 [kandaṁ]

ātana sāre kamaṇḍalu
kētanamambaramanaḍare caturaṅga balō
pētanati dhavaḷa rathanabhi
jātaṁ kṣatriyaranuṟada kali kr̥panātaṁ // ViVi.55 [kandaṁ]

mattitta gāṅgēyana dakṣiṇōpāntadoḷ karganekargidasamada
gajaghaṭāṭōpada naḍuve—

saradada mugilane biḍadanu
karisuva dhavaḷāśvadindamesedoppuva lō
harathamadu puliya paḻayige
verasu taḻattaḻise nindanātaṁ śalyaṁ // ViVi.56 [kandaṁ]

mattitta gaṅgāsutana vāmabhāgadoḷambara bhāgamaṁ kaṭṭi meḍaṟidantāgi
tanna rathadoḷoṭṭida keydugaḷa beḷage beḷagāge—


[p. 262]
kaṟe koraloḷ kaṇṇosaloḷ
peṟe makuṭadoḷugra dhanu karāgradoḷireya
ḷḷiṟiye harikētu nabhadoḷ
miṟuguva cembonna rathadanaśvatthāmaṁ // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

ā rudrāvatārana keladoḷ kikkiṟigiṟida taḻeduṟugala naḍuve
ponnarathamanēṟi nindaṁ bhūriśravanātana keladoḷbāḷabaṭṭaṁtūntiṭṭante
sandaṇisi ninda gōpakumāraraṇiya naḍuve ponnarathamanēṟinindātanenna tammaṁ
kr̥tavarmanātana keladoḷondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu suttiṟidu kanaka daṇḍa
maṇḍita vicitrātapatraṅgaḷa naḍuve maṇimakuṭa marīcigaḷ poḷeye nānā
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi nindar jayatsēna kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa daṇḍadhāra śatadaṇḍa
dhararavara keladoḷ nīḷa śrutāyudhaniyutāyudhācyutāyudharembavara
keladoḷnilebalada seṟekōloḷondakṣōhiṇī balamberasumayvattusāsira
madadāneverasu nindaṁ suyōdhananaṇuga maydunaṁ sindhudēśādhīśvaraṁ
jayadrathanātana kelaloḷ makara mastaka bhūmiyoḷ karaṭataṭagaḷita
madajaḷadhārāpūra pariplāvita sakaḷa bhūtaḷamappa nālku lakka bhadrahastiyuma
nondumāḍi ghaṭeya moneyoḷ diggajēndramenisida supratīka gajēndra
manēṟi nindātanindrana keḷeyaṁ bhagadattanātana keladoḷondu lakka kudureyu
maṟuvattu sāsira rathamu mondakṣōhiṇiya kālāḷverasu nindar sōmadatta
bāhlīkaravara keladoḷ dēvēndraṅge pagevarāgi vikramārjunana keyyoḷ satta
nivātakavaca kāḷakēya pauḷōma taḷatāḷukaremba daityar‌ vr̥ddha vairamaṁ nenedu
trigartādhīśa suśarma prabhr̥tigaḷuṁ saṁsaptakarumāgi puṭṭi mūrukōṭiyu
maṟuvattusāsira daitya pradhāna nāyakarumarjunanoḷ kāduva besanaṁ
duryōdhananoḷ bēḍi paḍedu padineṇṭu kōṭi rathamberasu bēṟoḍḍi
nindar‌ mattitta caturaṅgabaḷa jaḷanidhiya naḍuve kaḷiṅgarāja vaṅga koṅga
dēśādhīśvarareṇbattusāsira gajaghaṭegaḷuṁmūṟu lakka rathamumaṟuvattu kōṭi
padātiyuṁ berasu nindar mattaṁ kṣēmadhūrtiyuṁ bhīmasēnana keyyoḷ
satta bakāsura jaṭāsurana makkaḷaḷambhūṣa halāyudha musalāyudha kāḷa nīḷa
pramukha rūkṣarākṣasa balamberasu suttiṟidu baḷasiyu mire duśyāsanaṁ
[p. 263]
modalāge nūrvar tammandiruṁ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvar makkaḷumaṟu
vattusāsirarathamuṁ padineṇṭu sāsira madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷuṁ berasu poyva
pañcamahāśabdaṅgaḷ kāḷa nīḷa jaḷandharaṅgaḷ moḻaguvante moḻage gaganataḷaṁ
taḷirtante poḷedu miḷirva pāḷi mahādhvajaṅgaḷuṁ gagana sindhu phēna paṭaḷa
śaṅkha saṅkāśa pāṇḍu chatracāmaraṅgaḷuṁ peṟavuṁ rājacihnaṁ gaḷumeseye—

kanaka girīndra rundra śikharasthita bāḷa dinēśa bimbamaṁ
neneyise tanna ponna rathadoḷ nelasirdu viḷāsadinde bhī
mana moneyaṁ vanīpakaranārayalaṭṭi yugānta vārdhi bhōṁ
kene taḷarvandadiṁ taḷaralaṭṭipanalte phaṇīndrakētanaṁ // ViVi.58 [campakamāle]

seṟekōl seṟekōliṁ pa
ttaṟugāvuda balada pavaṇananitinitendā
naṟiyeṁ dēvāsuraroḷa
maṟiyeṁ kaṇḍinitu balamanānavanipatī // ViVi.59 [kandaṁ]

endu nāmuṁ namma balada nāyakaraneḍeyaṟidoḍḍuvamendu
drōṇana monegaṟuvattusāsira rathamberasu dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanumanaśvatthāmana monege
nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu śikhaṇḍiyumaṁ kr̥tavarmana monegondakṣōhiṇī
balaṁ berasu sātyakiyumaṁ duryōdhanana monegondu kōṭi rathamumondu
lakka bhadrahastiyuṁ berasu bhīmanumaṁ br̥hadbaḷana monege mūvattusāsira
rathamberasabhimanyuvumaṁ duśyāsanana monege nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu
nakulanumaṁ śakuniya monege nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu sahadēvanumaṁ kr̥pana
monegondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu kēkayarumaṁ sindhurājana monegondakṣō
hiṇī balamberasu drupadanumaṁ bhagadattana monegondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu
virāṭanumaṁ jaṭāsura bakāsurara makkaḷaḷambhūṣa haḷāyudha musaḷāyudha
kāḷa nīḷa naktañcarara monegondakṣōhiṇī balaṁ berasu ghaṭōtkacanumaṁ
vindanamonege padineṇṭu sāsira rathamumondulakka madadāneyumberasu
kontiyamāvanappa kontibhōjanumaṁ vindānuvindara monegaṟuvattu sāsira
rathamberasu nāgakumārananantabala samanvitaniḷāvantanumaṁ bhūriśravana monege
nālvattusāsira rathamuṁ nālvattusāsira madahastigaḷuṁ berasu madagajārūḍha
nuttaranumaṁ suyōdhanana makkaḷ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvara monegaṟuvattu
[p. 264]
sāsira rathamberasu suta sōmaka pramukharappa pañca pāṇḍavarumaṁ pēḻdu
kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa daṇḍadhāraremba mūvarakṣōhiṇīpatigaḷa monege
mūṟukōṭi rathamberasu pāṇḍya śrījayasōmakaraṁ pēḻdu vīra puṣkara
pāriyātra barbara śabara nēpāḷa mahīpāḷara monegeraḍu kōṭi rathamberasu
haihayaraṁ pēḻdu nīḷananaṟuvattusāsira bhadrahastiverasu tanna cakra rakṣege pēḻdu
saṁsaptakara padineṇṭu kōṭi rathakkarikēsariya rathamanondane pēḻdu yudhiṣṭhiraṁ
śalyana monege neṟedunindu keyvīsuvā prastāvadoḷ ‘śūraṁ bhēdēna
yōjayēt’ emba nayamaṁ keykoṇḍu vinayamane mundiṭṭu—

baḷameraḍuṁ tannane miḷa
miḷa nōḍe narēndranonde rathadindasuhr̥
dbaḷamaniradeydi bhīṣmara
caḷaṇa yugakkeṟage ninage jayamakkendaṁ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]

endu bhīṣmar tammamommanavinayakke mecci parase parakeyaṁ
keykoṇḍu—

guru kr̥pagurusutaśalyara |
caraṇaṅgaḷgeṟagi pōgi poḍevaḍuvudumā
daradindaṁ nalmeyoḷaṁ
parasi manaṅgoṇḍu nuḍidaravarā nr̥panaṁ // ViVi.61 [kandaṁ]

ninna baravindavemma ma
nanninageṟagidudu jayamumemmī deseyiṁ
danninage sārge pōgene
mannisi gurujanamanāgaḷantakatanayaṁ // ViVi.62 [kandaṁ]

maguḻdu tannoḍḍaṇakke baruttuṁ duryōdhanana tammanappa yuyutsuvaṁ
kaṇḍu—


[p. 265]
pavanajaninde kauravakulaṁ paḍaliṭṭavolakkumādoḍi
nnavaravarārumillaṇame santati keṭṭapudilli kāvenī
bavaradoḷīgaḷānivananendu nr̥paṁ dayeyindamā yuyu
tsuvanoḍagoṇḍu bandanenitādoḍamēṁ prabhu pollakeygumē // ViVi.63 [campakamāle]

antā yuyutsuvanoḍagoṇḍu bandu dharmaputranutsāhadoḷirpa
padadoḷ vikramārjunana manadoḷāda vyāmōhamaṁ kaḷeyalendu mukundaṁ
divyasvarūpamaṁ tōṟi—

adiradidirci taḷtiṟiyalī maledoḍḍida cāturaṅgameṁ
budu ninagoḍḍi nindudidanōvade kolvaḍe nīnumenna ka
jjadoḷesagendusaitajitanādiya vēdarahasyadoḷ niraṁ
tada[paricaryeyiṁ]neṟeye yōjisidaṁ kadanatriṇētranaṁ // ViVi.64 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ parasainyabhairavaṁ purāṇapuruṣanappa puruṣōttamaṅgeṟagi
poḍamaṭṭu ripupakṣakṣayakaramappa viśvakarma nirmitamāda tanna divyarathamaṁ
manōrathamberasurathāṅgadharanaṁ munnamēṟalvēḻdu mūṟu sūḻ balavandu
poḍamaṭṭu baḻiyaṁ tānēṟi vajrakavacamaṁ toṭṭu tavadoṇegaḷaneraḍuṁ
deseyoḷaṁ bigidu drōṇācāryaṅge manadoḷ namaskāraṅgeydu drōṇaṁ
bāḻgendu mahā pracaṇḍa gāṇḍīvamaṁ koṇḍēṟisi nīvi jēvoḍedu dēvadatta
śaṅkhamaṁ pūrisi saṁsaptakaroḍḍaṇadatta rathāṅgadharanaṁ rathamaṁ cōdisa
lvēḻdāgaḷ—

kuḷaśaiḷēndraṅgaḷambhōnidhigaḷakhiḷa digdantigaḷ viśvadhātrī
vaḷayaṁ pātāḷamūlaṁ sakala bhuvanamondondaṟoḷkēṇigoṇḍu
ccaḷisal sūsal paḷañcal siḍidoḍedaḷaṟal pāṟi jīṟēḻalandu
mmaḷisuttattirdarāvaṁ hariganoḷidiraṁ mīṟi māṟāmpa gaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.65 [mahāsragdhare]

embannegaṁ praḷaya kāla jātōtpāta vāta nirghātadindamaḷḷāḍi
taḷḷaṅkaṅguṭṭuva jaḷanidhigaḷante mēredappal bagevubhaya sainyaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍatta
rājarājanumitta dharmarājanumoḍanoḍane keyvīsidāgaḷ—


[p. 266]
pūrvāpara jaḷanidhigaḷa
gurvisuvinamondanondu tāguvavolagu
rvurvire parvi caturvala
mērvesadindandu bandu tāgittāgaḷ // ViVi.66 [kandaṁ]

ghaṭeya daḻadulivu laya ghana
ghaṭegaḷa moḻagenise poṭṭagoḍedattu raṭa
tpaṭu paṭaha śaṅkha bhēriya
caṭuvaḷitadindaṭaḷa paṭaḷamambara paṭaḷaṁ // ViVi.67 [kandaṁ]

kari turaga ratha padātiya
caraṇāsaṅghāta jāta rajamājasraṁ
neredambarakogeyal baḷa
bharadiṁ dhareyeḻdu pāṟuvantāytāgaḷ // ViVi.68 [kandaṁ]

samara rasapriyaroḷ sa
ttvamumiḷeyoḷ rajamumodave raṇagaḻtaleyoḷ
tamamuṁ mige sattva raja
stamaṅgaḷuṁkāṇalāduveraḍuṁ paḍeyoḷ // ViVi.69 [kandaṁ]

paḍeya poṟegagidu śēṣaṁ
peḍegaḷanuḍuguvudumeḷe bodillene biḻda
ttaḍigiḍe kūrmana bennaṁ
doḍedu siḍildoḍane nuccunūṟappinegaṁ // ViVi.70 [kandaṁ]

antu nelanumākāśamondondaṟoḷ tāgida bēgadoḷambaraṁ baraṁ
negeda dhūḷiyoḷ deseyaṟiyadeyuṁ tamma balamaṁ mārvalamanaṟi
yadeyuṁ cāturvalaṅgaḷ modala samakaṭṭugeṭṭu taḍavarisi taṭṭu
poṭṭendeccumiṭṭumiṟidutaṟidu ghaṭṭiseyumāṅkegoṇḍu kiṟidu poḻtu
kāde kāde suriva bisunettara sariyoḷamambina sariyoḷamambiriviṭṭu pāyva
madagajaṅgaḷa madajaladoḷaṁ balada kaḷakaḷakke masagi deseyaṟiyadeyuṁ paṟiye
[p. 267]
ghaṭṭisida kīḷa ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷ poṭṭagoḍeda tāḷugegaḷa rudhirajaladoḷ berasi
padagempanāḷda jātyaśvada lāḷājaḷadoḷaṁ neladoḷogeva rajaṁ modalmūlaṁ
giḍeyuṁ tiṟidikkidante talegaḷpaṟiduruḷdoḍe permaraṅgaḷa pōḻgaḷoḷagaṇiṁ
damogeda kēsurigaḷa baḷagadantaṭṭegaḷindambarambaraṁ negedu pāṟuva nettara
suṭṭuregaḷindaṁ mēge negeda rajaṁ masuḷanāge deseyaṟidu tamma balamumaṁ
mārvalamumanaṟidu navarudhira jaḷacaḷatsēcanadoḷghaṭṭisi
sinduradoḷ nelagaṭṭisidantirda raṅga bhūmiyoḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakar
bilgāḷegaṅgāduvāgaḷ—

piḍikey tīvida kūrgaṇe
maḍakālvaramaleva kacce niḍiyasiyoṟe ka
rpiḍida paṇegaṭṭu keypoḍe
beḍaṅganoḷakoḷe dhanurdharar peṇedeccar // ViVi.71 [kandaṁ]

śarasandhānaṁ niṭṭisa
laridembinameraḍu balada kaḍuvillar bhō
rgaredise kūrgaṇeyoḷ paṁ
darikkidantāytu gagana maṇḍaḷamellaṁ // ViVi.72 [kandaṁ]

gaṟisannegeydu tegeneṟe
deṟagi paraṅkalisi parvi kūkiṟidise keṁ
gaṟiya moneyambugaḷ ka
ṇdeṟeyisiduvu poṇarva billa kaḍuvittegaraṁ // ViVi.73 [kandaṁ]

ariva naḍuvuḍiva nērgō
lvaridurcuva naṭṭu toneva kaṇegaḷge mogaṁ
diriyadidiridiranadirade
surigiṟivanteccarambanambaṭṭuvinaṁ // ViVi.74 [kandaṁ]

piḍikeyya doṇeya podeyaṁ
biḍe muḍivinameccu surigegiḻtidiridiraṁ

[p. 268]
paḍe peṇediṟiduṁ bilvaḍe
paḍedudu bhōrgaredu pariva nettarakaḍalaṁ // ViVi.75 [kandaṁ]

antubhayabala dhanurdhara balaṅgaḷumaḻgi maḻgidāgaḷ—

toḷaguva bāḷ taḻattaḻipa kakkaḍe bumbhukadoḷ taguḷdu pa
jjaḷisuva pañcarāyudhamagurvisuvāvuti pūsidantiri
ṭṭaḷamamardirda māḷajige pakkareyikkidajāyilaṁ bhayaṁ
goḷise kaḍaṅgi tāgidudasuṅgoḷe tuṅga turaṅga sādhanaṁ // ViVi.76 [campakamāle]

antu viḷaya kāḷada kāḻkircina bēge sārvantirvaladaḷavuṅkircuṁ
kiḍiyumāge tāgidāgaḷ—

pasuge nelaṁ jalaṁ hayadoḍambaḍu vañcane kēṇamāsanaṁ
kose dese diṭṭi muṭṭi kelajaṅke nivartane kāṇke parvidē
rvesanadoḷāda balmeyoḷoḍambaḍe taḷtiṟivalli miñcinoḷ
musukida māḻkeyāytu samarāṅgaṇamuḷkuva bāḷgaḷuḷkadiṁ // ViVi.77 [campakamāle]

kara karavāḷa ghātadoḷarātiya pandale pañcarāyudhaṁ
berasesevaṭṭe toṭṭa kavacamberasēṟida vāji lōhava
kkareverasonde sūḻoḷe paḍalvaḍe dōrvaladurvu bīradoḷ
poredire binnaṇaṁ negaḻe taḷtiṟidar kelarāji raṅgadoḷ // ViVi.78 [campakamāle]

piḍidudirva bāḷa kiḍigaḷa
noḍanoḍanarevotti toṭṭa sannaṇavuriya
lkoḍarisidoḍavaṟaparvaṁ
biḍeyaridarisamitiyoḍane kādidararebar // ViVi.79 [kandaṁ]

bhugubhuganurcipāyva bisunettara suṭṭureyaṁ nelakke pa
rdugaḷugalīyadavvaḷisi pīrvinamormeyepoyva poygaḷiṁ
negedu mugilgaṭṭeḍegaḷoḷ talegaḷ toḍardirda jēnapu
ṭṭigaḷane pōltuvēṁ kalahamaccariyāyto turaṅgasainyadoḷ // ViVi.80 [campakamāle]


[p. 269]
anteraḍuṁ balada daḻaṅgaḷkōlāṭamāḍuvante kiṟidānuṁ bēgaṁ
taṭṭupoṭṭendu kōlkuṭṭi patteṇṭu sāsirakudureyaṭṭeyumēḻeṇṭu nettara
kaḍal kaḍalanaṭṭeyuṁ kādi basamaḻidu peṟapiṅgi nindāgaḷ praḷayaduriya
nuruḷi māḍidantānuṁ baḍavāgniyananuvisidantānuṁbaṟa siḍilakiḍigaḷa
baḷagamanoḷagumāḍidantānuṁ gondaṇisi sandaṇisi nindaṇiyaneraḍuṁ balada
kaḍitaleya nāyaka‌r keykoṇḍu baḷḷugeḍedekkevāṟu vāṟi palagevāḍigūḷisorki mārkoṇḍu kāde—

pusi nasu vañcane nōrpanu
vasidagalitu takkudakku page keybage ke
ykusuri nusuḷemba kēṇada
kusuriyanaṟidiṟidu meṟedu neṟeduṟadarebar // ViVi.81 [kandaṁ]

baṟa siḍileṟapantire baṁ
deṟagidaraṁ taḷtu bāḷa kīḻmoneyiṁ ta
ḷtaṟadaṟidubbaramembiva
naṟidiṟidar peṇabaṇambegaḷ negevinegaṁ // ViVi.82 [kandaṁ]

cārisi bāḷāgamamava
tāraṁ geydante kāladantakanane pō
ltāruttuṁ kavivadaṭara
nōrondōrondevoydu kondar palaraṁ // ViVi.83 [kandaṁ]

bāḷvāḷgaḷa ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷ
baḷvaḷa baḷedogedu negeda kiḍigaḷa bamba
lgaḷverasu poḷedu negedudu
bāḷvoge[kāṟa mugil]baḷḷimiṁ[cinindu]ḷkuvavōl // ViVi.84 [kandaṁ]


[p. 270]
tale neladoḷuruḷdoḍaṁ mē
ygaliyorvaṁ piḍidu taleyaniṭṭaṭṭeyoḷa
ggalisida muḷisiṁ māṭada
taleyiṭṭāḍuvavaninisu pōltanugeydaṁ // ViVi.85 [kandaṁ]

antaṇi maṇiyade seṇasi poṇardu kiṟidu poḻtu kādinindāgaḷ—

māruta ghāta sañcaḷita kētu samūhamudagra cakra cī
tkāramudāra vīra bhaṭa siṁha nināda vimiśritōtkaṭa
jyāravamambarāntaramanaḷḷiṟidavvaḷipannegaṁ śarā
sāradagurvu parvi nile tāgiduvugra rathaṁ rathāḷiyoḷ // ViVi.86 [utpalamālike]

antu tāgidāgaḷ—

kudureya baṇṇadiṁ rathada tōrkeyinettida citrakētu vr̥ṁ
dada kuṟupindudagra ratha cōdaka cihnadinātanītaneṁ
budanaṟidorvarorvarane maccaradiṁ gaṟisannegeydidi
rcida padadoḷ patatrimayamembinitāytu samasta diktaṭaṁ // ViVi.87 [campakamāle]

paraśu śara nikaradiṁ ku
mmarigaḍidavoloḍane kaḍiyerathigaḷ rathadiṁ
dharegiḻidu viratharatiratha
rarebar mēlvāydu rathigaḷaṁ surigiṟidar // ViVi.88 [kandaṁ]

tēraṁ pāyisi nōyisi
pāruvakuduregaḷanarebarerdeyuriyeccar‌
sārathiya rathiya talegaḷa
nōrondastradoḷe pāṟi jīṟēḻvinegaṁ // ViVi.89 [kandaṁ]

nettara kesaṟoḷ gāliga
ḷettaṁ taḷarade jigiltu nile dharegiḻidā
rdetti pariyisidarēṁ me
yvettudo rathakalpamalli sūtar kelabar // ViVi.90 [kandaṁ]


[p. 271]
antubhaya varūthiniya varūthaṅgaḷ mallāmalliyāge kāduvāgaḷ—

uḍidirdaccaḻidīsu taḻgida nogaṁ jīṟeḻda cakraṁ siḍil
poḍedantormeye sūsi pāṟida maḍaṁ nurgāda kīl sāyakaṁ
naḍe nondeyde suruḷduruḷda turagaṁ surkirda sūtaṁ kaḍal
kaḍalaṁ muṭṭi teraḷva nettara ponal kaṇgoṇḍudugrājiyoḷ // ViVi.91 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu patteṇṭu nettara kaḍal kaḍalanaṭṭeyuṁ varūtha yūthaṅgaḷaḷki
meḷkidantāgaḷ—

ikkida lōhavakkareyakarpugaḷiṁkavitarpa vindhya śai
lakkeṇeyāge jōdarisuvambina balsari tiṇṇamāgi ke
ymikku virōdhi sādhana ghaṭāḷiyanōḍisalāgaḷārdu bi
ṭṭikkidarugra sindhura ghaṭāvaḷiyaṁ muḷisiṁ niṣādigaḷ // ViVi.92 [utpalamālike]

ādityaṁ masuḷvannegaṁdhvaja ghaṭāṭōpaṅgaḷinda layāṁ
bhōdaṅgaḷ kavivantevōl kavivuduṁ kālgāpu kālgāpinoḷ
jōdar jōdaroḷāneyāneyoḷagurvappannegaṁ kāde ka
ṇgādaṁ celvesedattu mūṟu neleyiṁ mādyadgajēndrāhavaṁ // ViVi.93 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]

antā dantighaṭegaḷanārōhakar‌ tōṟikoṭṭondondarke
mogambugisi dāgaḷubhaya vyāḷadantivadhya kramaṅgaḷoḷ bhārgavar
surigiṟivantiṟiye sūsuva kennettar kaḻaldudirva sakkada sippugaḷuṁ siḍildu
jīṟēḻva kōḻkaḷumagurvaṁ paḍeye—

naḍuva saralge meyyoḷagaḍaṅguva saṅkuge diṅkugoḷva ka
kkaḍegidirurcuviṭṭigidirāneya kōḻkaḷa kōḷge nondu bā
yviḍadinisappoḍaṁpeḷaṟadaḷkade pāvinaliṭṭavōl poḍa
rpuḍugade biḻduvirda neleyiṁ kelavunmada gandhasindhuraṁ // ViVi.94 [campakamāle]


[p. 272]
pāṟuva pāṟumbaḷe koḷe
jīṟeḻdambarake tale siḍildoḍamā kā
ypāṟade haraṇaṁ geyduvu
jāṟallade jōdaraṭṭegaḷ kelavāgaḷ // ViVi.95 [kandaṁ]

kaṇakene cakra tīvra hatiyiṁ tale pōdoḍe jōdaraṭṭe saṁ
daṇisidabandhadiṁ bisugeyoḷ nelasirdesedāḍe naṭṭa kū
rgaṇeverasirdakūrgaṇegaḷuccaḷisuttire suydupuṇṇatiṁ
thiṇigaḷinandagurvuverasāḍiduvonderaḍāneyaṭṭegaḷ // ViVi.96 [campakamāle]

anteraḍuṁ balada karighaṭegaḷondondaṟoḷ tāgi taṭṭiṟiye
bisunetta[ra]rbigaḷurvipāye pērurvigaḷverasu jājina parvataṅgaḷante
keḍedaḻgitaḻgidāgaḷ—

ānireyēniṟivudu gaḍa
mī nālkuṁ balamidalte paribhavamenageṁ
dēnuṁ māṇade bhīmana
nūnabalaṁ bandu tāgidaṁ kurubaladoḷ // ViVi.97 [kandaṁ]

antu kurubalada karighaṭegaḷaṁ nuṅguvante desedesege miḷirdu miḷḷisida
siṅgada paḻavigeyuṁ kurubalakke miḻtu palmorevante moredu pariva tanna
kisuvonna rathamuṁ bhayaṅkarākāramāge pagevara gaṇṭalanottuvantepauṇḍramemba
śaṅkhamanotti mundoḍḍidoḍḍellamanambinabambaloḷe paḍalvaḍisuttuṁ barpa
bhīmasēnaṅge duryōdhananadiradidirāntāgaḷ—

entidirānteyante kaliyāgoḷasōradirendu bhīmanō
rante kanaldu tiṇṇamise pāyva saralgaḷaneydalīyadāṁ
tāntu nirantaraṁ taṟidu sūtananātana vājiyaṁ mahī
śaṁ tegedeccanacca bisunettara suṭṭure sūsuvannegaṁ // ViVi.98 [utpalamālike]


[p. 273]
ise masagi bhīmanīra
yduśitāstradinuruḷe sūtanuḍiye rathaṁ kī
lise kudure muṟiye paḻavige
masakadinecceccanonde saraloḷ nosalaṁ // ViVi.99 [kandaṁ]

paṭṭaṅgaṭṭida nosalaṁ
naṭṭa saralviḍidu nettarambiriviḍe ka
ṇgeṭṭirda nr̥pananaṅkada
kaṭṭāḷgaḷ kādu kaḷipeduryōdhananaṁ // ViVi.100 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ avananujarnūrvaruṁ bandu tannanorvanaṁ tāgidoḍa
nibarumaṁ viratharmāḍi bhāratamaninde sameyisuvenendu kōdaṇḍamaṁ bisuṭu
gadādaṇḍamaṁ bhujādaṇḍadoḷaḷavaḍisikoṇḍu—

kuru balamaṁ paḍalvaḍipa takkinoḷeytare barpa bīmanaṁ
bare baralīyadirdavaranāpadadoḷ peṟagikki gandhasiṁ
dhuraghaṭe nālku kōṭiverasāgaḍe bandu kaḷiṅgarājanāṁ
tire page keygevandu bardukāḍida balmuḷisiṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ // ViVi.101 [campakamāle]

antu kaḷiṅgarāja matta mātaṅga ghaṭegaḷa mēle muḷisaṁ kaḷevenendu
siṁhanādadinārdu—

gajeyaṁ bhōrene parvi bīsi kaḍupindeytandu māṟaunta sā
majasaṅghātamanondugoḷḷeraḍugoḷḷendurvi poyvondu po
ygejavaṅgundi siḍildu munnaḍiguruḷtarpannegaṁ bīḻe di
ggajamaṁ pōlva gajaṅgaḷaṁ palavumaṁ kondaṁ marunnandanaṁ // ViVi.102 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

baḍigoḷe bidu bibbara biri
doḍanuge posa muttu kōḍanūṟi madēbhaṁ

[p. 274]
keḍeduvu kolladirendira
daḍigeṟaguva teṟananinisananukarisuvinaṁ // ViVi.103 [kandaṁ]

antu patteṇṭusāsiramāneyaṁ paḍalvaḍisiyuṁ sairisalāṟade—

piḍidondondaṟa gātramaṁ tiripikoṇḍondondaṟoḷ poydu me
lvaḍagappannegamettikoṇḍasagavoyvoyloḷ taḍamboydumu
ḷḷaḍaguṁ nettarumelvumella desegaṁ jīṟeḻdu pāṟēḻe ba
ldaḍigaṁ bīsiyumondu kōṭivaregaṁ kondaṁ madēbhaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.104 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

siḍilantormeye poyye poyda bharadindondāne tōl nettare
lvaḍagondondaṟoḷondumondade gadā nirghātadiṁ māyamā
doḍe pō tappidenendu palmoredagurvappannegaṁ mīseyaṁ
kaḍidaṁ tōḷvaladēḻge meccuvanitarkugrājiyoḷ bhīmanā // ViVi.105 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

dhvajamuṁ bisugeyumēṟi
rda jōdaruṁ berasu gajeyinari gaja ghaṭeyaṁ
gijigijiyāgire poydoḍe
gujugujugoṇḍārdaramararambara taḷadoḷ // ViVi.106 [kandaṁ]

antu gāḷigoḍḍida ghana ghaṭeyante tanagoḍḍida kaḷiṅgarāja matta
mātaṅga ghaṭegaḷaṁ kaḻakuḻaṁ māḍidanannegamitta śalyana moneyoḷ dharmaputraṁ
kādi nālku kellambugaḷindātana varūtha sūta kētanaṅgaḷaṁ kaḍidu—

uramaṁ birivinamise ma
dra rājanaḷiyana parākramakkosedu mogaṁ
muriyade peṟatuṁ ratha[maṁ]
[tarisi kanaldaḍardu kadanakāgaḷe neṟedaṁ] // ViVi.107 [kandaṁ]

[muṟidu rathamaṁ]rathāśvama
nuṟade[raḍuṁ śarade]nālkaṟiṁ sūtananoṁ

[p. 275]
daṟikeya saraloḷ[māṇade]
taṟidaṁ paḻavigeyanēṁ kr̥tāstrano śalyaṁ // ViVi.108 [kandaṁ]

antu virathanaṁ māḍi dharmaputranaṁ piḍiyaleytarpa madra rājanaṁ
pannirchāsiramāneverasu nr̥pana cakrarakṣakaṁ nīḷaneḍegoṇḍu tāgidāgaḷ—

mr̥garāja nakhara bāṇā
ḷigaḷiṁ tegeneṟedu śalyanuṟadise biduvaṁ
mr̥garājaṅgaḷe pōḻvavo
lagalvinaṁ pōḻduvugra bāṇāvaḷigaḷ // ViVi.109 [kandaṁ]

antā dantighaṭeyaṁ paḍalvaḍisi nīḷanēṟidāneyumanūṟi
koṇḍeccāgaḷ—

peṟagiḍuva dantiyaṁ kali
niṟisi calaṁ nelase tōṟikuḍuvudumāgaḷ
poṟamuyvuvaraṁ tegeneṟe
duṟadeccaṁ śalyanānta nīḷana taleyaṁ // ViVi.110 [kandaṁ]

antu nīḷaṁ nīḷagiriya mēgaṇiṁ baṟasiḍil poḍeye keḍeva
mr̥garājanante hasti mastakadiṁ keḍevudumatta bhūriśravana moneyoḷ kāduttirdu
ttaraṁ nālvattu sāsiramāneverasarasanaṁ peṟagikki bandāntāgaḷ—

nage pagevāḍi gōgrahaṇadoḷ poṟamāṟida bannamondu ne
ṭṭage manamaṁ paḷañcaleye māṇade śalyananandaśalyanaṁ
bagevavolēḷidaṁ bagedu dantiyanāgaḍe tōṟikoṭṭu to
ṭṭage rathamaṁ paḍalvaḍisi pūḻdanarātiyanastrakōṭiyiṁ // ViVi.111 [campakamāle]

antuttaraṁ tanagaḷavumadaṭuṁ rājōttaramāge kādidoḍe śalyaṁ
virathanāgi siggāgi—


[p. 276]
tārakanaṁ guhaṁ muḷidu śaktiyināntiḍuvantarāti saṁ
hārakavappa visphurita śaktiyinātananiṭṭu khaḻgadiṁ
vāraṇamaṁ paḍalvaḍisi tāṁ peṟapiṅguvuduṁ balakke hā
hā ravamuṇme dantiverasājiyoḷuttaranaḻgitaḻgidaṁ // ViVi.112 [utpalamālike]

antuttaranaṁ javaṅge posatikkuvantikki basavaḻida śalyanaṁ kr̥tavarmaṁ
tanna rathamanēṟisikoṇḍu nindanannegamittalamarāpagāsutana moneyoḷ
bharaṅgeydu kāduva sēnānāyakaṁ śvētaṁ tanna tammanatītanādudaṁ kēḷdu—

praḷaya payōdhivōlaḷurdu peṅkuḷigoṇḍa madēbhavairivōl
keḷardu layāgnivōlaḷurdu madra mahīśananeyde tāge ba
ḷvaḷa baḷedattu śalyanoḷe kāḷegamīgaḷenuttumante ke
ykoḷalahikētu sindhutanayamberasāgaḍe bandu tāgidaṁ // ViVi.113 [campakamāle]

itta dharmaputranuṁ virāṭa dhr̥ṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍi cēkitāna kēkaya sātyaki
nakuḷa sahadēva saubhadra pramukha nāyakarverasu raṇapaṭahaṅgaḷaṁ negaḻce kr̥pa
kr̥tavarma viviṁśati vikarṇa citrasēna sōmadatta bhagadatta bāhlīka bhūriśravaḥ
prabhr̥tigaḷ gaṟisannegaidu kāduvāgaḷ—

naḍuva saral saralkoḷe suruḷva hayaṁ hayaduḷgaruḷgaḷoḷ
toḍarva bhaṭar bhaṭarkaḷoḷe toḻtuḻimāḻpa rathaṁ rathakke vā
ydaḍigiḍi meyvoṇarcuva mahāratharājiyoḷantagurvina
ccuḍidire kādi biccaḻisida‌r bisunettara suṭṭure sūsuvannegaṁ // ViVi.114 [campakamāle]

anteraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarorvarorvaroḷ talemaṭṭu kāduvāgaḷ
śvētaṁ tanna tammanaḻivinoḷāda muḷisinoḷ kaṇgāṇade śalyanaṁ muṭṭevandu—

muḷisinoḷeyde kempaḍarda kaṇgaḷinormeye nuṅguvantasuṁ
goḷe naḍe nōḍi māṇaduramaṁ biriyeccoḍe sūsi pāyvasr̥
gjaḷamavanugra kōpa śikhi taḷtaḷurvantevolāge śalyanā
gaḷe raṇadoḷ neṟaldoḍavanaṁ peṟagikki surāpagātmajaṁ // ViVi.115 [campakamāle]


[p. 277]
antu praḷayakāladandu mūḍuva pannirvarādityara tējamumaṁ
mahēśvara bhairavāḍambaramumaṁ yugānta kālāntakana masakamumaṁ
tannoḷaḷavaḍisikoṇḍu—

khara kiraṇa pracaṇḍa kiraṇāvaḷi lōkamaneyde parvuvaṁ
tire kaḍukeydu tanneraḍu keyyoḷamecca śarāḷigaḷ bhayaṁ
karataramāge bhū bhuvanamellamanormeye sutti mutti koṁ
ḍire desegāṇalāgadudalā raṇagaḻtale mandamādudō // ViVi.116 [campakamāle]

embinamambina bambaloḷaṁ jōḍāgi kōḍanūṟi keḍeda gajavrajaṅgaḷa
ḍoṇevugaḷindoṟetu pariva nettara kaḍalgaḷuṁ nettara kaḍalgaḷoḷ miḷirva
paḻavigegaḷ taledōṟe muḻuṅgida rathaṅgaḷuṁ rathaṅgaḷa gāligaḷgaḍḍamāgi
biḻdirda madahastigaḷuṁ madahasti mastakaṅgaḷanōsarisi rathamaṁ pariyisuva
rathacōdakaruṁ rathacōdakara biṭṭa bāy biṭṭantire biṭṭa tamma karuḷgaḷoḷ
tavetoḍardu kīḻaṁ karci diṇḍu maguḷdu keḍeva jātyaśvaṅgaḷuṁ jātyaśvaṅgaḷa
peṇada tintiṇiyoḷ toḍardeḍaputtumāḍuva subhaṭaraṭṭegaḷuṁ subhaṭaraṭṭe
gaḷaneḻbaṭṭi kuṭṭuva toṇḍu maruḷgaḷuṁ maruḷgaḷāṭamaṁ paḷapaḷanemeyikkade
nōḍi muguḷnage naguva vīra bhaṭara pandalegaḷumagurvumadbhuta bhayānaka
vīrabībhatsaraudrarasaṅgaḷaṁ puduṅgoḷisi gāṅgēyaṁ nāḍeyuṁ poḻtu kāde—

paṭṭaṅgaṭṭidiḷādhināthare payiñchāsirvaroḷḷānegaḷ
paṭṭaṅgaṭṭiduvondu lakka turagaṁ patteṇṭu lakkaṁ paḍa
lvaṭṭaḻkāḍiduvonde bilgene nadīputraṅge pēḻār calaṁ
baṭṭuṁ mārmaledambudoṭṭumuḻivar saṅgrāma raṅgāgradoḷ // ViVi.117 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embannegaṁ śvētanumanavarata śarāsāradiṁ kurubalamellamanaredu
saṇṇisidante māḍi taveneraviyanenitaṁ kondoḍamēvandapudendu
gāṅgēyaṅgadiradidiraṁ mārkoṇḍu bilvoydu nindāgaḷ—

śvētana billoḷirda madanāriya rūperdegoḷvuduṁ nadī
jātanudātta bhaktiyoḷe keymugidāgaḷidento nimma pe

[p. 278]
rmātina bīramīyeḍegevandude muppinoḷeyde lōka vi
khyātarirāgi keyduviḍivalliye kālviḍiyalke takkudē // ViVi.118 [utpalamāle]

enage raṇāgradoḷ poṇarvoḍaṅkada poṅkada sindhuputrano
rvane doreyendu nimmoḷe valaṁ taṟisandiṟiyalke pūṇdenā
nenagiṟivaḻtiyaṁ kiḍisi nimmaḷavaṁ peṟagikki nīmumiṁ
tiniterdegeṭṭiriṁ tuḻilasandaranārumanentu nambuvar // ViVi.119 [campakamāle]

endu tannaṁ nōye nuḍidoḍe sindhuputranintendaṁ—

ninagēnendoḍamendudoppidapudantēkennaninnī śarā
sanadoḷ śūla kapāla pāṇi dayeyiṁ bandirdanuntānumiṁ
tinitaṁ nīṁ nuḍivannegaṁ taḍevenē trailōkyanāthaṁ kaṇā
vinamanmastakanādenaṇmuvoḍe nīnī dēvanaṁ tōṟuvai // ViVi.120 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

iṟivantu ninage manadoḷ
taṟisalavuṇṭappoḍelavo dēvēśananēṁ
seṟeviḍidetolagu dēvana
maṟeyaṁ baḻikaṟiyalakkumenagaṁ ninagaṁ // ViVi.121 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ śvētanintendaṁ—

kāgevolintu bilge karamañjuvirañjalimā triṇētranaṁ
pō geḍegoṇḍu kāduvene kādenidaṁ haranittanendu nō
ḍāgaḍumaḻtiyiṁ piḍivenakkaṭa nimmanadirpuvalli cā
pāgamamēvudantenage bilvaramājiyoḷāmpa gaṇḍarār // ViVi.122 [utpalamālike]

bisuṭeṁ billanadēvudendu kaḍupindīḍāḍi sūryaprabhā
prasaraṅgaḷ masuḷvannegaṁ poḷevudondaṁ śaktiyaṁ koṇḍagu
rvisi gāṅgēyananiṭṭaniṭṭoḍadanīraydastradindeccu khaṁ
ḍisi pērāḷ tiṟidikkidante taleyaṁ pōgeccanā śvētanā // ViVi.123 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 279]
śvētana bīramanupamā
tītamanī dharege negaḻe negaḻdudanidanāṁ
pātāḷakkaṟipuveneṁ
bī teṟadoḷe dinapanapara jalanidhigiḻidaṁ // ViVi.124 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarapahāratūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisi tamma tamma
bīḍugaḷge pōdarannegamitta saṁsaptaka balamanellamanonde rathadoḷāditya
nasuraranadirpuvantāṭandu vikramārjunanumarātikāḷānaḷanumatirathamathananuṁ
ripukuraṅga kaṇṭhīravanuṁ sāhasābharaṇanumammanagandhavāraṇanuṁ paḍemecce
gaṇḍanuṁ parasainyabhairavanumemba pesargaḷananvartha māḍi—

neredanurāgadiṁ paḍeya pāḍiya bīrara peṇḍiraḻkaṟiṁ
parasiyoṟaldusēsegaḷanikke murāriya pāñcajanya vi
sphurita ravaṁ jayōtsavada ghōṣaṇeyantire pokkanātma maṁ
diramanudāttacittanavanītaḷa pūjya guṇaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.125 [campakamāle]


idu vividha vibudha janavinuta jinapadāmbhōja
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ

[ēkādaśāśvāsaṁ]

śrīyuvatiyanā vīra
śrīyuvatige savatimāḻpeneṁdari nr̥paru
ḷḷāyaveraseḻedukoṇḍu dha
rāyuvatige negaḻda hariganorvane gaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.1 [kandaṁ]

emba nija caritamaṁ pala
ruṁ baṇṇise kiviyanāntu kēḷuttumaḷuṁ
baṁ bīramenisi tanagidi
raṁ bandu kaḍaṅgi sattaraṁ pogaḻuttuṁ // ViVi.2 [kandaṁ]

antu vikrānta tuṅganirpannegamittaleraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakaraḻiye nonda
tammaṇugāḷgaḷa koṇḍāṭadānegaḷa naccina kuduregaḷa puṇgaḷanuḍiyalumōvaluṁ
mardubejjarumanaṭṭuttumikkida sannaṇaṅgaḷaṁ geldu kaṇakene pōgurci tamma
meyyoḷuḍidambugaḷumanelvaṁ naṭṭuḍida bāḷa kakkaḍeyuḍigaḷumanayaskāntamaṁ
tōṟi tegeyisuttuṁ vajramuṣṭiya poyloḷaṁ bāḷa kōḷoḷamuccaḷisida
kapāladōḍugaḷaṁ gaṅgegaṭṭuttuṁ—

unnata mastaka sthaḷadoḷambugaḷaḻduḍidirdoḍattami
ttanneṟe tandu baldaḍigariḻkuḻinoḷ kiḻe nondenennadaḥ
ennadaṇaṁ mogaṁ muriyadaḷkade bēnegaḷoḷ mogaṅgaḷaṁ
binnage māḍadirdaraḷavaccariyāge kelar mahārathar // ViVi.3 [utpalamālike]

rasamosarvannegaṁ taguḷe pāḍuva gāṇara gēyamaḻkaṟaṁ
posayise sōṅkuvoldolisuvōpaḷa sōṅku podaḻdajādiyoḷ
masagida kampu kampanoḷakoṇḍalevondela[rembi]vandupā
ṟisuvuvudagra vīra bhaṭarāhava kēḷi pariśramaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.4 [campakamāle]


[p. 281]
āgaḷ dharmanandanaṁ mukundaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi namma
sēnānāyakanuttāyakanāgi gāṅgēyarindamaḻidaninnārge vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭuvaṁ
pēḻimene—

bēḷveya koṇḍadoḷurcida
bāḷverasari balamanariyalendaṅkada ka
ṭṭāḷvīranati balaṁ nina
gāḷvesakendirdanalte dhr̥ṣṭadyumnaṁ // ViVi.5 [kandaṁ]

embudumī kajjamenna manadoḷoḍambaṭṭa kajjamātane vīrapaṭṭakke
takkanendu dharmanandanaṁ drupadanandanaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi piridumosageverasu
tāne vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi—

ā samara mukhadoḷesevari
kēsariya virōdhi rudhira jalanidhivol saṁ
dhyāsamayameseye taḻataḻa
nēsaṟ mūḍuvudumoḍḍaṇakkeḻtandar‌ // ViVi.6 [kandaṁ]

antajātaśatru munname bandoḍḍi śatru bala jalanidhiyaḷḷāḍe viḷaya
kāḷāniḷane bīsuvante keyvīsidāgaḷ—

caturaṅgaṁ caturaṅga sainyadoḷaḍu[rtuṁ]tiṟraneytandu tā
gi taḍaṁmeṭṭade kāde bāḷgaḷuḍigaḷjīṟeḻdumārtāgiśō
ṇita dhārāḷigaḷurci perci siḍiyal tēṅkal vimānaṅgaḷa
ḷki taguḷdāgaḷe mattamatta taḷardar dēvar nabhōbhāgadoḷ // ViVi.7 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarondorvaroḷ tāgi kiḍiguṭṭidante
kāduvāgaḷabhimanyu ugra tējanappa magadha tanūjananondepāṟeyambinoḷ
keyya kūsanikkuvantikkuvuduṁ neppiṅge neppugoḷḷade māṇenembante bakāsurana
maganaḷambhūṣanarjunana maganiḷāvantananantaka lōkamaneydisuvuduṁ
ghaṭōtkacaniḷāvantana sāvaṁ kaṇḍu sairisadaḷambhūṣananeḻbaṭṭuvudu mavanaḷki
bhagadattanāneya maṟeyaṁ puguvudumaḷambhūṣanaṁ pintikki bhagadattaṁ
ghaṭōtkacanaṁ mārkoṇḍu—


[p. 282]
utkōpa dahanadoḍane pr̥
ṣatkaṅgaḷkōṭi gaṇitadinduṟuvinamā
rdutkaca ditijananuṟade gha
ṭōtkacanaṁ biḻdu mūrchevōpinameccaṁ // ViVi.8 [kandaṁ]

annegaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ caturdaśabhuvanaṅgaḷellamaṁ teraḷci tēraisi
nuṅguvantu masakadiṁ bhagadattanaṁ mārkoṇḍu—

isuvudumecca śāta śara santatiyaṁ bhagadattaneyde khaṁ
ḍisi rathamaṁ paḍalvaḍise maccaradiṁ gajegoṇḍu tāge mā
ṇisalamarāpagāsutanidircuvuduṁ rathamaḻge poydu śaṁ
kisadidirānta saindhavanumaṁ pavanātmajanōḍe kādidaṁ // ViVi.9 [campakamāle]

antu kāde sindhurājana bembaladoḷ kādalendu banda nūrvar
kauravaruṁ bhīmanoḷ tāge tāgida bēgadiṁ durdharṣaṇa durmarṣaṇa
dīrghabāhu mahābāhu citrōpacitra nandopananda‌r modalāge mūvattu
mūvaraṁ javaṅge birdanikkuvantikki mattinuḻidarumanuḻiyalīyade
baḻisandāgaḷ—

modaliṭṭaṁ kolalendu kauravaraninnēkirpanārdurci mu
kkadivaṅgāṁkarameyde kūrpenivaruṁ sattapparindiṅge kā
vudanāṁ kāvenenutte bēṟe rathamaṁ bandēṟi pō pōgaleṁ
doduṟuttuṁ paritandu tāgitagardagaṅgāsutaṁ bhīmanaṁ // ViVi.10 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

annegamatta saṁsaptaka balamellamanaḷaṟe peḷaṟe kivuḻiduḻidu kolvalli
vikramārjunaṁ murāntakanoḷintendaṁ—

praḷaya payōdhi nādamane pōltu raṇānaka rāvamīgaḷa
ggaḷamesedappudattakaṟevambina balsariyindamā diśā
vaḷi masuḷdintu nīḷdapudu pōgade kāduva gaṇḍarilla ni
nnaḷiyanumā vr̥kōdaranumalladarilla peṟar murāntakā // ViVi.11 [campakamāle]

guru guruputra śalya bhagadatta nadīsutaremba sanda bī
rare maṟuvakkamaṇṇanoḍanirvare kūsugaḷemba śaṅkeyuṁ

[p. 283]
piridenagīgaḷādapudu māṇade cōdisu bēgamattala
tta rathamanendu bhōrgareye bandanarātige miḻtu barpavōl // ViVi.12 [campakamāke]

antu nelanadire barpa vikramārjunana baraviṅge kurubalamella
mollanulidōḍi surāpagānandanana maṟeyaṁ pokkāgaḷ—

eḍegoṇḍaṅkada śalya saindhava kr̥pa drōṇarkaḷuṁ sāyakaṁ
giḍe tannecca śarāḷigaḷ vilaya kālōlkaṅgaḷaṁ tāgidā
gaḍe tatsūta rathāśva kētana śaravrātaṅgaḷuṁ nurgi ka
ṇgiḍe bennaṭṭidanantu namma harigaṁ gaṇḍaṁ peṟar gaṇḍarē // ViVi.13 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antatiratha samaratha mahārathārdharatharkaḷanāne meṭṭida kuḷumpeya
nīrante dese desege kedaṟuvannameḻbaṭṭidāgaḷ sōlta tanna balamanaḷumbamāda
vikramārjunana bhujabalamumaṁ kaṇḍu kanaka tāḷadhvajaṅge pannagadhvajanintendaṁ—

muḷiye binnapamajja dāyigaroḷ virōdhamanintu ba
ḷvaḷane māḻpudanandu nimmane nambi māḍidenintu gō
vaḷiganaṁ geḍegoṇḍu muṁ baḷedoṭṭa pēḍiye nimmaniṁ
tiḷisi madbalamellamaṁ kole nōḍutirpudu pāḻiyē // ViVi.14 [taraḷaṁ]

mēḷadoḷentuṁ pō peṟa
rāḷaṁ chidrisuvevemba pāṇḍavaroḷ nīṁ
mēḷisi naṇpane bagedir
jōḷada pāḻiyumaninisu bageyiṁ nimmoḷ // ViVi.15 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ sindhutanūjanintendaṁ—

trijagakkaṁ guru dēvanādi puruṣaṁ kēḷorvanorvaṁ ripu
dhvajinī dhvaṁsakanāgi sanda kaliyuṁ billāḷuminnendoḍeṁ
tu jagatkhyātaranēḷipai maṟevenē muṁ pūṇdudaṁ bil rathaṁ
dhvajamambembivaneyde sandhisu jasaṁ nilvannegaṁ kāduveṁ // ViVi.16 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embudumanēka śarabharita śakaṭa sahasramanondumāḍi gāṅgēyana
peṟage nilisidāgaḷamarāpagānandananumamarēndranandananumorvarorvaraṁ
[p. 284]
gaṟisannegeydu kāduvāgaḷambara taḷadoḷellaṁ biḷiya mugilgaḷa caupaḷigegaḷoḷ
bandirda dēva vimānaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane kalaṅke kula girigaḷuṁ dikkarigaḷu
moḍanoḍane tāgidante tāgidāgaḷ—

upamātītada billa balme samasandondorvaroḷ parve pa
rvi paravyūha bhayaṅkaraṁ negedu pārdārdeccoḍambambana
ṭṭi paḷañcutte siḍilda tōragiḍiyindondondaṟoḷ bēvuduṁ
tripurambottisidante potti pogedattettaṁ viyanmaṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.17 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu brahmāṇḍamuriye kāde—

naḍapidanajjanendu vijayaṁ kaḍukeydisanenna maṁmanāṁ
naḍapidanendu sindhutanayaṁ kaḍukeydisanintu pāḍugā
doḍanoḍanirvaruṁ meṟeyalende śarāsana vidyeyiṁ paḍa
lvaḍisidarettamittamidiroḷ maledoḍḍida cāturaṅgamaṁ // ViVi.18 [campakamāle]

antu kiṟidu poḻtu keygādu kāde saritsutana suriva sarala
maḻeyoḷaḻida nija varūthiniya sāvuṁ nōvumēvamaṁ māḍe—

munideraḍambinoḷ rathamumaṁ padavillumaneyde pārdu ne
kkane kaḍidindra nandananaḷurkeyinārdoḍe divya sindhu naṁ
dananiradēṟi bēṟe rathamaṁ peṟatondu śarāsanakke me
llane niḍudōḷanuydu karamaccariyāge kaḍaṅgikādidaṁ // ViVi.19 [campakamāle]

antu tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgaderdegāya[lekka]yinembattu nālku lakka
baṇḍiyoḷ taṇḍa taṇḍade tīvidakāṇḍa praḷayānaḷa visphuliṅgōpamānaṅgaḷappa
niśita kāṇḍaṅgaḷindoḍḍida caturbalaṅgaḷa meyyoḷ rōma rōmandappade
naḍuvannameccu payiñchāsirvar makuṭabaddharumanondu lakka madadāneyumaṁ
mūṟu lakka rathamumanondu kōṭi turuṣka turaṅgaṅgaḷumaṁ padineṇṭu
kōṭi padātiyumanalasade pēsēḻe kondu paraśurāmanalli paḍeda
divyāstraṅgaḷanondanondu sūḻoḷe toṭṭu—

nuḍivaḷige narana rathamaṁ
paḍuveṇgāvuduvaraṁ siḍilvinamecca

[p. 285]
ccuḍiye bhujabalade hariyura
deḍeyaṁ biriyeccu meṟedanaḷavaṁ bhīṣmaṁ // ViVi.20 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ—

dēvāsuradoḷamindina
nōvaṁ nondaṟiyenuḻida keyduvinoḷivaṁ
sāvane seragaṁ bagedoḍe
sāvādapudendu cakri cakradoḷiṭṭaṁ // ViVi.21 [kandaṁ]

iṭṭoḍe tanagasurāriya
koṭṭa mahā vaiṣṇavāstramaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ
toṭṭisuvudumeraḍuṁ kiḍi
guṭṭi siḍil siḍiyepōrduvambarataḷadoḷ // ViVi.22 [kandaṁ]

pōrvudumiṁ peṟatambiṁ
tīrvude pageyendu pāśupatamaṁ piḍiyal
pārvudumarjunanāgaḷ
bērverasu kiḻalke bageye surareḍevokkar // ViVi.23 [kandaṁ]

ā prastāvadoḷ—

ennumanasurāriya piḍi
vunnata karacakramendu bhīṣmaṁ taṟiguṁ
munnamaḍaṅguvenembavo
lannegamastācaḷasthanādaṁ dinapaṁ // ViVi.24 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisimunnottidavēḷegaḷ
samudraṅgaḷaṁ puguvante tantamma bīḍugaḷaṁ pokkarāgaḷ—

barisi manegasura vairiya
narasaṁ bhīṣmaṅge cakramintēke mogaṁ
diridudo nimmaṁ piḍidena
garidenalariduṇṭe dhuradoḷēnasurārī // ViVi.25 [kandaṁ]


[p. 286]
besasene nuḍidaṁ muraneṁ
basurananenagāgi kādi bhīṣmaṁ piḍido
ppisidoḍe vaiṣṇava bāṇama
nosedittenadaṁ gelalkekeydugaḷoḷavē // ViVi.26 [kandaṁ]

bhēdadoḷallade gelalari
dādaṁ surasindhusutananindiruḷoḷ nīṁ
bhēdisene nr̥patiyorvane
ādaradiṁ bandu sindhusutanaṁ kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.27 [kandaṁ]

kaṇḍu poḍevaṭṭu nayamerde
goṇḍire pati nuḍidanenage dēvar kaluṣaṁ
goṇḍāgaḷ kāvar kaṇe
goṇḍavolendemba mātinantāgiradē // ViVi.28 [kandaṁ]

toṁmbaysāsirvar ni
mmambina bambaloḷe makuṭabaddhar‌ maḍidar
nambiṁ nambalimindiṁ
gombattu dinaṁ dalemma bennale nindir‌ // ViVi.29 [kandaṁ]

cakriya cakradoḷaṁ toḍa
rdākramisidudecca nija patatri dalene ni
mmī krama kamalakkeṟagade
vakrisi bhūcakradoḷage bāḻvarumoḷarē // ViVi.30 [kandaṁ]

sāve nimaticceyene poṇa

endoḍadellamaneyde kēḷdu karuṇārasahr̥dayanāgi mammana mogamaṁ

jagadoḷavadhyanaṁgelale bāradadādoḍamēṁ śikhaṇḍi to
ṭṭage koḷe bandu munde nile sāvenagappudu nāḷinondu kā

[p. 287]
ḷegadoḷidaṁ naraṅgaṟipadī teṟadiṁ negaḻdeyde vīra la
kṣmige neleyāgu pōgene nr̥paṁ poḍevaṭṭu manōnurāgadiṁ // ViVi.32 [campakamāle]

bandu mandaradharaṅge tadvr̥ttāntamanellamanaṟipi niścinta mananāgi
pavaḍisidāgaḷ—

cala caladāntu kāduva suyōdhana sādhanadoḍḍugaḷ kaḻa

āgaḷ kurudhvajiniyumanēka śaṅkha kāhaḷa bhērī paṇava jhallarī mr̥daṅga

isuva dhanurdharariṁ pā

suḻisuḻidoḍavariduvu ka
lpaḻiyoḷ bhōrgaredu pariva toṟegaḷa teṟadiṁ // ViVi.36 [kandaṁ]

antu cāturdantamondondaṟoḷōrante naḍuvagalvaraṁ kāduvuduṁ

[p. 288]
kurubalamembudī suranadījana tōḷvalamemba vajra paṁ

antu tāguvuduṁ sātyaki kr̥tavarmanoḷ yudhiṣṭhiraṁ śalyanoḷ

antu kiḍiguṭṭidante taḷtiṟiye jagadēkamallaṅge mārmaleyalāṟade

antu tāgida sindhunandanana kōpaśikhi śikhākaḷāpaṅgaḷoḷ

śarasandhānada bēgamambugaḷanaṁmbīmbante mēṇambinā

[p. 289]
antu bhīṣmaṁ grīṣmakāladādityanante kāydantakāladantakanante keḷardu

maṇimakuṭāḷigaḷverasuruḷda narēndra śiraṅgaḷoḷphaṇā
maṇigaḷa dīptigaḷ beḷage dhātriyanoyyane kaṇḍi māḍi kaṇ

seṇasiduvendoḍēvogaḻvudērvesanaṁ surasindhu putranā // ViVi.41 [campakamāle]

antu sōmaka balamellamaṁ pēḻe pesarilladantu kondu śrī jaya

mōjassaubhadra ghaṭōtkaca bhīmasēna nakula sahadēva sātyaki pañcapāṇḍava
pramukha nāyakarellarumberasu dharmaputraṁ śikhaṇḍiyaṁ mundiṭṭukoṇḍu bandu
pēṅkuḷigoṇḍa siṁhamaṁ muttuvante sutti muttidāgaḷ—

ambaramellamambinoḷe pūḻe mahībhujarettamecca ki
ttambugaḷettamavvaḷise māṇadavaṁ kaḍidikki tanna na
llambugaḷindamārdiradaḍurtise bhūbhujarellamalli bi
lluṁ beṟagāge bandu poṇardaṁ seragillade vikramārjunaṁ // ViVi.42 [utpalamālike]

antu poṇardāgaḷemma mammaṅgamemagamīgaḷanuvaraṁ dore

toṭṭeccāgaḷ—

jvaḷana patatriyaṁ kaḍidu vāruṇa patriyinaindra bāṇamaṁ

ccaḷise nadījanuccaḷise kādidanēṁ kaliyō guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.43 [campakamāle]

gaḷoḷ dharmaputraṅge tanna nuḍida nuḍivaḷiyaṁ nenedallaḷigāḷegaṅgāde—


[p. 290]
kaḍidanudagranāyakara sāyakamellamanā śikhaṇḍi po

giḍanavanāṅkegoḷḷanagiyaṁ sugiyaṁ sura sindhunandanaṁ // ViVi.44 [campakamāle]

idu raṇamennoḷāntiṟiva meygaliyuṁsamaraikamēruve
nnadaṭumaḷurkeyuṁ piridu pēḍigadentidirāmpenendaṇaṁ

rvidira siḍimbinoḷ pudidadondu kuḷācaḷadante sindhujaṁ // ViVi.45 [campakamāle]

tintiṇiyāge naṭṭa kaṇeyoḷ nela muṭṭade meyyoḷattami

ddhāntada śāsanaṁ bareda pottageyantamarāpagātmajaṁ // ViVi.46 [utpalamālike]

naḍedudu bāḷakāladoḷe toṭṭenagaṅkada śaucavīgaḷō
gaḍipude muṭṭi nāṁ nelananēkadupeṇgaḍimendu meyyoḷa
ḻdiḍida vikarṇa kōṭiyoḷaṇaṁ nela muṭṭade nōḍe biḻdoḍaṁ

antu śarapañjaradoḷoṟagiyumoḍaliṁ pattuviṭṭu pōpa jīvamaṁ

[p. 291]
antu śōkaṅgeydoḍe nīmantenalvēḍa kṣatriyadharmamintadarkaḻalvēḍa

embuduṁ duryōdhananintendaṁ—

adaṭinaḷurkeyaṁ baladaḷurkeyumaṁ geḍegoṇḍu nīmidā

āgaḷ duryōdhananātmīya sēnānāyakanappa gāṅgēyaṁ bidira

kr̥pa kr̥tavarmāśvatthāma śalya śakuni saindhava bhūriśravaḥ prabhr̥tigaḷgellaṁ

āytēsādhisikoṇḍu pāṇḍusutaraṁ naṇpiṅge bennittu dal
saytāytajjana mātu namma paḍeyaṁ kāvannarinnāro su

rdvaitaṁ bīrada bīravaṭṭamanidaṁ nirvyājadiṁ kaṭṭuvaṁ // ViVi.52 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 292]
embuduṁ karṇanintendaṁ—

surasindhūdbhavaniṁ baḻikke peṟarār sēnādhipatyakketa
kkare lōkaikadhanurdharaṁ kaḷaśajaṁ takkaṁ nadīnandanaṁ
ge raṇakkāṁ neramādenappoḍinitēkādappudī poḻte po
ḻtiravēḍīvudu bīravaṭṭamanadaṁ drōṇaṅge nīṁ bhūpatī // ViVi.53 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu bhīṣmādanantaraṁ drōṇayembudu parāśara vacanamene karṇana
nuḍigoḍambaṭṭu—

visasana raṅgakkānire
besagoḷvude peṟaranendu jaya paṭahaṅgaḷ
desedesegesevinegaṁ ka
ṭṭisikoṇḍaṁ bīravaṭṭamaṁ kaḷaśabhavaṁ // ViVi.54 [kandaṁ]

antu kumbhasambhavananēka śātakumbha kumbhasambhr̥ta maṅgaḷa gaṅgā
jalaṅgaḷiṁ pavitrīkr̥ta gātranāgi kaurava baḷāgragaṇyanāgirdanitta tadvr̥ttānta
manellamanajātaśatru kēḷdu janārdananoḍane ripubaḷa mardanōpāyamaṁ

adaṭaṁ sindhutanūbhavaṁ vijayanoḷ mārkoṇḍaṇaṁ kādalā
ṟade bembiḻdoḍe kādalendu besanaṁ pūṇdaṁ gaḍaṁ drōṇanaṁ
taduvaṁ nōḍuvenendu kaṇ taṇivinaṁ nōḍalke barpante baṁ
dudayādrīndramanēṟe bhānu poṟamaṭṭoḍḍittanīkārṇavaṁ // ViVi.55 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ pāṇḍava balada sēnānāyakaṁ dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanoḍḍida vajravyūhakke
padmavyūhamanoḍḍi tadvyūhada monege vandu—

śōṇāśvaṅgaśaḷ rajata rathamaṁ poḍe kumbhadhvajaṁ gī
rvāṇāvāsambaramaḍare māḻoḍḍudal sāladennī
bāṇāvāsakkenutumaḷavaṁ bīṟutuṁ bilge jāṇaṁ
drōṇaṁ nindaṁ masagi tiruputtondu kūrambanāgaḷ // ViVi.56 [mandākrānte]

ā sakaḷa dharādhīśara
bīsuva kuñcamane pārdu bīsaloḍaṁ ke

[p. 293]
yvīsaloḍamaṟidu tāgidu
vāsukaraṁ berasu taḍeyadubhaya balaṅgaḷ // ViVi.57 [kandaṁ]

antu cāturdantamondondaṟoḷ tāgi taḷtiṟivalli talegaḷ paṟiye
barigaḷ muṟiye toḍegaḷuḍiye puṇgaḷ suliye—

oḍane nabhambaraṁ siḍilva pandale sūsuva kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷ
toḍare teraḷda nettara kaḍal neṇadoḷgesaṟoḷ jigiltagu
rvaḍare nirantaraṁ poḷeva bāḷuḍi suyva nava vraṇaṅgaḷoḷ
poḍare podaḻdudadbhuta bhayānakamāhava raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.58 [campakamāle]

āgaḷeraḍuṁ balada sēnānāyakarondorvaroḷ kāduvāgaḷ
kumbhasambhavaṁ dharmaputrana moneyoḷ bharaṅgeydu kāduvāgaḷ—

dhvajamaṁ khaṇḍisi pūṇdubāṇadoḷe dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanaṁ neṭṭano
ṭṭajeyiṁ tūḷdi śikhaṇḍiyaṁ drupadanaṁ kāypindamēsāḍi mi
kku javaṁ kolvavolātaniṁ kiṟiyaraṁ pannorvaraṁ kondu ma
tsyajanaṁ māṇade kondanonde śaradiṁ niśyaṅkanaṁ śaṅkanaṁ // ViVi.59 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ sālvala dēśadarasaṁ cēkitsaṁ praḷaya kālada mēgha ghaṭegaḷenisu

ōronde pāreyambino
ḷōronde gajēndramuruḷe tege neṟedecce
ccōraṇadoḷ cēkitsana
nārumagurvise ghaṭōdbhavaṁ taṟidārdaṁ // ViVi.60 [kandaṁ]

antu pāṇḍava balamellamanallakallōlaṁ māḍi kaḷaśakētananajāta

kādal saṁsaptakarkaḷ karedoḍavara bennaṁ taguḷdāda kāypiṁ
kāduttirpātanantā kaḷakaḷamanadaṁ kēḷdu bhōrendu bande
ccā divyāstraṅgaḷiṁ tammovajarugiye tammaṇṇanaṁ śauryadindaṁ
kādaṁ muṁbijjanaṁkādariganuḻidaraṁ kāvudēṁ cōdyamāytē // ViVi.61 [sragdhare]


[p. 294]
āgaḷ mārtāṇḍaṁ pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana śara nikara sphurita kiraṇaṅgaḷ
kaviye tanna kiraṇaṅgaḷ masuḷdaparajaḷanidhigiḻidanāgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra
tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisidāgaḷ—

paḍegaḷeraḍuṁ bīḍiṅgettaṁ teraḷdu negaḻteyaṁ
paḍedaḻidaraṁ meccuttutsāhadiṁ pogaḻuttumo
ḷpaḍare nuḍiyuttantirdādityanandudayādriya
ttaḍare poṟamaṭṭāgaḷ bandoḍḍi ninduvu kōpadiṁ // ViVi.62 [hariṇīplutaṁ]

antoḍḍi ninda cātu
rdantaṁ keyvīsuvannegaṁ sairisadō
rante peṇediṟiduvante di
gantāntamaneydi pariye nettara toṟegaḷ // ViVi.63 [kandaṁ]

aḻgida bilvaḍe māṇade
taḻgida rathameydebagidapuṇgaḷa poṟeyiṁ
moḻgida kari ghaṭe javanaḍu
vaḻgeyananukarise vīra bhaṭa raṇaraṅgaṁ // ViVi.64 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ dhr̥ṣṭakētu vr̥ṣasēnanoḷ sātyaki bhagadattanoḷ drupada
dhr̥ṣṭadyumnarirvaruṁ drōṇācāryanoḷ prativindhyaṁ saubalanoḷ
ghaṭōtkacaṁ karṇanoḷ peṇedu kāde—

posa maseyambugaḷ desegaḷaṁ masuḷvannegameydepāye pā
yisuva rathaṅgaḷā rathada kīlmuṟidāgaḷe keyyanalli kō
desaguva sūtarambu koḷe sūtaruruḷdumiḷātaḷakke pā
ydasiyeḷe tāgi taḷtiṟiva niccaṭaroppidārājiraṅgadoḷ // ViVi.65 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ kaḷiṅgarājana gajaghaṭegaḷanitumondāgi bhīmasēnana rathamaṁ
viḷaya kāḷa jaḷadharaṅgaḷellamondāgi kulagiriyaṁ muttuvante sutti
muttidāgaḷ—

rathadiṁ dhātrige pāydu koṇḍu gadeyaṁ keysārdudasmanmanō
rathamindendu kaḍaṅgi māṇade siḍil poyvantevōl poyvuduṁ
rathayūtha dhvaja śastraśaṅkha[puṭa]doḷ ghaṇṭāsamētaṁ mahā
rathanindaṁ kuḷaśaiḷadante karigaḷ bīḻtanduvugrājiyoḷ // ViVi.66 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 295]
madavaddantigaḷaṁ kaṟuttasagavoylpoydājiyoḷ bhīmanā
rdodedīḍāḍidoḍattajāṇḍa taṭamaṁtāpannegaṁ pāṟi tā
ṟida pērāneyoḍalgaḷabhrataḷadoḷ silkirduvōrondu mā
ṇade bīḻtarpuvu beṭṭu bīḻva teṟadindinnuṁ kurukṣētradoḷ // ViVi.67 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

toḍare taḍaṅgāl poydoḍe
keḍeduṁ tividoḍe suruḷdu mōdidoḍirade
lvaḍagāgi maḍidu biḻduvu
gaḍaṇade karighaṭegaḷēṁ balasthano bhīmaṁ // ViVi.68 [kandaṁ]

antalli padinālsāsira madadāneyumaṁkaḷiṅganāyakaṁ bhānudattaṁ
modalāge nūrvararasumakkaḷumaṁ kondoḍe kaurava balamellamollanu
lidōḍi bhagadattanāneya maṟeyaṁ pokkāgaḷ—

negaḻdeṁ dēvēndranairāvatada keḷeyanennēṟidīyāneyuṁ dal
digibhaṁ duryōdhanaṁ naccidanenagidiraṁ bhīmaneḻtandanīgaḷ
mugilaṁ muṭṭittu sandennaḷavumadaṭuvendārdu dōrdarpayuktaṁ
bhagadattaṁ supratīkadvipamanupacitōtsāhadiṁ tōṟikoṭṭaṁ // ViVi.69 [mahāsragdhare]

mada kariya pariva bharadiṁ
dadirdoḍe nelanoḍḍi ninda caduraṅgamumo
rmodale naḍugidudu kūḍida
caduraṅgada maṇeyanalgidantappinegaṁ // ViVi.70 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷasuranuyda nelananādi varāhanaṟasalendu sakaḷa jaḷacarakaḷita
jaḷanidhigaḷaṁ kalaṅkuvante pāṇḍava baḷa jaḷanidhiyanaḷikuḷa jhēṅkāra mukharita
viśāla karaṭa taṭamā diśāgajēndraṁ kalaṅke—

taḷardudu karṇatāḷa pavanāhatiyiṁ jaḷarāśi keyya ba
ḷvaḷikege diggajaṁ deseyinatta teraḷduvu kāypiniṁ diśā
vaḷiverasambaraṁ pogedu pottidudāda madāmbuviṁ jagaṁ
jaḷadhivolāytadaṁ neṟeye baṇṇiparār gaḷa supratīkamaṁ // ViVi.71 [campakamāle]


[p. 296]
kara nakha danta ghātadinuruḷva caturbaladiṁ teraḷva ne
ttara kaḍalā kaḍalvaregameyde mahā makaraṁ samudradoḷ
parivavolintagurvuverasā bhagadattana kāloḷantadēṁ
paridudo supratīka gajamaccariyappinamāji raṅgadoḷ // ViVi.72 [campakamāle]

antu parida bīdigaḷoḷellaṁ nettara toṟegaḷ pariye keṇḍada toṟe
[yante]parida supratīkaṁkeyya kāla kōḍēṟinoḷ balamanellaṁ javanejivuḷiduḻivante toḻtuḻiduḻidu padinālsāsira madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷu
manondu lakkarathamumanaredusaṇṇisidante māḍidāgaḷ gajāsuranoḷāsuraṁ
berasu tāguvandhakārātiyante bhīmasēnaṁ bandu poṇare—

tolagidu supratīka gajamāṁ bhagadattanenilli ninna tō
ḷvalada poḍarpu salladele sāyade pōgene kēḷdu bhīmanāṁ
toleyadirurkinoḷ nuḍiveyī kari sūkariyalte patti gaṁ
ṭalanoḍeyotti kondapenidaltidaṟammanumennanāmpudē // ViVi.73 [campakamāle]

endu nārācaṅgaḷiṁ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgadantu supratīka kariyemba
giriya mēle bhīmanemba kālamēghaṁ sarala sariyaṁ suriye—

siḍileṟapandadindeṟagi dikkari tanna varūthamaṁ paḍa
lvaḍise marutsutaṁ muḷidu maccaradiṁ gajegoṇḍu suttugoṁ
ḍaḍigiḍe nurgipoydu peṟapiṅguvuduṁ kari nondu kōpadiṁ
piḍideṟagittu bhīmananagurvisi pāṇḍava sainyamaḷkuṟal // ViVi.74 [campakamāle]

anteṟagidoḍe kōḍakeyya kāleḍegaḷoḷbiṇpumaṁ[peṇe]vanda
diṁdērduḍokkaraṅgoṇḍu kurukṣētradindatta panneraḍu yōjanambara
mottuvuduṁ—

kariyuṁ kuru bhūmiya naḍu
varegaṁ pavanajananotte tōḷvalamāgaḷ
sari sariyādudu taddi
kkarigaṁ bhīmaṅgamugra saṅgara dhareyoḷ // ViVi.75 [kandaṁ]


[p. 297]
annegamitta saṁsaptakabalamellamanaḷaṟe peḷaṟekivuḻeduḻidu kolva
vikrāntatuṁgaṁ cakriyanintendaṁ—

paridudu supratīkagajamēṟidavaṁ bhagadattanā mada
dviradamanāṅkegoṇḍu peṇevaṁ pavanātmajanīgaḷāhavaṁ
piridudalatta pōpamene tadrathamaṁ hari vāyuvēgadiṁ
pariyise tāgidaṁ hariganaṅkada poṅkada supratīkamaṁ // ViVi.76 [campakamāle]

antu tāgi mr̥garāja nakhara mārgaṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ kūrmanakhāstraṅgaḷoḷa
māneyumaṁ bhagadattanumaṁ pūḻdoḍe bhagadattaṁ muḷidubhūdattamappa
divyāṅkuśamaṁ koṇḍu—

iḍuvudumadu vilayāgniya
kiḍigaḷanuguḻuttumeydevarpudumidiraṁ
naḍedajaranuradināntoḍe
tuḍugevolesedirdudaṅkuśaṁ kandharadoḷ // ViVi.77 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ cōdyambaṭṭidēnendu besagoḷe—

idu peṟataltu bhūtalamanāṁ taralādi varāhanādenaṁ
dadaṟa viṣāṇamaṁ baḻiyamā vasudhāṅganegittēnītanā
sudatiyapautranāke kuḍe bandudivaṅgenagalladānalā
gadudaṟinānteniṁ taṟivudī kari kandharamaṁ guṇārṇavā // ViVi.78 [campakamāle]

embudumonde divyaśaradiṁ śiramaṁ paṟiyeccoḍātano
ttambadināntoḍāṁ baṟide tappidenendu kirīṭi tanna bi
llaṁ bisuṭirdoḍacyutanidētarinākulamirdenōḍideṁ
tembudumeccananteraḍu keygaḷumaṁ muḷisiṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.79 [utpalamālike]

eccavana taleyumaṁ paṟi
yeccoḍe dikkariya taleyumātana taleyuṁ
paccikkidante keygaḷu
maccariyappinegamoḍanuruḷduvu dhareyoḷ // ViVi.80 [kandaṁ]


[p. 298]
ittarigaṅgamitra jayamappudumattamararkaḷārdu sū
suttire puṣpavr̥ṣṭigaḷanōgaravūgaḷa baṇḍaneyde pī
ruttoḍavanduvindra vanadiṁ maṟidumbigaḷindra nīlamaṁ
muttumanōḷiyōḷiyoḷe kōdeḻalikkida māleyantevōl // ViVi.81 [utpalamālike]

dharaṇī sutanaḻidaṁ di
kkari keḍedudu nara śaraṅgaḷiṁ bhuvanamumi
nnuriyadiradānaḍaṅguve
niradembavolarkanapara jaḷanidhigiḻidaṁ // ViVi.82 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisi tantamma bīḍugaḷge
pōpuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ bhagadattana sāviṅgaḻaldu toṭṭa sannaṇamanappoḍaṁ
kaḷeyadeyumaramanege pōgade kumbhasambhavanalligevandu—

masakaṅgundada supratīka gajamaṁ dhātrīsutaṁ kīṟi cō
disi bhīmaṁ gele muṭṭevandu hariyuṁ tānuṁ bharaṅgeydu ta
nnesakaṁ gāyadadharmayuddhade naraṁ kolvalli kaṇḍintupē
kṣisi nīmuṁ naḍe nōḍutirdirene mattinnāranāṁ nambuveṁ // ViVi.83 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu nuḍida pannagadhvajana nuḍige kārmukācāryanintendaṁ—

enagaltārgamasādhyanalte vijayaṁ nīnātanaṁ gelva mā
tanamōghaṁ bisuḍinde nāḷe vijayaṁ mārkoḷḷadandurki po
kkananāntorvananikkuveṁ kadanadoḷ mēṇ kaṭṭuveṁ dharma naṁ
dananaṁ nīnidanintu nambu bageyalvēḍannanaṁbhūpatī // ViVi.84 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embudumāninitaṁ nimmapūṇisale bandenendu poḍemaṭṭu
bīḻkoṇḍu pōgi saṁsaptakarkaḷge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi—

arigananāmpa gaṇḍumadaṭuṁ nimagāvagamādudāhavā
jiradoḷadarke nāḷe naranaṁ tegeduyvudu dharmaputranaṁ
guru piḍidappanendavaranāgaḷe pūṇisi pōgavēḻdu ma
ccaradoḷe māṇadoḍḍidanasuṅgoḷekakkara sañje sañjeyoḷ // ViVi.85 [campakamāle]


[p. 299]
āgaḷ pāṇḍava patākiniyumirade poṟamaṭṭardhacandravyūhamanoḍḍi
nile saṁsaptakar‌ tamage miḻtugarevante vikramārjunanaṁ kareduydaritta—

aṟipidaṁ guru bhārgavanintīyoḍdanidaṁ gelalāvanuṁ
neṟeyanurkinaḷurkeyinorvaṁ pokkoḍe pokkanemattaṇaṁ
poṟamaḍaṁtaṟidoṭṭuvenantā pāṇḍava sainyamanendu bi
lleṟeyanoḍḍidanaṅkada cakravyūhamanāhava raṅgadoḷ // ViVi.86 [anavadyaṁ]

antoḍḍida cakravyūhada naḍuveḍeyaṟidu kaḷiṅga rājana karighaṭegaḷumaṁ
karṇa śalya śakuni kr̥pa kr̥tavarma bhūriśravōśvatthāma duryōdhana vr̥ṣasēna
lakkaṇādigaḷappatiratha mahāratha samarathārdharatharkaḷanirisi mattamavara
baḷasiyumanēka sāmajabalamberasu jayatsēna sudakṣiṇa kāmbhōjādi nāyakara
nirisi mattamavara keladoḷeḍeyaṟidu bakāsura jaṭāsurara makkaḷappaḷambhūṣaṇa
haḷāyudha musaḷāyudha kāḷa nīḷa rūkṣa rākṣasa balamanirisi mattamavara
keladoḷivargivar pāsaṭiyāgirpudendu ninda neleyoḷ taḷarade nilvantāgirisi
guheya bāgiloḷ siṁhamirpandadiṁ bhāradvājaṁ sindhurājamberasu
cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ neṟedu meṟedu nindāgaḷ dharmaputranēgeyva
teṟanumanaṟiyadabhimanyuvaṁ karedintendaṁ—

idu cakravyūhamī vyūhamanoḍevadaṭaṁ pārthanantātanuṁ geṁ
ṭidanemmī nālvaruṁ bhēdisalaṟiyevidaṁ kanda nīṁ ballapēḻeṁ
budumānemmayyanalkēḷdaṟivenidanidēnayya cintāntaraṁ po
kkidanīgaḷ vanya gandhadviradame koḷanaṁ pokkavōl kādi tōrpeṁ // ViVi.87 [mahāsragdhare]

analana koṭṭa gāṇḍivada tēra murāriya meccadēva dē
vana dayegeyda sāyakada bembaladoḷ kaliyendu kemmana
mmananadaṭaḻgutirpiravidēṁpageyoḍḍu gelalkaḷumbameṁ
banituvaraṁ manakke nimagattaḷagaṁ bare matte māṇbenē // ViVi.88 [campakamāle]


[p. 300]
neṟedu caturvalamberasu banduṟadoḍḍida gaṇḍarārume
nnaṟiyada gaṇḍarē negeda nettara suṭṭure kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷ
paṟidu nabhambaraṁ paredu parvi layāgni śikhākaḷāpamaṁ
maṟeyise tāgi taḷtiṟiyadannegamentu naraṅgevuṭṭideṁ // ViVi.89 [campakamāle]

embuduṁ yamanandananintendaṁ—

anuvaradalli taḷtu pageyaṁ tave kondoḍamāntarāti sā
dhanadoḷagaḻgi taḻgidoḍamennaya santatigāgisirda ni
nnane mada danti danta musalāhatigaṁ karavāḷa bāygamaṁ
bina monegaṁ mahārathara tintiṇigaṁ piḍidentu nūṅkuveṁ // ViVi.90 [campakamāle]

magane padinālku varuṣada
maganai ninnannanorvanaṁ pagevaḍeyo
ḍḍugaḷanoḍeyalkevēḻderde
dhagamene sairisuvupāyamāvudu kaṟuvē // ViVi.91 [kandaṁ]

endoḍā mātaṁ mārkoṇḍabhimanyuvintendaṁ—

kramamaṁ keykoḷalendu puṭṭi raṇadoḷ sāvannegaṁ māṇdoḍa
kramamakkuṁ kramamakkumē kramamanānēgeydapeṁ vikramaṁ
kramamāṁ vikramadātaneṁkramada mātantirke māṇdirdoḍāṁ
kramakendirdene biṭṭoḍaṁ biḍadoḍaṁ bīḻkoṇḍeniṁ māṇbenē // ViVi.92 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

endu tannēṟida kanaka rathamaṁ tanna manadannanappa jayanemba sārathiyaṁ
cōdisendāgaḷ—

eṟaguva baṭṭinambugaḷa balsari kumbhajanaṁ maraḷcepā
ydaṟikeya pāreyambugaḷa tandalagurvisi sindhurājanaṁ
maṟugise bāgiloḷ musuṟi ninda ghaṭāvaḷiyaṁ teraḷci ta
ttaṟadaṟidotti pokkanabhimanyu virōdhi baḷāmbu rāśiyaṁ // ViVi.93 [campakamāle]

antu pokku virōdhi sainyamaṁ māri pokkante peṇamayaṁ māḍi
tūrikoṇḍa jōḷadantire paḍalvaḍisidāgaḷ—

oṇagidudondu pervidira pervodaṟiṁ moredurvuvāśuśu
kṣaṇiyavolānta khaḻga nivahakke rathakke daḻakke matta vā

[p. 301]
raṇa nivahakke takkinabhimanyuva kūrgaṇe pāydu nuṅgaluṁ
ṭoṇeyalumurci mukkalumidēṁ neṟe kaltuvo yuddharaṅgadoḷ // ViVi.94 [campakamāle]

antidirānta mārpaḍeyellamaṁ javana paḍege paḍigaccikkuvantikkininda
naranandananaṁ kaṇḍu vikramakkaṁ kramakkaṁ puruḍisuva suyōdhanana makkaḷ lakkaṇaṁ
modalāge nūrvarumondāge bandu tāgidāgaḷ—

sūḻaisecceccu billaṁ rathada kudureyaṁ sūtanaṁ khaṇḍisuttā
ṟēḻeṇṭombattu pattembaṟikeya saralindūṟikoṇḍāva meyyuṁ
pāḻembantāge pārdārduṟadise muḷisiṁ nūrvaruṁ ponnatāḻgaḷ
sūṟoḷ bīḻvante biḻdar makuṭa maṇigaṇadyōtisārar kumārar // ViVi.95 [sragdhare]

āgaḷ suyōdhanana makkaḷa sāvaṁ kaṇḍu tammaṇṇana mogamanāva
mogadoḷ nōḻpenendu duśyāsanaṁ bandu tāgidāgaḷ—

onde saralindamavanerde
yaṁ dokkane tiṇṇameccu kolalollanesaṁ
krandananandana tanayaṁ
tandeya pūṇkeyane nenedu duśyāsananaṁ // ViVi.96 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ kānīna sūnu vr̥ṣasēnanēnuṁmāṇade kāduttirdanannegamitta
naranandanana baḻivaḻiyaṁ taguḷdu gaḻevaḻiya pāvinante cakravyūhamaṁ
pugalendu barpa drupada virāṭa dhr̥ṣṭadyumna bhīmasēna sahadēva nakula yudhiṣṭhira
ghaṭōtkacādigaḷoḍane mallāmalliyāgi kāduva kumbhasambhavanallige
duryōdhanaṁ bandu namma balamellamabhimanyuvinambina moneyoḷ tūḷdu
teraḷdōḍidappudu nimagalli kāḷegamati bharamēgeyvamene sindhurājanindinanu
varakīyeḍeyoḷenitādoḍamīśvara varaprasādadoḷāne sālvenendintendaṁ—

uṟadidirāntu ninda ripu sainyamanāhava raṅgadalli ta
ttaṟadaṟidikkalāṁ neṟeveninniravēḍoḍagoṇḍu pōgu ni
nnaṟikeya kumbhasambhavananendoḍe pāṇḍava sainyamaṁ kaṟu
ttiṟivanitondaḷurke ninagētaṟoḷādudo pēḻ jayadrathā // ViVi.97 [campakamāle]


[p. 302]
ene jayadrathanintendaṁ—

naranoḷ munnagapaṭṭudondaḻaloḷāṁ kaiḷāsa śaiḷēśanaṁ
piriduṁ bhaktiyoḷarcisuttumire taddēvādhipaṁ meccideṁ
naranorvaṁ poṟagāgalondu divasaṁ kauntēyaraṁ kādi gel
nirutaṁ nīnene pettenāṁ baramanadrīndrātmajādhīśanoḷ // ViVi.98 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

enda sindhurājana nuḍige rājādhirājaneraḍu muyvumaṁ nōḍi—

ninnane nacci pāṇḍavaroḷāntiṟiyal taṟisandu pūṇdenāṁ
ninna śarāḷigaḷgagidu ninduvu pāṇḍava sainyamendoḍiṁ
ninna bhujapratāpadaḷavārgamasādhyamāytadēṁ
ninnaḷavindaminnenage sārdudarāti jayaṁ jayadrathā // ViVi.99 [utpalamālike]

endu pogaḻdu sindhurājananiralvēḻdu kumbhasambhavanuṁ tānu
mabhimanyuvina saṅgrāma raṅgamaneyde vandu—

uḍida rathaṅgaḷiṭṭeḍegaḷoḷ makuṭaṅgaḷa ratnadīptigaḷ
poḍarvinamaḻgi taḻgida nijātmajaraṁ naḍe nōḍi kaṇṇa nī
roḍanoḍanurcipāye muḷisindadanoyyane tāḷdi kāypinoḷ
kaḍagi jagaṁṅgaḷaṁ noṇedu nuṅgalumāṭisidaṁ suyōdhanaṁ // ViVi.100 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ drōṇa drōṇaputra kr̥pa kr̥tavarma karṇa śalya śakuni duśyāsana
vr̥ṣasēnādigaḷāḷdana muḷida mogamanaṟidu dharmayuddhamaṁ bisuṭu
naranandanana rathamaṁ suttimuttikoṇḍu—

tēraṁ kudureyanesaguva
sārathiyaṁ billanadaṟa goṇeyumanuṟadā
rdōrorvarondaneccoḍe
bīraṁ gadegoṇḍu bīraraṁ beṅkoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.101 [kandaṁ]

beṅkoḷe kaḷiṅga rājana
nūṅkida karighaṭeyanuḍiye baḍi baḍidettaṁ
kiṅkoḻemāḻpudumuṟade
ccaṁ karṇaṁ niśita śaradineraḍuṁ karamaṁ // ViVi.102 [kandaṁ]


[p. 303]
karameraḍuṁ paṟivudumā
karadindaṁ tanna kunnageyyoḷe koṇḍu
ddhura ratha cakradiniṭṭaṁ
tiripi narapriya tanūjanakṣōhiṇiyaṁ // ViVi.103 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ duśyāsanana magaṁ gadāyudhanaḻiye nonda siṅgada mēle
beragaṟiyada beḷḷāḷ pāyvante kiḻta bāḷverasu pāyvuduṁ—

sphurita kr̥pāṇa pāṇigidiraṁ naḍedaḷkuṟe toṭṭu vāydu ḍo
kkaradoḷe mikka dikkariyanikkuvavōl nelakikki patti ka
ttarigoḷe kāydu kaṇtumuḻdusir kusidantakanantameyde mey
paravaśavāge jōldanabhimanyu bhayaṅkara raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.104 [campakamāle]

anitaṇmi satta naranaṁ
danaṅge kaṇ sōltu bageyadamarēndranani
nnenage tanagemba dēvāṁ
ganeyara kaḷakaḷame piridumāytambaradoḷ // ViVi.105 [kandaṁ]

abhimanyu maraṇa vārtā
prabhūta śōkāgni dharmatanayananiradaṁ
dabhibhavisi tannanaḷurdaṁ |
te bhāskaraṁ keṅkamādanastācaladoḷ // ViVi.106 [kandaṁ]

antu nijatanūjana maraṇa śravaṇāśani ghātadiṁ kuḷaśailaṁ keḍevante
keḍedu mūrchāgatanāda dharmaputranaṁ bhīmasēna nakuḷa sahadēva sātyaki drupada
virāṭādigaḷapahatakadana‌r mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bīḍiṅge pōdarāgaḷ
dharmaputrana śōkamanāṟisalendu kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyanaṁ bandu saṁsāra
sthitiyanaṟiyadavarante nīnintu śōkākrāntanādoḍe—

enitidirāntarāti balamantanitaṁ tave kondutatsuyō
dhana sutarenna bāṇa gaṇadiṁ tavadirdaro yuddhadāḷge rō
danamenagāvudayyanenagēkeyo śōkipanendu dharmanaṁ
dana naranandanaṁ ninage saggadoḷēnabhimanyu nōyanē // ViVi.107 [campakamāle]


[p. 304]
jñānamayanāgi saṁsā
rānityateyaṁ jalakkanāgaṟidirda
jñāniyavōlnīnuṁ śō
kānalasantapta cittanappudu doreyē // ViVi.108 [kandaṁ]

endu ṣōḍaśa rājōpākhyānamanaṟipi dharmaputrana śōkamanāṟe
nuḍidu pārāśara munīndraṁ pōdanittal—

aḻidudu mattanūja śatamājiyoḷittabhimanyuvorvana
ttaḻidanidāvagellamenagaṁkaliyādano pūṇda gaṇḍavā
taḻiyade gaṇḍanintaḻivudīyaḻivinnenagāji raṅgadoḷ
gaḻiyisugembidaṁ nuḍiyutuṁ ghaṭasambhavanoḷ suyōdhanaṁ // ViVi.109 [campakamāle]

antu bīḍiṅge pōdanannegamitta saṁsaptaka baḷajaḷanidhiyaṁ baḍabānaḷana
ḷurvantaḷurdu nija vijaya kaṭakakke vijayaṁ baravare—

hari nijayōgadindaṟidu tannaḷiyaṁ layamādudaṁ bhayaṁ
kara kapi kētanaṅgaṟipalollade bandu śamanta pañcakaṁ
baramiḻidalli saṅgara pariśramamaṁ kaḷeyendu maydunaṁ
berasu jaḷāvagāhadoḷirutte mahā kapaṭa prapañcadiṁ // ViVi.110 [campakamāle]

jaḷamantra mantritāśaya
jaḷadoḷ naraninisu muḻuge nija sutanasuhr̥
dbaḷa jaḷanidhiyoḷ phalguṇa
muḻugidanembidane nuḍidu hari muḻuguvuduṁ // ViVi.111 [kandaṁ]

bhōṅkane kēḷderda kadaḍi ka
laṅkida bageverasu negedu nālkuṁ deseyaṁ
śaṅkākuḷitaṁ nōḍi ma
naṁkoḷukene muḻuginegeda hariyaṁ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.112 [kandaṁ]

ākāśa vacanamidu suta
śōkamanenagaṟipidappudasmattanayaṁ
gēkendaṟiyeṁ maraṇama
dā kurupatiyindamādudāgalevēḻkuṁ // ViVi.113 [kandaṁ]


[p. 305]
indina cakravyūhama
nāṁ dalaṇaṁ meccalāṟenenutuṁ rathamaṁ
bandēṟi magana manakata
monduttaramerdeyanaleya naranintendaṁ // ViVi.114 [kandaṁ]

kadanadināṁ bare niccalu
midirvandu koralge vāydu bāyvāyoḷalaṁ
pidirgoḷe tambulamaṁ ko
ḷḷade māṇdī magana taḍavidēnasurārī // ViVi.115 [kandaṁ]

enuttuṁ bīḍaneyde vandu śōkasāgaradoḷ muḻugāḍuva
parijanamuṁ tanna mogava nōḍal nāṇci taleyaṁ bāgi nalanaṁ bareyuttu
mirda vīrabhaṭarumaṁ kaṇḍu magana sāvaṁ niścayisi rājamandiramaṁ pokku
rathadindamiḻidu dharmaputraṅgaṁ vāyuputraṅgaṁ poḍevaṭṭu kuḷḷirpudumavar
taleyaṁ bāgi nelanaṁ bareyuttumire kirīṭi kaṇḍidēnendu besagoḷe
dharmaputranintendaṁ—

guru cakravyūhamaṁ paṇṇidoḍe pugalidaṁ ballarārendoḍiṁ nā
nire mattār ballarendorvane ripu baḷa vārāśiyaṁ pokku mikkāṁ
taranāṭandikki duryōdhanana tanayaraṁ nūrvaraṁ kondu tatsaṁ
garadoḷ kādemmanintāntiṟidu nijasutaṁ dēvalōkakke sandaṁ // ViVi.116 [mahāsragdhare]

baramaṁ bāḷa śaśāṅkamauḷi kuḍe pettondurkinindōvadāṁ
tu raṇōtsāhadinemmanorvane bharaṅgeydatta duryōdhanaṁ
berasā drōṇananaṭṭi sindhu viṣayādhīśaṁ podaḻdondu ma
ccaradiṁ ninna tanūjanaṁ kolisidaṁ mattāntavar kolvarē // ViVi.117 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

embuduṁ pracaṇḍa kōpa pāvaka praśamita śōkarasanumunnata lalāṭa
taṭa ghaṭita bhīṣaṇa bhrukuṭiyuṁ kalpānta dinakara durnirīkṣanumutpāta
mārutanante sakala bhūbhr̥tkampakāriyuṁ vindhyācaḷadante vardhamānōtsēdhanumandhakārātiyante bhairavākāranumāgi—

raseyiṁ bhūtaḷadiṁ kuḷādri kuḷadiṁ digdantiyiṁ vārdhiyiṁ
deseyindāgasadindajāṇḍa taṭadindattelli pokkirdumiṁ

[p. 306]
misukal tīrgume vairigenna sutanaṁ kondirdudaṁ kēḷdu sai
risi māṇdirdapeninnumendoḍidanāṁ pēḻētaṟoḷ nīguveṁ // ViVi.118 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

baḷeda suta śōkadindī
gaḷe surigumesuriyavā jayadrathana citā
naḷanindamogeda pogegaḷ
koḷe surivoḍe surivuvenna nayana jalaṅgaḷ // ViVi.119 [kandaṁ]

bisajabhavanakke mr̥ḍana
kkasurāntakanakke kāvoḍaṁ nāḷinoḷa
rvisekondu sindhu rājana
basiṟaṁ pōḻdenna magananāṁ tegeyadireṁ // ViVi.120 [kandaṁ]

kondenna magananiṁ bhaya
dindaṁ rasevokkumajana guṇḍigevokkuṁ
mandaradharanīporkuḻa
pondāvarevokku mēṇavaṁ bardukuvanē // ViVi.121 [kandaṁ]

paḍe paḍemeccegaṇḍanene sandarikēsariyembagurvu nē
rpaḍe negaḻdānaṇaṁseḍedu māṇbene nāḷe dinēśanastada
ttuḍugada munna saindhavanagurvise kolladoḍēno gāṇḍīvaṁ
biḍidane ciḥ tovalviḍidenallene vairige yuddharaṅgadoḷ // ViVi.122 [campakamāle]

endu nr̥pa paramātmaṁ kr̥tapratijñanādudaṁ saindhavana sajjanaṁ dujjōda
nana taṅge duśyaḷe kēḷdu malamala maṟugi tammaṇṇanallige vandu kālamēle
kavidu paṭṭu—

tanna sutanaḻiyalaḻiyal
ninnaya maydunananarjunaṁ pūṇdanada
rkānnaḍugi bandeninnī
nennōleya kaḍagadaḻivanēṁ nōḍidapā // ViVi.123 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ muguḷnage nakkintendaṁ—


[p. 307]
maruḷakkamagana śōkadi
nuruḷduṁ pūṇdavana pūṇke duśyāsananoḷ
karatanadindennoḷamā
marutsutaṁ pūṇdu pūṇkeyantevolakkuṁ // ViVi.124 [kandaṁ]

kr̥ta vividhāstraśastrayamaputra marutsutayajñasēnaru
ddhata baḷaretti kādi sugidōḍidarallarekāvarī viviṁ
śati kr̥pa karṇa śalya kaḷaśōdbhava tatpriya putrarendoḍa
pratirathanaṁ jayadrathananājiyoḷeytare varṣa gaṇḍarār // ViVi.125 [campakamāle]

endu duśyaḷeyanoḍagoṇḍu kumbhasambhavanallige vandintendaṁ—

suta śōkōdrēkadiṁ saindhavananaḻivenendarjunaṁ pūṇdanintī
sati bandaḷ kāvudātmānujeya kaḍagamaṁ nīme mārkoḷvoḍār tā
vitarar muṭṭal samarthar kadanadoḷene gelvāseyantirke sindhu
kṣitipaṁ tānēnanādaṁ raṇadoḷadane pōgānumappeṁ narēndrā // ViVi.126 [mahāsragdhare]

bijayaṅgeyyene pōpuduṁ nr̥panadaṁ dharmātmajaṁ kēḷdu pē
ḻdajitaṅgā hari pēḻdudondu nayadindā rātriyoḷ pōgi kuṁ
bhajanaṁ kaṇḍu vinamranāgi nuḍidaṁ nīmintu keykoṇḍu kā
de jagatpūjita beṭṭanādoḍemagiṁ bāḻvāseyāvāseyō // ViVi.127 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

nimmaḷavanaṟidu munname
nimma prārthisidemīgaḷaduvaṁ maṟedir
nimmaya dharmada makkaḷe
vemmaṁ kaḍegaṇisi nimage negaḻvudu doreyē // ViVi.128 [kandaṁ]

ene guru karuṇā rasamadu
manadiṁ poṟapoṇme ninage jayamakkumanaṁ
tana pēḻda teṟade negaḻene
vinayade bīḻkoṇḍu nr̥pati bīḍaṁ pokkaṁ // ViVi.129 [kandaṁ]


[p. 308]
āgaḷārūḍhasarvajñaṁ pratijñārūḍhanāgi gaṅgānadī taraṅgōpamāna
dukūlāmbara paridhānanumāgi dhavaḷa śayyātaḷadoḷ maṟedoṟagida[na]mō
ghāstra dhanañjayanaṁ puṇḍarīkākṣaṁ nōḍi—

aridu kolalke saindhavananājiyoḷītana pūṇda pūṇkeyuṁ
piridavanugra pāśupata bāṇadinallade sāyanantadaṁ
haranosedittumēnaduṟa muṣṭiyanīyane bēḍavēḻpudā
daradadanendu cakri śivanallige koṇḍogedaṁ kirīṭiyaṁ // ViVi.130 [campakamāle]

antu manaḥpavanavēgadiṁ kailāsa śaiḷamaneydi kadanatriṇētranaṁ triṇētrana
mundiḻipuvudumabhavaṁ tanna pādapadmaṅgaḷgeṟagidatirathamathananumaṁ
madhumathananumanamr̥ta dr̥ṣṭiyiṁ nōḍi pāśupatada muṣṭiyaṁ bēḍalendu
bandudaṁ tanna divya jñānadindamaṟidu—

apagata kapaṭade naṭanada
nupadēśaṅgeydu parasi pōgene poḍema
ṭṭu pasādameṁdaharigana
nupēndranā darbhaśayana taḷakiḻipuvuduṁ // ViVi.131 [kandaṁ]

antudāramahēśvaranīśvara varaprasādanamellaṁ tanage nenasāgeyuṁ
kanasinandamāgi tōṟe maṅgaḷa pāṭhaka ravaṅgaḷoḷ bhōṅkaneḻcattanannegaṁ—

tanna sutanaḻaloḷarjuna
nennudayamaneyde pārdu pagevara bēroḷ
bennīraneṟeyadiranada
nānnōḍuvenemba teṟadininanudayisidaṁ // ViVi.132 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷubhaya sainyāmburāśigaḷamburāśigaḷ neleyiṁ taḷarvante taḷare
kaḷaśa sambhavanandinanuvaradoḷ tannaṁ paricchēdisi kanaka kaḷaśa sambhr̥ta maṅgaḷa
jaḷaṅgaḷaṁ mindu dhavaḷa vasana dukūlāmbara maṅgaḷa vibhūṣaṇanuṁ nirvartita
sandhyōpāsananuṁ parisamāpta japanumarcita śitikaṇṭhanumāhuti
hutāgnihōtranuṁ pūjita dharāmaranuṁnīrājita rathaturaganumāgi rajata
rathamanēṟi saṅgrāma bhūmiyaneydevandu sāmantacūḍāmaṇiyaninisu
mārkoṇḍu nilvoḍaṁ sindhurājanaṁ kāvoḍamanēka vyūha racaneyoḷallade
[p. 309]
gelal bāradendu cakravyūhamanidiroḷoḍḍi sakaḷa sāmanta cakramaniralvēḻdallige
nālkuṁ yōjanada padumavyūhadoḷaṅgarāja śalya vr̥ṣasēna kr̥pa
kr̥tavarmāśvatthāmaraṁ duryōdhanaṁ berasirisi mattitta nālku yōjanada śakaṭa
vyūhada bāgiloḷ bāhlīka sōmadatta vindānuvindaroḍane saṁsaptakaranirisi
śakaṭa vyūhada peṟage nālku yōjanadoḷardhacandra vyūhadoḷadhika balarappa
saubala duśyāsanādi pradhāna vīrabhaṭa kōṭiya naḍuve sindhurājananirisi modala
cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ śarāsanācāryaṁ nindanitta pāṇḍava balamellamuṁ
vikramārjunanuṁ vajrapañjaradantabhēdyamappa vajravyūhamanoḍḍi dharmarāja
noḍane bhīma nakuḷa sahadēva sātyaki dhr̥ṣṭadyumna ghaṭōtkaca pramukha nāyakaraṁ
pēḻdu drupada virāṭa śikhaṇḍi yudhāmanyūttamaujaḥ kaikaya pradhāna nāyakaraṁ
tannoḍane kūḍikoṇḍu nijāgrajanaṁ bīḻkoṇḍu nija rathamaṁ rathāṅgadharanaṁ
munnamēṟalvēḻdu mūṟu sūḻbalavandu poḍemaṭṭu rathamanēṟi
vajrakavacamaṁ toṭṭu tavadoṇegaḷanamare bigidu gāṇḍīvamanēṟisi nīvi
jēvoḍedāgaḷ—

bhavaṁ bhavanagōtradindajanajāṇḍadiṁ bhānu bhā
nu vīdhiyiniḷātaḷaṁ taḷadineyde kiḻteḻdu tū
ḷvavārya bhuja vīryamaṁ neṟeye tōrpinaṁ kumbha saṁ
bhavaṁ maraletāgidaṁ ripukuraṅgakaṇṭhīravaṁ // ViVi.133 [pr̥thvi]

antu tāgi cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ tannaṁ pugalīyadaḍḍamāgininda
kārmukācāryananuṟe seṟegeyyade vinayāstramaneccu vinayamane mundiṭṭu
balavandu poḍamaṭṭu pōgevōge—

kamanīyaṁ balavandu pōpananelē pōpōgadir pōgadir
samarakkennoḍanañji pōdeyenalinteṁdaṁnaraṁ drōṇaraṁ
nimagānañjuvudenna bālatanadindandādudindādudē
nimagānañjadoḍañjisal neṟevenē trailōkyamaṁ yuddhadoḷ // ViVi.134 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu vinayamane nuḍida vikramārjunanaṁ guruvanēkāśīrva
vacanaṅgaḷiṁ parasuvuduṁ padumanābhana cōdisuva ratha vēgadiṁ padma
vyūhamaneydevandu suyōdhanana sādhanadoḷ tāgidāgaḷ—


[p. 310]
posamaseyambu kāra maḻevōl kaṟeyuttire nērdu sīḷdu khaṁ
ḍisi kaḍidoṭṭi suṭṭanitumaṁ nija mārgaṇa kōṭiyindagu
rvise tegedeccu tanna moneyambugaḷiṁ caturaṅgameyde kī
lise paḍe citradonde paḍeyantevolāytakaḷaṅka rāmaniṁ // ViVi.135 [campakamāle]

aḍi toḍe porkuḻuṁ tegale kai kaṇakāl koralembivuṁ beral
naḍuvura ben basiṟ toḷaku karcaremuyvu musumbu mūgu pe
rdoḍe kaṭi muṁmaḍaṁ paraḍu sandi nosal paṇe kaṇ kadampiveṁ
beḍeyane naṭṭuvurcidavu nērduvu sīḷduvu pārthanambugaḷ // ViVi.136 [campakamāle]

antu māṟānta mārpaḍeyellamaṁ javanokkalikki tannoḷ pōgade
peṇeda bāhlīka sōmadatta bhūriśravaranāne meṭṭida kuḷumpeya nīrante dese
desege sūsuvannegameḻbaṭṭi kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa jayatsēnarembareytare
mūvarakṣōhiṇī patigaḷverasu nālsāsirvar makuṭa vardhanaraṁ kondu
śalyanuramaṁ biriyeccu kr̥paraṁ viratharmāḍi naḍuvagaliḻivinaṁ kādi baḻaldu
kuduregaḷaṁ nīroḷikkalendu dēvakhātavemba maḍuviṅge barpudumitta
duryōdhanaṁ drōṇarallige vandu—

aḻidudu cāturaṅga balamaḷkuṟadānta mahāratharkaḷuṁ
kaḻakuḻamādudoḍḍaṇamaṇaṁ taledōṟale gaṇḍarilla to
ttaḻaduḻidappaninninisu bēgade saindhavanaṁ negaḻteyaṁ
gaḻiyisikoḷvoḍinninisu nindiṟiyiṁ taṟisandu pārthanoḷ // ViVi.137 [campakamāle]

embuduṁ drōṇācāryaṁ muguḷnage nakku vikramārjunananiḷisi nuḍiva
ninneṇagōṇaṅgaḷumekkasakkatanaṅgaḷumettamōduvu—

ninagarasāḷtanaṁ nuḍiva bīrara bīradaḷurke vikramā
rjunanoḷadēke salladenagātanasādhyanavadhyanānumī
moreyoḷe nindu kādidapenannegamenna varūtha sūta kē
tana kavacaṅgaḷiṁ neṟedu taḷtiṟi nīṁ jagadēkamallanoḷ // ViVi.138 [campakamāle]

embuduṁ suyōdhananēnādoḍēnādudenna pageya nānē
kolvenendabhēdya kavacamaṁ toṭṭu divyaśarāsana śaraṅgaḷaṁ koṇḍukaḷaśakētana
varūthanāgi pōgi—


[p. 311]
taḍeyade rājarājanidiraṁ bare bhōrgaredeccoḍambugaḷ
naḍade siḍilvuduṁ karataḷvadvayamaṁ biriyeccu keyduvaṁ
piḍivadaṭellamaṁ kiḍisi tāṁ kolalollanebhīmanātanaṁ
maḍipuvenenda pūṇke pusiyādapudendamarēndranandanaṁ // ViVi.139 [campakamāle]

annegamitta dharmaputranamōghāstra dhanañjayanaṁ keykoḷalaṭṭi
doḍe kaurava baḷa jaḷanidhiya naḍuvanuttarisibarpa sātyakiyaṁbhūriśrava
neḍegoṇḍāntu—

pōgadirendu mūdalise sātyaki tīvra śarāḷiyindagu
rvāge varūthamaṁ kaḍidoḍurcida bāḷvarasātaneydevaṁ
dāgaḷidirce tānumasiyaṁ seragillade kiḻtu pāydu bhū
bhāga nabhōvibhāgavaramaḷkuṟe taḷtiṟidar‌ virōdhigaḷ // ViVi.140 [utpalamālike]

antirvarumōrorvaroḷ bīramumaṁ biṅkamumaṁ meṟedu
dāsavaṇadaṇḍeyaṁ tōradiṇḍeyāḍidante dese desege kedaṟida kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷuṁ
nāraṅga sakaḷavaṭṭeyapaḻayigegaḷante nabhakke miḷirdu miḷḷisi pāṟuva nettara
suṭṭuregaḷumatibhayaṅkarākāramāge kādi basavaḻida sātyakiyaṁ bhūriśravana
śramadoḷ nelakikki gaṇṭalaṁ meṭṭi taleyanarivāgaḷ sātyaki bhūmi yuddha
pravīṇanappudaṟindātana bāḷa bāyoḷ cakrākr̥tiyoḷ taleyaṁ tiruputtu
mirdāgaḷadaṁmurāntakaṁ kaṇḍu vidviṣṭa vidrāvaṇaṅge tōṟidoḍe—

naraneccoḍe paṟidu karaṁ
karavāḷoḍanamare kāsi beccante vasuṁ
dhareyoḷ biḻdirdudadēṁ
tiravō pūṇisida muṣṭi bhūriśravanā // ViVi.141 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ sātyaki muḷisinol kaṇgāṇade bhūriśravana taleyanaridu
tannēṟiṅge tāne siggāgi pōdanannegaṁ yamanandanana besadoḷ phalguṇanaṁ
keykoḷal barpa marunnandanaṅgā drōṇaraḍḍaṁ bandoḍe guruge
gurudakṣiṇeguḍuvantavara rathamaṁ śata cūrṇaṁ māḍi kaḷiṅgarāja gaja ghaṭegaḷa
nauṅki sorkuttuṁ bare duśyāsanādigaḷadiradidiraṁ bandāntoḍe—


[p. 312]
niḍuvage saipininde dorekoṇḍudivar gajegoṇḍenappoḍī
gaḍe paredappareccu tave kolvenivandiranendu naccina
ccuḍivinameccoḍecceḍeyineccaruṇāmbu kalaṅki pāye mu
nnaḍiyoḷuraḷdarandhanr̥panandanarandu maruttanūjanā // ViVi.142 [campakamāle]

antu durmukha durmada durdharṣaṇa‌r modalāge mūvattu
mūvaraṁ kondu duśyāsananaṁ virathanaṁ māḍi duryōdhanananonde niśita
viśikha hatiyiṁ suruḷduruḷvinameccu mūrchāgatanaṁ māḍi siṁhanādadinārdu
muṭṭevarpāgaḷāḷdana sāvaṁ nōḍalāṟade—

eḍegoṇḍaṅkada karṇaneydevare divyāstraṅgaḷindaṁ siḍil
poḍevantappinameccudagra rathamaṁ muyyēḻu sūḻ kōpadiṁ
kaḍiyal sārdoḍaḻaldu sūtasutanondugrēṣuviṁ tiṇṇame
ccoḍanārdaṁ nasu mūrchevōgi rathadoḷ bhīma naralvannegaṁ // ViVi.143 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu mūrchāgatanāda bhīmana koraloḷ billaṁ kōdu mēgillade
tegedu—

tāṁ gaḍamennāḷdana toḍe
yaṁ gaḍaminnuḍivanennoḷaṁ kāduvaneṁ
daṅgapati nuḍidu kollade
tāṅgidanambikege nuḍida nuḍi nile manadoḷ // ViVi.144 [kandaṁ]

annegamitta cāṇūrāri jarāsandhāriya munnegedu baḻikkaḍaṅgida
siṁhanādakke manaḥkṣatambaṭṭu sātyakiyanārayalaṭṭidoḍātaṁ bandacētananāgi
biḻdirda vr̥kōdaranaṁ tanna rathamanēṟisikoṇḍu kūḍe vandanannegaṁ
duryōdhanaṁ karṇamberasu saindhavana moneyoḷātanaṁ peṟagikki munde
nindāgaḷ—

dinakaranasta mastakamanāsevaḍal bagedappanēke ke
mmane taḍevai jayadrathananikkuḻidāroḷamiṁ toḍaṅkavē
ḍenutumajaṁ marujjavade cōdise pārthana dēvadatta ni
svanadoḷe tīvi poṭṭanoḍavantevolādudajāṇḍa maṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.145 [campakamāle]

caṭuḷita cakranēmi parivartana ghaṭṭana ghāta nirbhara
sphuṭita dharātaḷaṁ vijayanugra rathaṁ paridattu dal ghaṭā

[p. 313]
ghaṭita haṭadvirōdhi rudhiraplava lampaṭa saṅkaṭōtkaṭaṁ
kaṭakaṭaghāta nāka taṭasaṅkaṭa saṅgara raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.146 [campakamāle]

āgaḷ kurudhvajinige bhayajvaramuṁ mahēśvarajvaramuṁ bare barpudāra
mahēśvarana rathada baravaṁ kaṇḍu karṇa śalya śakuni śāradvata kr̥tavarma
duryōdhana duśyāsanar modalādatiratha samaratha mahārathārdharatharoṁ
devindeyalladondorvaroḷ sandhisi gondaṇisi nindāgaḷ—

śaradoḷagurci pōpa poḷapiṅgoḷagāgi taguḷdudondu be
ḷsarigeṇeyādudīyeṟaguvambina balsariyembinaṁniraṁ
taradoḷe pāyda kūrgaṇegaḷaṁ taṟidoṭṭi teraḷci toḷdikoṁ
ḍaredu maguḻci saṇṇisidanānta caturvalamaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.147 [campakamāle]

kaligaṁ ballāḷgamambettideniduve padaṁ mārkoḷal sindhurājaṁ
gelalendāṁ bandeniṁ kondapane neredu nindānimendāntaraṁ mū
dalisutteccaṁ pracaṇḍa praḷaya ghana ghaṭāravadindārdu bāṇā
valiyindaṁ pūḻe rōdō vivaramanodavittondu ghōrāndhakāraṁ // ViVi.148 [mahāsragdhare]

antamōghāstra dhanañjayanecca śara saṅghātadinogeda raṇagaḻtaleye
molagaḻtaleyaṁ māḍe nēsaṟ paṭṭattu vijayaṁ sōltanendu kaurava
balamārdoḍe—

jvaḷadanaḷāstradindamise kaḻtale tūḷdu teraḷdudāgaḷu
mmaḷisi mahārathar peḷaṟe saindhavanennaḷaviṅgamenna dō
rvaḷadaḷaviṅgamiṁ seḍediral doreyaltenagendu bandasuṁ
goḷe poṇardaṁ surar‌ pogaḻe tannaḷavaṁ jagadēkamallanoḷ // ViVi.149 [campakamāle]

antatiratha mathanana rathakkadiradidiraṁ tanna rathamaṁ pariyisi jayadrathaṁ
muṭṭevandu—

ninne poraḷci ninna maganaṁ seragillade kondenindumiṁ
tinnegamirpudaṁ bhayadinirdene ninnane pārutirdeneṁ
dunnata śauryadindajitanaṁ naranaṁ munideccanēḻumeṁ
ṭunniśitāstradindadaṭadēṁ dorevettudo sindhurājanā // ViVi.150 [utpalamālike]


[p. 314]
anteccu kiccuṁ kiḍiyumāgi percidummaccaradindaccariyāgekāde—

entasmatputranaṁ saṅgaradoḷaḻideyinnante nil‌ śakti cātu
rdantaṅgaḷ ninnanāṁ kolveḍeyoḷelavo pēḻ kāvuvē kāyavaṇmeṁ
dantāntecceccu sūta dhvaja haya ratha saṅghātamaṁ nurge lōka
kkantaṁ māḻpantakambōl gadeviḍiduṟadeytarpanaṁ kaṇḍanantaṁ // ViVi.151 [sragdhare]

tuḍu pāśupatamanene nara
neḍemaḍagade tuḍe diśāḷi naḍugidudu suru
ḷduḍugidudu viyattaḷameḷe |
piḍugidudu kalaṅki kadaḍidudu śivana manaṁ // ViVi.152 [kandaṁ]

suḻiyoḷagirdu beṭṭu poṟapoṇmuvinaṁ lavaṇāmburāśi ku
kkuḻagudivalli kūḻgudiye mēge siḍildaguḷante kūḍe ta
ttaḻagudiyuttumirpa kudiyoḷ siḍidalliya muttugaḷ chaḻil
chaḻilene koṇḍuvormodale rudra surēndra vimānapaṅtkiyaṁ // ViVi.153 [campakamāle]

antu samudra kṣōbhamuṁ trailōkya kṣōbhamumoḍanoḍanāge—

tegeneṟedūṟikoṇḍise śiraṁ paridatta viyattaḷambaraṁ
negedoḍe rāhu bāydeṟedu nuṅgale bandapudemba śaṅkeyiṁ
dagidu dinēśanasta giriyaṁ maṟegoṇḍanamōghamemba mā
tugaḷa negaḻteyaṁ paḍedanāhavadoḷ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.154 [campakamāle]

biridalarōḷi saggada madāḷigaḷaṁ geḍegoṇḍu dēva suṁ
dariyara keygaḷindamuge tumburu nāradarondu gēyadiṁ
caramerdeyaṁ paḷañcaleye vīralatāṅgiyasōṅku meyyoḷaṁ
kurise nirākuḷaṁ kaḷedanāji pariśramamaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.155 [campakamāle]

varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa
